*Oṃ awiǥnamāstu*

<sragđarā>:1.
– – –| – ⏑ –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

siṅgiḥ đyakṣêŋ kalaṅwan saŋ aṅawaki laṅö mūṙtti saŋ hyaŋ manoƀū,
pūjān riŋ puṣpa muṅgwiŋ sarasija gĕlarĕn muṣṭi niŋ kāmatantra,
maṅke caṇḍyā nirêŋ  ƀāṣa saꝑalakĕna yan dèwa niŋ kūŋ winimba,
Āpan riŋ niṣkalânaṅga kawuwusan ira n saŋ maṅö wri ŋ palambaŋ*

hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ kāṙttikâṅambĕki kawi kakawin riŋ pasiṙ paṙwwatârūm,
līlâdandan ǥanâpiṇḍa karas ira lĕṅö lwiṙ nika syuḥ kilatnya,
tansaḥ taŋ ciṇḍaga mrik tanaḥ ira n alaṅö maṙṇnana ŋ laṅwa-laṅwan,
gĕntĕṙ lagy-âṅatag ƀāwa nira n aṅikĕti ŋ twas niŋ onĕŋ tinambaŋ*

maṅgalyā ni ṅhulun đꜽṙyya sahaja makĕdö mrākrĕtā ŋ ƀomakāwya,
de niŋ siṅgiḥ mataŋnya n panulada kakawin ndān adoḥ yan paniṙwwa,
himpĕṙ wintaŋ lawan sūṙyya kĕta gati niki n taṇḍiṅĕn kāwidagđan,
Āpan taṇḍiŋ laṅö dūra n amalika karas yan kadohan tanaḥnya*

hyaŋ wiṣṇw-aṅjanma riŋ mađyapada makadadin śrī mahārāja krĕṣṇa,
mwaŋ saŋ hyaŋ bāsukī maṅkana dadi baladewâgraja śrī narendra,
kapwâgöŋ riŋ kaśaktin praƀawa nira dudug trus tĕkêŋ swaṙggaloka,
sākṣād āditya kĕmbaṙ sira taya dumĕlö de ni göŋ niŋ pratāpa*

sakweḥ niŋ śatru kāṅśādi saha bala hilaŋ de nirâlaḥ wiśīṙṇna,
swasŧa ŋ rāt ṅkā n suƀikṣâhayu sahana nikāŋ āśramâtiṅkaḥ akram,
sājñā saŋ mānu hetunya n apagĕḥ irikaŋ śāsanêŋ mānawādi,
māry-ambĕk crol ikaŋ duṣṭa sumiliḥ aharĕp muṅsirêŋ đaṙmmayukti*

maṅgĕḥ göŋ niŋ kaśaktin ri haji sama-sama mwaŋ mahāmeru riŋ twas,
kadyâḍaṅhan marêkaŋ triƀuwana winawêŋ hasta de śrī narendra,
towin sampūṙṇna śaktî sira matika dumeḥ wīṙyya lumrâniwāṙyya,
Āpan taŋ wīṙyya riŋ nīti sira kadi catussāgarâlaṅǥanīya*

ramyâtyantâhalĕp rājya nira ṅaran ikêŋ dwārawaty-âtiśoƀa,
Antuk niŋ hyaŋ paḍa bwat puji wijaḥ aturun kabwatan tan hanâsor,
bapranyâmâs lawan gopura maṇik inukiṙ prāṇa pūṙwwâpurâgo,
hetunya n swaṙgga riŋ meru linĕwiḥ ahajöŋ tan katon ṅke ri loka*

denya kweḥ niŋ karaŋ ratna saꝑala pakirim hyaŋ samudrê narendra,
prastāwanya n maṇik rāmya racana niŋ umaḥ mās parĕmpw-î hatĕpnya,
sambanđanya praśastêŋ ƀuwana halĕp ikaŋ rājya yâtyanta riŋ śrī,
Āpan saŋ hyaŋ đanendrâṅhudani ya rajaṭâṅkĕn pituŋ lek hudan mās*

riŋ kastrī-hajyan akweḥ grĕha kanaka kinoṙyyan maṇik padmarāga,
söŋ-söŋ nīŋ oṣađi byakta lumarap ahulap ƀāswarâṅĕṇḍĕp-ĕṇḍĕp,
towîki n teja niŋ ratna patiga sumĕnö nitya kīṙṇnê nataṙnya,
hetunya n tan pĕtĕŋ riŋ wĕṅi sumaji jugā pañjut iŋ kāla sore*

lāwan tāmanya makweḥ tuwu-tuwuhan ikâpādapâkambaŋ awwaḥ,
wwaḥ riŋ māsânurun rūm lĕṅĕŋ amisan apan tan hanâganti-ganti,
nityâṅjraḥ paṅkajanyêŋ  talaga pinatigêŋ candrakānta pradīpta,
wyaṙŧêkaŋ paṙwwata mwaŋ pasiṙ i hana nika n wāḥ laṅö rob kalaṅwan*

ṅkâṙṇnaḥ leṙ taŋ paṅastryānan alun-alun i heŋ bajralepanya ratna,
salwânīlâwaṅuntuṙ pinakasaƀa-saƀā saŋ watĕk yadw-asewa,ꦉ
kaywanyâneka tejanya ri kĕñaṙ i sĕnö niŋ maṇik ƀūṣaṇâƀra,
lagy-aṅde saṅśaya n wwantĕna rawi manusup nāgatêŋ rāhuwimba*

hīṅanya n sāri niŋ rājya tiki hana rikaŋ dwārawaty-adwitīya,
laṅgĕŋ kapwêki rāmyanya tuwi paḍa mahāmūlya kālanya makweḥ,
mambö ganđanya lumrâŋ asĕp asawaŋ aket mrik hrĕbuk tūt hawan göŋ,
daṙppêkāŋ atpadânatpada maṅusiṙ inak hetukanya n pĕnuḥ wwaŋ*

maṅkā krĕp niŋ grĕhâkaṇṭa sakuwu-sakuwū seriŋ iŋ rājyađāni,
denyâtiṅkaḥ mahantĕn ri lĕbuḥ ika lawan pañcuran wāṇḍirâgöŋ,
len tekaŋ bwat salö mwaŋ patani ri tĕpi niŋ māṙgga ramyâpapuṇyan,
muṅgwiŋ doḥ paṅhyaṅan śela tuwi katulajĕg caṇḍi kapwâpucak mās*

lwaḥ saṅkeŋ jro kaḍatwan hĕniŋ i bañu nikâdrĕs hilīnyâṅgaluntaŋ,
tañjuŋ wūṅw-âsanâśoka suraƀi kamuniŋ muṅgwi piṅgiṙ nikaŋ lwaḥ,
siṅgroŋ-siṅgroŋ ikā rantunan iŋ iwak ariŋ lālanâliṇḍuṅan wwad,
kĕmbaŋ laywan kahily-aṅduluṙ anak-anakan keṭakâṅumbaŋ-umbaŋ*

ndātan dwa n tan bĕsuṙ taŋ wwaŋ umulat irikā nyāsa makweḥ tinonton,
lyan tekaŋ lakwa-lakwan para ratu n umarĕk mwaŋ watĕk yođamantrī,
saṅkĕp saŋ wrĕṣṇi-wīṙ-ânđaka saha panĕṅĕṙ cūḍaratna pradīpta,
pantĕs-pantĕs rare saŋ yadukula winanîŋ praŋ sĕḍĕŋ daṙśśanīya*

sāmpun prāptâtatā riŋ wataṅan alun-alun mantri saŋ nāŧa krĕṣṇa,
sahyâgasyak magoṣṫy-âwĕtu guyu hana tâƀāwakâmiṇḍa-miṇḍa,
māry-âśabdârarĕm ḍyam ri wijil ira mahārāja saṅkeŋ kaḍatwan,
kewalyâkāra saŋ śrī nrĕpati winulatan tan wawaŋ yan panāntwa*

nantĕn tapwan masowe haji maṅuliḥ-uliḥ jag ḍatĕŋ saŋ mahāṙṣi,
saṅkeŋ swaṙggâduluṙ somya sira sama-samêŋ sidđi sīra n paḍa hyaŋ,
kagyat-gyat saŋ narendrâmulati muniwarâpan sawaŋ riŋ paṅipyan,
gorawy-atyanta saŋ ƀūpati karaṇa nira n tan paṅantî palaṅka*

nyā pwâŋ aṙgǥâtiśoƀânupama suci matis muṅgu riŋ kumƀa ratna,
yekā sāmpun panuṅsuŋ narapati ri mahāpaṇḍya tuṣṭa prahaṙṣa,
lāwan tekaŋ palaṅkâśayana ya humaḍaŋ saṅgrahê saŋ tapaswī,
rĕp-rĕp-rĕp-rĕp maluṅguḥ muniwara ri tĕlas Iŋ maśāntî narendra*

mojaṙ saŋ nāŧa ḍū ƀāgya tĕka muniwara prāpta riŋ deśa śūnya,
hopĕn tekaŋ purī yan gatarasa pinaran tan hanênuṅsiṙ-uṅsir,
maṅke n kambaḥ tĕkap saŋ prawara hana gamantanya maṅgiḥ pawitra,
Āpan saŋ paṇḍitâṅde hayu humilaṅakĕn kleśa niŋ janmaƀūmi*

Astam rānak mahāpaṇḍya kadi wihikan iŋ swaṙgga yan ton mahāṙṣi,
siṅgiḥ yan ƀāgyamanta ṅhulun apa ta kunaŋ kāṙyya riŋ pūṙwwajanma,
nityāśaṅkw-âmaṅun đaṙmma karika maṅipuk yajñā ṅūny-ânanĕm soŋ,
ndaḥ yeki n rakwa maṅke ꝑala nika ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ paṅĕmpwan para ṅke*

Om om om sājña saŋ śrī nrĕpati kudaŋ ike saṅhulun sidđayogī, 
maṅke n sāmpun katon byakta ri dadi ƀagawān weṣṇawa śrī narendra,
sakweḥ saŋ sidđayogīśwara kita śaraṇanyêki muṅgwiŋ swacitta,
Aṅhiŋ siḥta n sināđyâṅlĕpasakĕna sarāt riŋ padânindyajāti*

ḍū tan maṅkā pwa de saŋ yatiwara maṅucap ri ṅhulun hīnabudđi,
nantĕn denya ŋ warānugraha maṅudaŋ-ṅudaŋ saŋ mahaṙṣîŋ kadi ṅwaŋ,
ndañ jātinya n puriḥ saŋ sujana juga mahâṅastawâṅde prahaṙṣa,
lwiṙ prāptêŋ brahmaloka ṅwaŋ ahawana wuwus de mahāpaṇḍya mojar*

ndaḥ kṣāntabya ṅhulun toḥ sahuri taña ranak saŋ mahaṙṣî yatīndra,
ndy-ânuŋ saṅkan paran ndon saṅapa sira ṅaran saŋ yati ṅwaŋ turuŋ wruḥ,
nā liŋ saŋ nāŧa krĕṣṇâtaña wawaŋ awaraḥ don irê saŋ narendra,
siṅgiḥ-siṅgiḥ wuwustê kami laki majarê tiṅka-tiṅkaḥ mahāṙṣi*

ṅūni pwa ꝁyāti saŋ hyaŋ narahari makasāđyā kahaywān ikaŋ rāt,
pūjāƀyāsêŋ wiđi bwat krama sira satatâmrĕdđyakĕn śiṣyasaṅǥa,
nāhan saŋ paṇḍya śiṣyâtuha tinuhakĕn iŋ kahyaṅan de ƀaṭāra,
śudđasŧānâđika ndaḥ panĕmu nira mahāđyātmikâreḥ pralīna*

ndā ndā siṅgiḥ pwa yâtyanta halĕp ira huwus pūṙṇna riŋ jñānasanđi,
saṙwwajña mwaŋ tikāŋ aṣṭaguṇa paḍa hanê saŋ rĕsi byaktasidđa,
tĕkwan tekaŋ kamāhātmyan ira sama lawan hyaŋ prajāpaty-anindya,
niṙwiǥnâstu swaƀāwa ṅhaṅĕn-aṅĕn i sira n sāmpun iŋ waktraśoca*

nā liŋ saŋ paṇḍya tan len ṅaran ira ƀagawān aṅgirâtyantawāgmī,
saŋ sākṣāt hyaŋ wiđīśabda sakala ṅuniweḥ śāraṇêŋ ādikāwya,
riŋ kꜽśwaryan tanorâmaḍana sira yan iŋ saṙwwayogaprayoga,
śrīy ātmā śudđabudđi pratuhu-tuhu kawīndrâdi sidđāntaśāstra*

sāmpun teki n waraḥ ni ṅhulun i haji kunaŋ don mahaṙṣî narendra,
paṅrakṣantêŋ trilokôdasina nira ri saŋ nāŧa maṅke n para ṅke,
Atyantêŋ ƀūṙ ƀuwaḥ swaḥ kinawaśakĕn ikaŋ rākṣasâkweḥ prakīṙṇna,
wadwānyêŋ dānawânāma naraka pĕnuḥ iŋ dik-widik tan pahīṅan*

śīṙṇna ŋ swaṙggâlilaŋ taŋ patapan apan ikaŋ rākṣasâṅrampa-rampak,
luṅhā saŋ tāpasâtiṅgal alaradan adoḥ sāri-sāri n tinumpu,
len taŋ wāhwâṅlawan kapwa mati ginarabag kāsihan ya ŋ daridra,
waṅkaynyâṅlaḥ-laḥ iŋ maṇḍala saha daluwaŋ kaṇḍi-kaṇḍinya kontal*

tīḍak ḍīkötahui
<wikrĕti>:2.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

kunaŋ pwa haji tatwa saŋ naraka rĕṅwakĕna tiki tĕkap nareśwara,
ƀaṭāra hari padmayoni sira tâṅucap-ucap ulaḥ iŋ kadigjayan,
tanora liŋ irâmaḍāna ri kaśaktin ira pisaniṅū hana ŋ lĕwiḥ,
ya hetu nira māna kāṙyya nira liŋ nira sahana nikaŋ jagattraya*

sĕḍĕŋ nira magoṣṫi jag hana ta liṅga maṇik aṅadĕg iŋ pahīṅanan,
dawānya manĕhĕṙ katon dadi sirâṅliŋ apa tiki katon asamƀawa,
manaḥ nira wawaŋ tĕkânatapa liṅga wahu mayat ikaŋ taṅan kiwa,
Umiṇḍuhuṙ ikaŋ maṇik-sꝑaṭika-liṅga sadĕdĕg irikā n tiniṅhalan*

kapūhan aṅĕṭĕk ƀaṭāra maṅadĕg paḍa maṅayuhi puñcak iŋ maṇik,
samaṅkana tikaŋ maṇik makin umiṇḍuhuṙ amatĕṅaḥ iŋ naƀastala,
ya tâmaṅunakĕn gĕlĕŋ ri sira saŋ rwa mamariƀawa maṅdĕhâṅdĕdĕl,
paḍâṅgrĕgut añakra tan hana jugâmyati warayaŋ irâwaluy-waluy*

kaṅelan asuwe ƀaṭāra hari keśawa muwaḥ irikâṅdadak ƀawa,
nĕhĕṙ matĕmahan warāha sawukiṙ himawan iki sirânwab iŋ lĕmaḥ,
prayojana katĕmwa buṅkaḥ ikanaŋ maṇik ulaḥ-ulahĕn maran rĕbaḥ,
lĕpas tĕka ri soṙ kaḍāha sira tan palaca-laca wĕkas nikaŋ maṇik*

prajāpati sirâtemaḥ manuk uluŋ wĕkas anatap pucak nikaŋ maṇik,
huwus tĕka sirê kaḍāhaka nikê ruhuṙ ika binĕlaḥ nirêŋ hĕlar,
lĕpas pwa sira tan katon wĕkas ikaŋ maṇik aruhuṙ adoḥ samaṙ lĕyĕp,
tuhun bañu niŋ aṙṇnawânĕḍuni ƀūṙ ƀuwaḥ inusiṙ apan catuṙmmuꝁa*

kĕbĕk pwa kalĕbū taŋ aṇḍaƀuwanâṙṇnawa kadi muwahêka tuṅgala,
muwaḥ sahana saŋ hyaŋ aṅhyaṅi ƀaṭāra hari mari marūpa sūkara,
samantara ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu humĕnĕŋ pinĕkul ira juga ŋ jagattraya,
huwus pwa masamāđi pūṙṇna tikaŋ aṇḍaƀuwana kadi ṅūni tambayan*

manon ta sira dewatī hyaŋ ikanaŋ lĕmaḥ atiśaya riŋ guṇâhayu,
sahaṙṣa sira tan dwa sāhasa mamaṅkwakĕn anuculi sanđi niŋ tapiḥ,
kunaŋ pwa sira saŋ kinol nira ya tâkrak anaṅis anulak sirâkĕtĕr,
miṅe kawawa mūṙcꞓa melik i ƀaṭāra mituturi sira n warāhika*

Ilik nira wasunđarī mwaŋ iki rāga nira sira ƀaṭāra keśawa,
tinūt i paṅiḍam nirêŋ kṣitisuta ŋ rasatala pinakaṅgwan iŋ rare,
lawas nira wasunđarâmĕtĕṅakĕn tĕka tahun ika sewu tan kuraŋ,
mijil pwa tanayan ƀaṭāra mađusūđana yatika marūpa dānawa*

prajāpati sirâwĕlas maṅanumoda sira tĕhĕṙ aweḥ anugraha,
sirâṅarani riŋ rare si narakâstujaya wijaya liŋ nirâṅgamĕl,
rinatwakĕn irêka saŋ kṣitisuta pwa makahulun ikaŋ jagattraya,
ri göŋ i siḥ irêkihĕn kamalayoni karaṇa ni mahīsutâñjaya*

tĕlasnya n inanugrahan ciha-cihâpraṅa juga kaharĕpnya tan waneḥ,
mijil ta ya marêŋ samudra saha sañjata dinuluṙ ikaŋ balāsura,
manuṅgaŋ iŋ iwak liman wija-wijaḥ saha bala nika rāmya tūt hawan,
hanan jĕnĕk aliṅgiḥ iŋ karaŋ aṅuṅkuli halun i surud nikaŋ bañu*

ry-uliḥnya saka riŋ samudra tadanantara maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn ta yâpraṅa,
đaneśwara sirêka liŋnya ya tĕkāna nagara nira rakwa rampasĕn,
Umaṅkat ahawan haṅin saha balanya kumukus aduluṙ mahānala,
tĕkâṅgĕsĕṅi rājya muntab i gĕlĕŋnya tinahĕn ika maṅkin ujwala*

katiṅgal ikanaŋ wimāna maṇipuṣpaka tĕkap ira saŋ đaneśwara,
ya tênalap ikaŋ mahīsuta manuṅgaŋ atĕhĕṙ umuliḥ sakeŋ raṇa,
Ikāŋ asurasaṅǥa yâṅadĕgakĕn kuṭa ni naraka muṅgu riŋ du lor,
Amumpunana paścimottara sadeśa baruṇa kalawan đanāđipa*

tĕlasnya magawe kuṭâdƀuta samaṅkana marawaśa riŋ tapowana,
nihan tiki nimitta saŋ rĕṣi samânasi pamahayu saŋ nareśwara,
narendra juga yântakā niŋ asurāđipa pawĕkas ira hyaŋ ôśwara,
mataŋnya n aṅusiṙ wĕlas ṅhulun i saŋ praƀu tumaḍaha ŋ āśrayê haji*

nahan wuwus i saŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada mawara-waraḥ ri saŋ praƀu,
watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ sumöŋ ri muꝁa duhꝁa nira lumuḥ aṅĕmbĕŋ iŋ mata,
narendra wĕkasan tumuntĕn atiyatna maṅanumata don mahāyati,
mĕhaḥ sira mĕṅĕs wawaŋ wĕtu ni luḥ nira mamarĕṅi luḥ mahāmuni*

maśabda naranāŧa sis kadi linād hati ni ranak ira mpu maṅrĕṅö,
nihan ṅhulun atoha jīwita rumakṣa sahana-hana riŋ tapowana,
tuhun makasiluṅluṅa ŋ yaśa juga ṅhulun amahayu ƀūmimaṇḍala,
Anugraha mahāṙṣi ri ṅhulun acaṇḍya ri pagĕha nikaŋ jagadđita*

nda yêki sipi ƀāgya niŋ tapa suꝁa ṅhulun inuƀaya de nareśwara,
kunaŋ pwa mapa dāya saŋ praƀu mapêki hiṅĕt-iṅĕt i saŋ narāđipa,
kunĕŋ ri panukū mahīsuta marêŋ amarapura dumon sureśwara,
kĕnoḥ niki balanya hĕntyakĕna siŋ kawĕkas amariƀūta riŋ wiku*

syapêka hinutus narāđipa rumakṣa ri para rĕṣi riŋ himālaya,
kapagwakĕna tan hĕlĕm-hĕlĕmĕn āpan awĕdi sira riŋ balāsura,
kṣamākĕna marêki śabda niŋ aminta śaraṇa kadi tan paṅantyakĕn,
swaƀāwa nikaŋ āśrayâmicaraṇâśraya karĕs ika yâṅgrĕmĕt-grĕmĕt*

ya tôjaṙ ira saŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada wawaŋ asahuṙ nareśwara,
tatan sigi-sigin kunĕŋ wĕtu ni saṅhulun aṅutusa yogyarakṣakā,
hanêki pinakāgra niŋ swatanayêka gati niki tĕlas krĕtāyuđa,
lumakwa mara riŋ tapowana sumapwana ŋ asura sukĕt niŋ āśrama*

Anantara ḍatĕŋ ta sāmba humatuṙ dadi tinuduhakĕn ri saŋ rĕṣi,
sĕḍĕŋ wĕrĕ-wĕrĕḥ katon raras ira n lituhayu ya mawoṙ guṇâđika,
kapūhan aṅĕṭĕk mahāmuni mulat prasama tĕhĕṙ anaṙkka liŋ Ira,
nyamâŋ tapi-tapîŋ girī rumaras iŋ piṅulahana tumiṅhalê sira*

ri samparan iraŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ wihikana sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
tĕlas pinaripoṣitânarima nāna sira paḍa maśānti saŋ praƀu,
humantuk ahawan tawaŋ sira hanêŋ jalada jĕnĕk aṅöb samaṙ-samar,
hanan kadi wayaŋ katon kinĕliran puti-putiḥ adamaṙ traŋ iŋ rawi*

byatīta gati saŋ watĕk rĕṣi narendra sira tiki gumanti waṙṇnanĕn,
prayojana mahāṙṣi muṅgu ri manaḥ nira yatika hinöm nirâṅdadak,
saŋ udđawa sirâwuwus praƀu kĕnoḥ larisakĕna ŋ upāya de haji,
narendrasuta sāmba maṅkata lawan sakatuduha tumūta rakṣaka*

yadin tan alahâbwata ŋ musuḥ atambĕha hana juga mājarê haji,
watĕk yadu waneḥ muwaḥ tumuluṅê nrĕpasuta tumuluy riŋ āśrama,
kahinya n akĕḍik marêka bala niŋ naraka paḍa mareŋ kadewatan,
Alaḥnya niyatanya haywa kapalaŋ palĕkasa nira saŋ nrĕpātmaja*

kunaŋ hala nikiŋ hĕlĕm-hĕlĕma de narapati maṅupāya riŋ musuḥ,
hilaŋ yaśa narendra saŋ yati paḍâsasaran alaradan mareŋ waneḥ,
Ikaŋ musuḥ agöŋ ya donya tĕmahan milaṅakĕn i śarīra saŋ praƀu,
Apuy sumĕlap iŋ hatĕp ṅaran ikā hĕnĕṅakĕna gatinya de haji*

nihan paṅupamanya rakwa hana ta wwaŋ asawa-sawaḥ iŋ lĕmaḥ rĕnĕk,
saniścaya ta yêŋ parinya yan ahaywa maraṇa tuwi tan hanâṅapa,
hana pwa ri lĕmĕḥ nikâmatuna hetu ni dukut i sawaḥ nikâruhur,
Alit wĕtu nikaŋ pari n karahaban waliṅi ya hala niŋ palĕḥ-palĕḥ*

prakāśa mara kīṙtti saŋ praƀu tĕlas pinakasuluḥ ikaŋ prajāhita,
wulan-wulan iraŋ mahājana tanora lumĕwihana śoƀitâbuṅaḥ,
katon kalĕwihan rikânuꝁani saṅka ri wĕtu nikaŋ ambĕk uttama,
prihĕn tĕmĕn ikaŋ karakṣan ika de nrĕpati makaꝑalâŋ jagadđita*

rĕsĕp rasa ni śabda rakryan apatiḥ pinatiḥ ira narendra riŋ naya,
wĕtunya ŋ upapatti yukti ya ta muꝁya niŋ ayu niŋ upāya de haji,
manaḥ prawarawīra haṙṣa rumĕṅö wacana nira saŋ udđawêŋ saƀā,
hatuṙ salaga kāṅinan kapanasan sumĕkaṙ i tĕka niŋ hudan wĕṅi*

wawaŋ nrĕpati krĕṣṇa mantuk i dalĕm nagara ri parahasyan iŋ daṅū,
narendrasuta sāmba sāmpun aśilê harĕp ira pinapak wineḥ sĕpaḥ,
tĕñuḥ twas ira śīṙṇna rakwa dadi luḥ drawa ri mata nira n parambĕhan,
panampĕta nira n taṅis mara-maraḥ nrĕpasuta riy asiḥ nirâṅrĕsĕp*

tuhanku bapa tan sake lalis iki ṅhulun umutus i māsku riŋ ƀaya,
Asiḥku ri kitêki haywa ta kitânalaḥ-iḍĕp i sabudđya ni ṅhulun,
prasidđa hurip i ṅhulun kita mataŋnya kapan awĕnaṅâku niṣṫura,
kadigjayan ike katönku ri wĕkaṅkw-i saŋ anulus anĕmwa kapraƀun*

kita pwa hinarĕp-harĕpku śaraṇaṅkw-amagĕhakĕna đaṙmma ni ṅhulun,
t-akīṙtti t-aṅusiṙ guṇâđika tuhanku laki t-aṅipuk ambĕk iŋ jagat,
Ameta kajanapriyan ta kita wuṅsu hawana ni ḍatĕŋ nikaŋ hayu,
nihan ṅhulun acaṇḍya māsku saꝑalâṅusira pagĕha niŋ jagadđita*

lanâmala-malaṙ ṅhulun bapa manĕmwa ꝑala niŋ awĕkâdi śaktimān,
tan āri masamāđi riŋ rahina riŋ wĕṅi saha japa đīra subrata,
kitêki saŋ iniṣṭi niŋ twas i yayaḥta laki kĕkĕsakĕnta riŋ hati,
wĕlas larapan iŋ siḥ i ṅwaŋ awĕkâpunagi maharĕp iŋ tĕkêŋ paran*

pajātyan ira saŋ makānak ađimuꝁya pituhun iŋ anak maran suꝁa,
kaduhꝁan ira yan katona patita ŋ tanaya nira calānanêŋ sarāt,
kaduṙyyaśan ikaŋ maputra wiparīta kawĕdi nika yan pamīḍana,
halib halĕp irânaka pratitaƀakti magĕlĕm anĕnĕbw-amet guṇa*

hanêki pawaraḥ nirâdipuruṣâminĕkĕti riŋ ulaḥ mwaŋ iŋ gati,
yateka kinĕkĕsku riŋ twas abuṅaḥ makasuluḥ iŋ amet prayojana,
kapaṅgihan ikaŋ janottama wiśeṣa katĕwasa tĕkapnya tan hilaŋ,
maṇik-maṇik iŋ aṅgĕgö kira-kirâṅalahakĕna pataṇḍĕg iŋ musuḥ*

wĕka pwa saŋ aṅuṅsi haywa ni yayaḥ hyun ika ya ta kayuktyan iŋ wĕka,
gawe niŋ atuha pwa nitya gawayĕn ya makalarapana twaŋ iŋ bapa,
kadaŋ suꝁa tĕkapnya rakwa hiniḍĕpnya wariṅin i samīpa niŋ hĕnū,
dudū pamuji niŋ sarāt ri saguṇanya saꝑala pinalaṙ paṅöbana*

kalīṅa niŋ ujaṙ ku māsku saꝑala ṅwaŋ awĕka guṇawān sulakṣaṇa,
Ikaŋ ꝑala ri yajña sātus apitowi tan amaḍa kasoṙ ya de nikā,
putus niŋ atiƀāgyamanta sira saŋ pinituhu niŋ anak mapet hayu,
mataŋnya kamituhwa haywa ta manaḥta cala yaśani ta ṅhulun tuhan*

<jagadđita>:3.

nā liŋ saŋ naranāŧa mojaṙ i narendratanaya mamanis wuwus nira,
saŋ sāmbâdara tan sahuṙ tuhun anĕmbaḥ amuhun iki rakwa maṅkata,
maṅkin sök hati saŋ narendra mamĕlas ry-anak ira wahu-wahwa maṅkana,
de niŋ siḥ pinĕgat mataŋnya n umilī bañu ni mata nira n hawan pipi*

ṅkānê jro nagarêki saŋ nrĕpasutâmuhuna tumama kaṙwwa pawwahan,
dewī jāmbawatī wawaŋ sira kataṅgama ri tĕka nareśwarātmaja,
haṙṣânantwa paran ta kāṙyya ni wĕkaṅku mapa kita diṅaryan aṅlawad,
maṅke n prāpta kitê ṅhulun kadi hañaṙ dinadak apa tikaŋ prayojana*

siṅgiḥ liŋ ra bibî ṅhulun bibi hajînutus ira naranāŧa maṅkata,
ndān ṅkānêŋ himawāntapaṙwwata tĕhĕṙ paramarĕṣi sirêka rakṣanĕn,
Agyêki ṅhulun induŋ oliha yaśânĕmuha kawijayan ṅwaŋ iŋ raṇa,
denyâsaṅwa pati ṅwaŋ amrihakĕn iŋ nrĕpati pamuhakêŋ hutaŋ hurip*

ndān amwīta lumampaha ṅwaŋ ibu hetu maṅuƀayahitâmbĕk i ṅhulun,
haywâśoka pajātyan iŋ pinakaputra panuluyana đaṙmma niŋ yayaḥ,
ṅhiŋ pintaṅkw-i panambĕhanta pawĕkas-wĕkas aṅinakanê twas i ṅhulun,
praŋ kahyunkw-ibu len kasiṅhan iŋ ayun pakahawan iy asiḥ nareśwara*

Ūḍū maṅkana kapwa māsku tak aweḥ ṅhulun i kita lumakwa mapraṅa,
Ewĕḥ riŋ giṇa śūra riŋ raṇa ṅaranya kahali-halin i ṅhulun tuhan,
Āpan maṙmma dahat ra reṇa ni wĕkaṅku mapa ta wĕnaṅanta taṅgwana,
t-aṅhera pwa huwus wĕkaṅku kita haywa mamituhu ri saŋ nareśwara*

wruḥ ta ṅwaŋ manahâṅgagap manaḥ i saŋ narapati tan asiḥ nirê ṅhulun,
maṅke wyakti ni tan harĕp nira nihan ta kita bapa kinon mareŋ musuḥ,
sis milw-ânaku tan sinanmata narendra kita bapa makebu ri ṅhulun,
Āpan ṅūni riris nirê ṅhulun agöŋ ḍumawuḥ ika tumus tĕkêŋ kita*

tan maṅkêki n ade manampĕtana kāṙyya paṅutus ira saŋ nareśwara,
Ājñā niŋ guru teki tan dadi linaṅǥanan ibu paṅatīta ri ṅhulun,
yadyan mātya sadenya kapwa saha ƀakti ri haji makasoṅa ni ṅhulun,
ƀāgyan yan mahurip siwil palaṙ anĕmwa wiƀawa siḥ i saŋ hyaŋ i ṅhulun*

saŋ kṣepanya lumampaha ṅhulun ameta hawana niŋ akīṙttya riŋ jagat,
tan saṅkeŋ pamihaŋ sahuṙkkw-i kita cihna niŋ aguṇa kasiṅhawikraman,
jāti kṣatriya tan panoliha kadaŋ kula bapa bibi yāwat iŋ raṇa,
kastutyan kajayan lawan suꝁa nikaŋ ƀuwana kaharĕp i ṅwaŋ amriha*

Om putrâpa liṅanya reṇa ni wĕkaṅku pasayut ika tan wĕnaŋ kĕdö,
ndā sāmpun mapa tôjaraṅku ri kitânaku hali-halinaṅku niŋ wĕka,
nāhan taŋ paṅanugrahaṅkw-i tanayan mami kawaca maṇiknya ƀāswara,
lāwan ƀūṣana saṙwwaratna jayaśatru ta kita bapa denya riŋ raṇa*

dewī maṙmma sirê narendrasuta sāmba kinawacan irêki hinyasan,
sakweḥ niŋ maṇiƀūṣaṇâṙjja kinĕnākĕn ira tĕhĕṙ i saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
tuṣṭâmbĕk nira saŋ narendradayitā mulati ŋ anak umaṅkatâpraṅa,
cĕt moǥâsemu rĕs tikaŋ twas anahā ŋ pati karaṇa ni luḥ nirômijil*

lamlam tan pawalĕṙ halĕp nrĕpatiputra sawaŋ ira tawaŋ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,
Aƀrâwā maṅĕḍap maṇik nira sawintaŋ apupul i hiriŋ nikaŋ laṅit,
len taŋ hintĕn irêŋ kapö kumĕñaṙ aṅgyat akilat ahulap tiniṅhalan,
sākṣād handaru teja niŋ kawaca ƀāswara lagi tinahā n panunwana*

ry-aṅkat saŋ nrĕpaputra saṅka ri dalĕm nagara dinuluṙ iŋ hulat maliŋ,
līlā tañ jriḥ i paṅhaḍaŋ niŋ akire turida nira n aliṇḍuṅañ crĕmin,
tan seṅĕḥ rinĕbut riŋ ambĕk iŋ akūŋ karĕsĕpana makolihê sira,
maṙmmâṅde kĕtĕṙ iŋ twas asriŋ awaluy liriŋ ira yan anambaṅi ŋ liriŋ*

ceṭī kāṙwwa tuhan mahâṅucap-ucap turida nika ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
muṅgwî saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ hawan ri haliwat nrĕpasuta sahajâmirĕṅwakĕn,
liŋnyântĕnku lĕwös laṅö saŋ asawaŋ wulan araras anūkṣmakĕn lulut,
rāmya ṅwaŋ tumutâṅduluṙ kadi wulañjaṙ aṅirim aṅĕnoḥ sumaṇḍiṅa*

saŋ luṅhâsiha de tuhanku bapa tiṅhali gati niŋ akūŋ kĕnêŋ unĕŋ,
toliḥ griŋnya kakiṅkiṅan karakĕtan siḥ aṅusapi ri luḥnya meḥ tibā,
haywânĕṅgaḥ iwĕḥ sinambat iŋ apinta śayana tuluṅĕnta riŋ jinĕm,
tambānanta tĕmĕn tiki n lara matanya kalilipĕn i māsku tan lipur*

tustus niŋ mađu sāri niŋ kusuma saŋ ḍinawuhan i manaḥta yak maṅö,
nityâwastu manis nirânalaga riŋ muꝁa tĕlas apĕnĕd sinukṣukan,
Alwaŋ kūŋ raras iŋ manumbĕṙ ahawañ jaruman ahurusan maweḥ ṭikā,
maṅke ṅwaŋ turidâlarônĕŋ iki hetu niŋ awaraḥ akon tumiṅhala*

nāntĕn teki hajöŋnya kāri riŋ asaṅwa kuŋ umulat i tapwan iŋ gati,
yan muṅgwiŋ kakawin manisnya pinakāntya mamutusi tĕkap Iŋ aṅrĕṅö,

rāhasyâƀaya niŋ rasanya saꝑalârasana tamakĕnêŋ pasaṅgaman*

nāhan liŋnya waneḥ dudū saŋ aṅaraŋ sumĕmu-sĕmu rĕṅūnya yan liriŋ,
riṅraŋ haṙṣa rimaŋ-rimaŋnya n alarâwiṅit aṅĕsaḥ awaṙṇna kasrĕpan,
maṙmmanya n paturū ya tânamara lĕŋlĕŋ arurub asanâhulĕs gaḍuŋ,
kady-âṅipya mareŋ smarālaya mahĕnwa lĕyĕp i kukus iŋ hrĕbuk miṅiŋ*

wwantĕn ƀrānta kĕdö manūtakĕn unĕŋnya karakĕtan aminta sanmata,
tamtam ry-ambĕk ikâṅajap midĕra riŋ wukiṙ amasaha kūŋnya riŋ pasir,
maṅkin lĕŋlĕŋ atön gĕrĕḥ raras i rūmnya n aṅidani laṅö nikaŋ rimaŋ,
jañjan citta niki n tan eṅĕt i sĕkaṙnya tan atutuṙ i luṅsuṙ iŋ gĕluŋ*

Akweḥ taŋ paricārikâmĕkulakĕn lulut ika ri nareśwarātmaja,
tuṅtuŋ niŋ turidanya rakwa riŋ awaknya sinahaja winiṅkis iŋ laṅö,
len kiṅkiŋ lara kūŋ maṅĕn-haṅĕn ikaŋ rĕṇa pamawan unĕŋ raras hati,
rĕs rūm-rūm i liriŋnya haṙṣa pamalanda nika winawanâmatan-matan*

sāmpun prāpta ri heŋ narendratanaya praṇata ri sira saŋ halāyuđa,
Amwīt maṅkata māṙ manāntwa mawĕlas ri sira tĕhĕṙ aweḥ warāyuđa,
ndā tapwan masuwe muwaḥ sira marê narapati harimūṙtti riŋ saƀā,
ndān amwīta muwaḥ lawan pinĕkĕtan gati nira hana riŋ himālaya*

ndān saŋ śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa māṙ hati nira n mulat iŋ anak umaṅkatâlaga,
waspâgātra dine hasiḥ nira sinambay anaku liŋ irâṅgamĕl taṅan,
maṙmmêŋ putra maśabda manda wĕkasan ta manaṅis asĕkĕl nareśwara,
ramyârūm karĕṅö kunĕŋ pĕyĕḥ ikaŋ swara kadi gĕrĕḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat*

ndā putraṅku suđīrakĕn sapaṅutusku dumamĕlakĕn iŋ prajāhita,
haywêwĕḥ pinakāśrayâmbĕk awilāsa ŋ amalaku parāśrayê kita,

matyâmatya jayanta tan mupakarêŋ pinahayu nira wīra tan surud*

tan pamƀagnakĕnêŋ harĕp-harĕp iŋ aty-amalaku śaraṇâtiduhꝁita,

tuṅgal-tuṅgala kastawan prakaśitâđipati ṅaran ira ñ jayêŋ raṇa*

yan bwat kṣatriyađaṙmma niŋ yadukulâkral anuluṅi kahaywan iŋ prajā,

lagy-âśoca ri luḥ nikaŋ ǥariṇi niŋ musuḥ amalaku milwa patyana*

haywâjīwita yadyapî ƀaya marê kapĕjaha tuwi haywa saṅśaya,
kastutyanta ꝑalanya göṅakĕna de niŋ aṅulati lĕkasta rakṣaka,
yeka kṣatriyađaṙmma tan dadi surud tumuluṅa ri saduhꝁa niŋ para*

jīwājīwa ni saŋ mahāpuruṣa donya dadaha ri kahaywan iŋ jagat,
kīṙttyākīṙttya ni saŋ huwus krĕtayaśâmuli-muliha wiśīṙṇna niŋ prajā,
đaṙmmāđaṙmma ri siŋ pinaṇḍita mahāṙdđika pinakapatīṙŧan iŋ sarāt,
putrāputra tumiṙwwa kāṙyya nira saŋ wwaŋ atuha laki yogya tūtakĕn*

yan wwaŋ śakti tan ahyun iŋ yaśa hade kinarajakĕna śakti riŋ para,
maṅkā wwaŋ mapirak yadin kapana tan pamirakana sarāt ya tan padon,

tañ jīwān ika jīwa niŋ wimuꝁa riŋ hayu kadi-kadi jīwa niŋ kĕnas*

nyā ŋ kāṙyyâđiparatra teki riŋ akāṙyya sĕḍĕŋ i kahananya sāđana,
mwaŋ kāṙyyâmuhara prasidđa hayu yêka katĕmu riŋ ihatra don ikā,
kāṙyyā kāṙyyakĕnanta kāṙyya saꝑalâmuhara kasuꝑalanta riŋ jagat*

saŋ niṣkāṙyya ri saŋ kṣinatriya tanora hinaliwatan i ṅhulun kabeḥ,

yatnêkī kita sātiruny-aku gumantyana n asuꝁa maran pwa yâbuṅaḥ,
pöŋ-pöŋ yowana śaktimanta kita saṅhulun anaku lĕwas paṅāśrayan,

māry-âweha kaṅelanêŋ atuha kapwa kahalĕpa nikaŋ tĕkêŋ tĕkan*

wwantĕn śabda niraŋ rĕṣi prawara nārada ri kita rikāna keṅĕti,
tan wwaŋ len kita rakṣakā liŋ ira riŋ himagiri śaraṇā mahāyati,
nāhan taŋ laras uttamâtiśaya śakti nika ya ta pawehan i ṅhulun,
Om swasŧā tanayaṅku māsku jayaśatru ta kita bapa riŋ himālaya*

toḥ t-aṅkat hara pöṅakĕn hayu nikaŋ diwasa makaꝑalā ŋ kadigjayan,

wwantĕn daṙśśaniyêŋ raras wwaŋ apaṅus prawala ṅaran ikaŋ kadaŋ haji,
Anwam pantĕs amaṅku pawwahan iraŋ nrĕpasuta manulus wicakṣaṇa,

lampaḥ niŋ raŧa rāmya riŋ lĕbuḥ atūt palipiran i harĕp nikaŋ tĕpas,
mambö wāluka denya keriṙ i siriṙ niŋ anila mapulaŋ lawan hrĕbuk,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda waṙṇna masyaŋ umarêŋ acala dumulurê nrĕpātmaja,
grit niŋ cakra nikaŋ raŧâsĕmu surak pinarĕṅan i gĕrĕḥ munî du lor*

meǥâbāŋ mahirĕŋ waneḥ asĕmu riṅriŋ anawĕṅi hiriŋ nikaŋ laṅit,
kuntul möṙ aduluṙ ñamut-ñamut awaṙṇna mĕnuṙ aluñut iŋ gĕluŋ lukar,
mandrâlon kĕtĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ kadi taṅis niŋ ahayu kawĕkas hanêŋ jinĕm*

tuṅhā niŋ paraṅan lĕṅöŋ hana wuruŋ-wuruṅan niŋ atanaḥ karîŋ śilā*

paṇḍan raṅkaŋ atuntunan ri tĕpi niŋ pasiṙ asira-siran karaŋ liman,
kady-aṅlaṅhuy ariṅgĕkan ri tĕka niŋ bañu pasaŋ amatĕmwakĕn harus,
kĕmbaŋ laywan awoṙ karamkam apulaŋ lagi karawit i roknya karyakan,
Aṙjjā gātra nikaŋ puḍak-puḍak acihna kakawin iŋ akūŋ katuṅhapan*

strī wāhw-âdaluwaŋ tigaŋ siki kapaṅgiḥ anamun i parasnya riŋ pilis,
ndan rakwêka marâṅirim ri saŋ adihyaŋ amawa ri sakāpti saŋ pĕjaḥ,

byaṙ kĕbyaṙ siniriṙ-siriṙ niŋ aṅin edi kadi sĕmi pamiṅkisan puḍak*

Olaḥ niŋ  ṙyyak alumba-lumba maṅusiṙ paraŋ atĕpi guhā liwaŋ-liwuŋ,
lwiṙ kuṅkaŋ karĕṅö swaranya jĕmuṙ iŋ paraŋ anaragi mandra kāṅinan,
himpĕṙ hintĕn awoṙ pawal sira-siratnya ri papupul ikaŋ sahiŋ-sahiŋ,
kady-âpet kalaṅön katon uwuṙ-uwuṙ nika karakĕt i duṅhus iŋ karaŋ*

nūsânuṅgalakĕn laṅö lĕṅĕŋ ikâhyun anarukaha rāmya niŋ pasir,
ndan pakṣâmadanāśramêka rinĕgĕpnya n aṅusira parantya niŋ maṅö,

cöt sidđy-âniluman katon kakĕñaran rawi lĕyĕp ajamaŋ kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ*

ṅkānêŋ lod hana ta plawā nikaŋ amañciŋ aparahu jukuŋ panuṅgalan,
rūpanyâputiḥ aṅhulap-hulap apan lumarap i larap iŋ wway iŋ tasik,

mumbul pwa ŋ gajamīna kāraṇa nikân paṅĕcĕpuk awĕlaḥ mareŋ tĕpi*

<śiꝁariṇī>:4.

sawaŋ kanyā lwiṙ niŋ pasisiṙ i halintaŋ nrĕpasuta,
lĕṅöŋ waṙṇnanyâhyas mapata-patahan taŋ  ṙyyak alaṅö,
layaṙ niŋ baṇyāgânusu-nusu katon manda tan awās,
limut niŋ wway māwrâsĕmu-sĕmu pupuṙ piṅhay i pipi*

huwus luṅhâdoḥ saŋ nrĕpasuta tĕkêŋ wanwa masĕnĕt,
Alas loṙ kulwan wetan ika marĕnĕb tīṙŧa maparĕk,
pucaŋ mwaŋ nyū makrĕp walahaṙ ika tūbanya gumuruḥ,
makĕmpoŋ-kĕmpoŋ taŋ palu daluwaŋ asraŋ masawuran*

Aliṅgiḥ riŋ watw-aṙjja śumayana kāliḥ pamucaṅan,

paṅādeśā sambat kawĕkas i lawö niŋ puḍak arūm*

hanêki n kaṙwwêstrī wĕḍihan ika ragyan wahu lĕsĕḥ,

trĕbis wiṣṭi lwiṙ niŋ kahawan asamīpâlas alaṅö,
paraŋ groŋ-groŋ roŋ niŋ juraŋ i hiriṅanyâmuwuhi rĕs,

Arimbit kambaŋ rimbaŋ iŋ acala rūmnyâmuwuhi kūŋ,

tuhun kambaŋ laywan paṅisi ni rarasnya n winulatan*

liraŋ ramyâjaṅjaŋ pinanuliṅakĕn de nikaŋ ĕpiŋ,

kunĕŋ nyāpan ratryâṅhinĕpa ta ranak saŋ muniwara,

kamāhātmyan saŋ paṇḍita masiha ri twas niŋ umara,

Ikaŋ sanđyā sāmpun marahup asalin ƀūṣaṇa sira,

wulan piŋ nĕm riŋ kāṙttika kahatuṙ aṅde turida kūŋ,
sahaṙṣâsyaŋ rowaŋ nini tapi marâṅdon amĕŋ-amĕŋ,
kunĕŋnyê saŋ sāmbâṅawaśakĕn arĕpnyêŋ hati pinĕm,
Uḍū saŋ tāmuy liŋ niki n api kasaṇḍuŋ mapi gigir*

hanâtaṇḍak ramyâṅiduṅakĕn unĕŋnya n karakĕtan,

rahinâwa waspada patiṅkaḥ i kayu ri sare nikaŋ gĕgĕr,
pacakiṅkuk iŋ bakikuk aṅlawani gaguŋ i piṅgiṙ iŋ juraŋ,

Irikā nini hyaŋ awuṅū dadakan inatag iŋ hayam halas*

lwaḥ i tīra tan lumaris iŋ muꝁa mahiwagakĕn susuk-susuk,
śawa niŋ maṅö saha laras kusuma wĕkas ikânusup-nusup*

Anĕḍĕk patiṅhalan ikaŋ jalađi riŋ anĕkâ kasaŋ carik,
tan apujy-anajyakĕn ikaŋ sarasi saha lawan huraŋ tanaḥ,
riŋ awaṙgga rūmnya karikā tan asĕgĕha tĕmĕn pananmata,
riŋ ahimya-himyan iki len kawi paḍa mapasuṅsuṅan hañaŋ*

katĕkāna rāmya riŋ añaṙ palabuhan alaṅö tiniṅhalan,
ri pĕkĕnya kambaḥ asarik racana ni pajajaṙnya len tĕpas,
warugâruhuṙ paṅuṅaṅañ jinamanikan i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
pamalantĕnanya karĕṅö swara ni palu nikâṅiriŋ kiduŋ*

kahatuṙ manis pĕkĕn ikâtiśaya suꝁa ḍatĕŋ nrĕpātmaja,
Atihaŋ-tihaŋ tarima têkiŋ amalija lulut paḍâhajöŋ,
Amuraḥ liriŋnya tinawākĕn ika ri haliwat nrĕpātmaja,
Irikā n katon kupa-kupaŋnya saha jaja sajöŋnya pintanĕn*

masuhun-suhun sĕkaṙ ikaŋ parawan ajaja kūŋnya kaṅlihan,
mawade hayunya ri harĕpnya hañaṅĕn ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
mwaŋ apaṅkwa-paṅkwana tĕṅaḥnya maṅusira tĕwas karāsikan,
lalu kāsihanya tuna kūŋnya manaḍaḥ-asihêŋ kuraŋ wĕlas*

haliwat nirêrikaŋ anaṙŧa pira-pira kadoḥ nira n huwus,
Aṅawinđyapaṙwwata ri pāṙśśwa nika hawan irâmuraŋ-muraŋ,
milu duhꝁa budđi nira de ni gatarasa nikā n kuraŋ tahĕn,
kadi melikêki riŋ apan sira mulati tĕgal nikâpaḍaŋ*

pakulan-kulan pasanakan kaludan ika samâṅhapit raras,
rwi sisiṙ pilaŋ rukĕm aṅap lumaru-laru sĕwönya riŋ sapāŋ,
kasine lĕwas kapanasan tĕlas akuniŋ i saṇḍiŋ iŋ hawan,
Aṅalas manis gula gumantuŋ ika tinĕmu niŋ mahas maṅö*

lumalay-lalay galiŋ ikânwam asuluṙ aṅayuḥ tahĕn ragas,
wruḥ ataṅkil iŋ lĕbak ikaŋ mata-mata kulumâṅuṅaŋ tawaŋ,
kalawan gaḍuŋnya sumĕkaṙ-mĕkaṙ ika kadi pahyas iŋ maṅö,
Umaḥ iŋ maƀaṇḍagiṇa paṇḍan ika ri baciṅaḥnya sök pacĕḥ*

lumaris muwaḥ nrĕpasutê hayunan ira ri mađya niŋ tĕgal,
rĕmĕŋ aṅdadak truḥ awĕlas ri gati nira n aṅölakĕn panas,
pawanâṅiriŋ miriṙ alon maṅatĕrakĕn i saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
gĕrĕḥ aṅhiṅöt-iṅĕti riŋ hawan ika dug aganti riŋ tĕgal*

gunuŋ ojayan wahu katon awuk-awuk aṅawuṙ sakeŋ adoḥ,
kadi kahyaṅan paṅalusan hyaŋ atanu kalaṅönya tan sipi,
Aruhuṙ lĕyĕp lwiṙ ilaŋ iŋ jalađara riŋ anūtakĕn laṅö,
paran iŋ limut gati nikâpatitisan iŋ ĕbun sakeŋ tawaŋ*

hiriŋ iŋ laṅit pili-piliḥ lalayan ira ƀaṭāra manmaŧa,
matulis laṅö ni jaladanya winĕtu-wĕtu niŋ samīraṇa,
I ruhuṙnya teja mawĕnĕs kinĕñarakĕn i polaḥ iŋ kilat,
wukiṙ ojayan kalimutan lĕyĕp asĕmu tulis hañaṙ lutur*

Anuluy lari nrĕpatiputra sira wahu sumĕṅka riŋ wukir,
kahiriŋ-hiriŋ lari nikaŋ raŧa ri hiriṅan iŋ gĕgĕṙ-gĕgĕr,
Irikaŋ juraŋ hana ta wuṅkuk akaramas amaṅkuk iŋ śilā,
kadi tiṅkaḥ iŋ susuḥ aneŋ watu maṅariŋ-ariŋ sakeŋ bañu*

Aliwat  nrĕpātmaja riŋ ojayan alaris ikaŋ raŧâgêlis,
Aniraŋ ri yātragiri rîmbaŋ ika hawan irâmuraŋ-muraŋ,
Agĕlaṙ tikaŋ wrĕṣaƀa hinwan iriya maduluṙ yaŧāsuꝁa,
tan awĕdy-anon gaja-turaṅga-raŧa paḍa lumakw-arampakan*

lwaḥ ahöt anambak karĕṅö swara gaṅari nikaŋ saraswatī,
kĕna śāpa rakwa karaṇanya n inĕnahakĕn iŋ tĕgal marū,
kawĕlas-harĕp tahĕn ikêŋ tĕpi sana-sini lot hibĕk lĕbū,
kasihan tan asmi hana maṅragasi lĕṅĕŋ aṅantyakĕn jawuḥ*

Awiwākṣitêka n alawas nrĕpatanaya lumampaḥ iŋ hĕnu,
ḍatĕŋ iŋ himādri sira n aṙjja mulati lĕṅĕŋ iŋ wanāntara,
patapan katiṅgal alawas kabuyutan ika saṇḍiŋ iŋ hawan,
Awiraŋ katonan ikaŋ aṙcca kajĕnĕkan aliṇḍuṅan tahĕn*

rāmya panuṅsuŋ iŋ himagirî nrĕpatisuta paḍâgawe parahita,

đaṙmma hilaŋ tĕlas kaḍĕḍĕtan kabubak i lalayanya tan kahuniṅa,

tan hana kapwa pakṣa hayu riŋ jagat i panaput iŋ tamaḥ maṅawaśa,
tan kabĕnĕṙ pradeśa nika de ny-awuṙ-awuṙ ika piṇḍa duṣṭa sagawe,

kagyat umunduṙ awri rumĕṅö hrik i kuda naranāŧaputra kadunuŋ,

taṙkka nikaŋ waneḥ riya turaṅga niŋ aburu katiṅgal iŋ lagi-lagi,
yan tan ikaŋ wiku pwa ya cumaṅkaḥ akuda lumagā lawan kita kunĕŋ,

haywa tatan prayatna haja denta jaḍa-jaḍa ri don i saŋ para rĕṣi,

tan kadi saŋ wiku wruḥ i rusit tutuk ika humĕnĕŋ hatinya kuṭila*

sūkṣma ri don ikaŋ wiku manīti yan inupakarâlĕmĕḥ mamalĕsa,

toḥ niyatanya maṅkana mataŋnya paran iki hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ dudu-dudū*

Om tuhu liṅta pāman aku ṅūni winaraḥ iŋ anon raŧâdulu-dulur,
wwaŋ paḍa wīrayođa ya wicakṣaṇa lituhayu rakwa mahyas asiga,

duṙjana saŋ watĕk rĕṣi ṅaranya maharĕp i halanta duṙyyaśa wiku*

ndaḥ mapa taŋ huliḥ bapa rare liŋ ika hana ta yâwrĕgas wariṅutĕn,
doḥ yatiku n kita n pamitahâwĕdi-wĕdi kita tan muwaḥ milu-milu,
denya paran kawĕdyana rikiŋ musuḥ aku lawananya mon hyaṅa tuwi,
yan tak utaŋ sugiḥ nira wĕnaŋ muliḥ aku turuŋ olihâṅjara-jaraḥ*

ƀoḥ t-ajĕjĕp muwaḥ paran ikaŋ makuda-kuda nihan waluy kita kabeḥ,
nā ta wuwusnya kapwa ya paḍâṅijiŋ ahaliṅan iŋ wwit iŋ tahĕn agöŋ,
liṅsiṙ ikaŋ wulan kadi mahânuluhi ri bala saŋ janāṙddanasuta,
hetu nikaŋ balāsura mulat yatika yatiku liŋnya yan paḍa humuŋ*

munduṙ adān ta yâruḥ-aruhan surak atĕhĕṙ atiṅkaḥ iŋ tĕgal alas,
byakta huwus gĕlaṙnya tumuluy nrĕpatanaya manuṅgaŋ iŋ raŧa nira,

parĕŋ asusun ikaŋ wil wīra riŋ praŋ magaṇḍi,

lawan umulûsusnya lumaḥ umambĕk*

hana ta tugĕl tuṙnya jĕnĕk aluṅguḥ,
maṅarut-arut mulyaṙ ika matanya,
Amalaku lūdĕn ta ya gupay aṅliḥ,
karaṇa nikâmātyakĕn iŋ awaknya*

hana ta kĕnêŋ hrū mata nika kāliḥ,
Aṅaway-away pwâmalaku tinuntun,
lumaku kasaṇḍuŋ titiṙ amurug rwi,
lalu kadunuŋ riŋ juraŋ anĕmu groŋ*

kasihan ikaŋ meḥ pĕjaha kacakra,
tikĕl i pupūnya n kanin ikana trus,
dalĕm i tatunya n ri ḍaḍa manumbĕr,
Ininum ike rāḥnya ya malapa wway*

tahĕn ikanaŋ pāṙśśwa kadi binaṅbaŋ,
makatiritis rāḥ kawĕkas i ronya,
makakuratil taŋ kuṇapa kasaŋsaŋ,
Usus awilĕt riŋ paŋ ika gumantuŋ*

ri pucak ikaŋ hori hana kasaṅga,
paru-paru limpā ri caraŋ ikâbāŋ,
sahaja dagiŋ mwaŋ hrĕdaya sumampir,
kadi ta manambe riŋ asura māti*

<girisa>:10.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – – –| – – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 16

nrĕpasuta sira mintaṙ ṅkā saṅkeŋ wana palagan,
dinakara sira māwās rāmya ŋ deśa winulatan,
limut anapihi kaywan keṅkab de niŋ aṅin alon,
hana luru-luruk aṅjraḥ mahw-aṅde lulut iŋ akūŋ*

wwara patapan asimpaṙ miṅkis kāmpiran iŋ unĕŋ,
kukus i patanĕkanyârok mwaŋ meǥa marawayan,
racana ni paciranyânyāsâṙjjâtulis alaṅö,
yan iŋ amarani kaṇṭa ṅhiŋ prāptâṅjĕnĕki maṅö*

nrĕpasuta dumunuŋ seriŋ mwaŋ ƀrĕtya nira kabeḥ,
kawaca linuputan len taŋ cāpāstra kinĕkĕsan,
lumaku sira marâdyus riŋ sĕñjaŋ suci mahĕniŋ,
ri tĕlas ira matīṙŧâmūjêŋ hyaŋ nĕhĕṙ ajapa*

kuda nira winiwekâṅheṙttalyânĕḍuni  paruŋ,
makin atika tinalyan de niŋ tis tan inasĕhan,
Umilu tika si dāruky-adyus tan tĕka sakarĕŋ,
Apan aṅurutut asriŋ Untunyâgaṭik akaṭuk*

ri huwus ira mamūjā saŋ sāmbâdara humarĕk,
ri sira muniwarâsiḥ maṙmmâswāgata masĕgĕḥ,
Anaku bapa tan iŋ rāt maṅke n prāpta kita huwus,
Uliḥ i pajapa ni ṅwaŋ priḥ rakṣanta kami kabeḥ*

kadi sinipi ganas niŋ dꜽtya ṅke mamarikala,
manikĕp anawan adwa lwiṙ doṣanya pinĕjahan,
kari patapan ikā sāk saŋ wikw-âlaradan adoḥ,
Aṅaluṣa tĕmahanyâmet uṅgwan manusu-nusup*

nahan ika pawaraḥ saŋ paṇḍyâśabda saha kĕtĕr,
narapatisuta māṙ maṅrĕṅwākĕn pawuwus ira,
tĕhĕṙ aṅupaśamākĕn saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja sumahur,
pala-palarĕn iŋ ambĕk rānak saŋ rĕṣi śaraṇa*

nrĕpatisuta tinamw-iŋ bwat sopācara mahalĕp,
barubi pinakasamsam luṅlūṅañ cinacaṙ ira,
kunaŋ aṅinaki ri twas tiṅhal saŋ muniduhitā,
karaṇa nira matambĕḥ kūŋ tapwan warĕg alulut*

ri tĕlas ira tinamw-î roṇḍon kāṅinan iŋ aṅin,
Akusa-kasikan olaḥ tamtamnya n warĕg aṅĕsaḥ,
nrĕpatanaya sinambe niŋ jriŋ pādapa maṅĕliḥ,
karaṇa nira n anoliḥ de niŋ syuŋ maṅaku kaka*

manuk awurahan asraŋ ṅkānêŋ ambulu matasak,
nyaŋ arĕbut i paŋ aṅjraḥ mwaŋ rowaŋnya siliḥ-adĕḥ,
ndan anĕṅĕn-aṅiwākĕn wwaḥ niŋ hambawaŋ umaḍam,
lutuŋ akĕmilan oṅsil siŋ roṇḍon piniliḥ ikā*

rusit ikaŋ acalâkweḥ priṅganyâjuraŋ apiṅit,
hapi mamaḍĕmi ŋ ampyal priŋnya ŋ nyū makin alupa,
marukĕt awilĕt odwad riŋ kaywan milu kawilĕt,
wruḥ aṅuṭilani rowaŋ budđinyâṅruhuṙ i hawan*

<Aśwalalita>:11.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

hana mata pājaran lĕṅĕŋ amānuṣênĕmukan iŋ himâraŋ anipis,
Aṅaṅaṙ-aṅaṙ katonan i sĕkaṙnya waṙṇna tulis iŋ sujînisisakĕn,

Apĕnĕd arūm paḍârĕs umiṅis lumaṇḍĕp i liriŋ nikâṅrĕsi hati*

guru kaki wāhu saṅka riŋ alas lawan tapa-tapâmikul huwi hilus,

nrĕpasuta lālanê suku nikaŋ wukiṙ jĕnĕk i rāmya niŋ sakamatan,

pinakapuriḥ saŋ uttama ǥinoṣita n pamarituṣṭa riŋ para nanā*

<wasantatilaka>: 12.
– – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 14

sāmpun kalaṅlaṅan ikaŋ suku niŋ himādri,
de saŋ narendrasuta sāmba suđīrajāti,
sakweḥ mahāṙṣi suꝁa tan hana wiǥnamātra,
yajña prasidđa ginaway nira dewapūjā*

Atyanta tuṣṭa nira saŋ wiku riŋ himādri,
tan dwâṅrĕṅö turaḥ i dānawaśatru kāri,
hetunya sāhasa muwaḥ rumaraḥ mahāṙṣi,
sabsab paḍanya n umarêŋ wiku tan padoṣa*

luṅhā ta saŋ rĕṣi paḍâṅhili nora kantun,
Āpan kasampaṙ aradin tinawan waneḥnya,
len maṅlawan mati turaḥnya kawös tinūt tlas,
ṅĕs-ṅösĕn epu manusup maṅusī guhâjro*

maṅkā tikaŋ tapa-tapi prihatin gupêpuḥ,
tan wriŋ paranya malayū manaṅis masambat,
runtiŋ tapiḥnya daluwaŋnya rujit kasambit,
santĕn ragĕt karagĕt iŋ rwi dumeḥ rarasnya*

mwaŋ saŋ watĕk guru ninîki maṅiṇḍit-iṇḍit,
tan saḥ panucyan ira len tĕnunan pamuswan,
lāwan tikaŋ wusu-wusū lawayan gumantuŋ,
kapwêka liŋ nira siluṅluṅan iŋ paratra*

Abwat kaki mpu burayut mamikul ry-anaknya,
rañcaknya mesi sapuluḥ sasisiḥ tinaṅguŋ,
puṇḍaknya kaṙwwa paḍa mesi wĕgig siliḥ-prĕp,
wadwān ikâmĕtĕŋ uwus kalimêŋ pisuswan*

maṅgĕḥ swađaṙmma nira saŋ macĕpuḥ sinuṇḍaŋ,
kāliḥ pwa ya n taṅan irôṅsil ikaŋ manuṇḍaŋ,
moǥêka kasrĕk irikaŋ wadarâwwaḥ akrĕp,
caṅkĕm nirêka maṅakĕp kaƀaran kacaṇṭyal*

kañcit ḍatĕŋ nrĕpatiputra lawan balâkweḥ,
kapwâmanaḥ sira lawan bala tan tahĕn twas,
Alwaŋ tikaŋ musuḥ aneka rinok paṅohan,
hetunya kaṇḍĕg alayū paṅarĕpnya kondur*

Enak ta budđi nira saŋ rĕṣiśiṣyasaṅǥa,
milwâpuliḥ saha patil suligi mwaŋ umban,
dukduk wuluḥ watu pinaṇḍĕmakĕn ya moliḥ,
saŋ mona māri humĕnĕŋ mamisuḥ sirâkrak*

saŋ dewagurw-aṅadu śiṣya marĕk manonton,
Ambĕk malañciṅan aniṅsĕti badđa ruñcud,
nā liŋ nirâpraṅa ta haywa takut hiḍĕpku,
mon ko mamāti kĕna teki musuḥku wāhya*

yan ko makoliha musuhmu mĕnêŋ payudđan,
ndak gañjaṙ iŋ basahan aṙjja tĕkêŋ jamaŋnya,
yapwan hanâṅgalaḥ amātyani riŋ prawīra,
denyâlaƀā pinahalĕp hana siṅhĕlanya*

maṅkin ta saŋ tapa-tapâmriḥ arampak apraŋ,
Endaḥ samaṇḍala-samaṇḍala paṇṭa-paṇṭan,
guntĕnya saŋ ǥalusĕkaṙ pinakāđikāra,
maṅrikwakĕn ta gati saŋ kabayan kaki hyaŋ*

Anyāt katon wiku turuŋ wiratîki mapraŋ,
Unduṙ wuwus nika tumandaŋ aṅuṇḍa dukduk,
tan wruḥ ta ko ry-aku pinun mun aṅakw-asajña,
liŋnyâgarap kasalahan ya masumba-sumbar*

len taŋ waneḥ wiku kapeṅin anon wanîŋ praŋ,
mĕṅgĕp tumūt ndan ahiwaŋ sinurak marâgyaŋ,
denyâpraŋ aṅragayaḥ aṅlawani ŋ prawīra,
keṅĕl kĕnêŋ watu wĕhaŋnya rurū bahĕmnya*

Anyāt paḍâlwaŋ abutĕŋ marukĕt siliḥ-prĕp,
rambut kasaṇḍuŋ akusut kadudut karĕṅgut,
rodrânahut ya sinahut maluñut siliḥ-tūr,
kapwâṅgrĕgut muwaḥ akañjaṙ aṅaṅgut-aṅgut*

Enak pataṅkĕp ikanâṅlaga riŋ kamantyan,
Eṅgal paḍâlwaŋ ananā wiku rākṣasâkweḥ,
maṅsö ta wadwa nira saŋ naranāŧaputra,
kapwâṅawit paḍa mamātyani śatru śakti*

sāmpun lĕpas ni warayaŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba,
tan pāntarânarawatâṅibĕki ŋ payudđan,
kontap kabĕntaṙ ikanaŋ suraśatru denya,
himpĕṙ śata n tumaji rūpa nikaŋ paḍôliḥ*

bĕntaṙ bubaṙ mababaran bala rākṣasâlaḥ,
maṅkin wiśīṙṇna hinudan-hudanan warāstra,
waṅkay matip mibab-ibab sawaneḥ katimpal,
waṅkwaŋ pupū hana tugĕl dalĕmanya runtuḥ*

kyāti pralamba tuhan iŋ bala dꜽtyawīra,
yekâpuliḥ mapagi wūk nrĕpaputra sāmba,
muṇḍôṇḍa śūla nika śakti malaṇḍĕp atwas,
maṅduk narendrasuta tan pañarik linesan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:13.

muntab krođa nikaŋ pralamba ri luput saŋ sāmba wīrottama,
hetunya n pamanaḥ mahâmaruputîŋ hrū śakti tan pāntara,
saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja śūra maṅlĕpasakĕn krorāstra sök tan pĕgat,
đwastêkaŋ panaḥ iŋ pralamba kasĕsĕb niśśeṣa kasyūḥ hilaŋ*

tan syūḥ yadyan ikaŋ musuḥ lawananâmbĕknyâpan alpāđama,
nāhan tôjaṙ i dārukîya karĕṅö de saŋ narendrātmaja,
nyā ṅhrū śakti kawođanâstra pamanaḥ saŋ sāmba siṅhākrĕti,
trus limpad hati niŋ pralamba kawĕnaŋ prāṇanya sāmpun hilaŋ*

luṅhârĕs malayū turaḥ-turaḥ ikaŋ dꜽtyômuliḥ riŋ pura,
riŋ pātāla waneḥ paranya mahawan riŋ jro nikaŋ sāgara,
ṅĕs-ṅösĕn winaliŋnya wiṣṇu manurun saŋ sāmba śūrêŋ raṇa,
meṅguŋ budđi nirâtakut maharĕp aṅhily-âpan awrin kawös*

tuṣṭâmbĕk nira saŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ mantuk mareŋ kahyaṅan,
mwaŋ śiṣya prajurit hulūnya makusut banđanya siṅsal waneḥ,
len taŋ mājarakĕn waninya makaput caṅkĕmnya de niŋ hidu,
wwantĕñ jriḥ maṅabuk haneŋ wuri yayânaṅgaḥ ya milwânuduk*

byātītan gati saŋ watĕk tapa paḍâgoṣṫi praŋ iŋ maṇḍala,
saŋ krĕṣṇātmaja mintaṙ aṅlarisakĕn lampaḥ nikaŋ syandana,
ramyâtūt gĕgĕṙ iŋ wukiṙ gaga-gagā ŋ deśâtatā koṅkulan,
himpĕṙ wastra putiḥ katiṅhalan ikaŋ toyâṅĕbĕk riŋ sawaḥ*

wwantĕn  kahyaṅan uttamêŋ halĕp apūṙwwâtyanta norâṅhirib,
denya n śoƀita kapwa saṙwwa hinĕduk nyāsanya ramyâlaṅö,
towy-âmiṅkiṅakĕñ juraŋ tĕḍunan iŋ wwe saṅka riŋ paṙwwata,
gĕntĕṙ niŋ bañu tan pasaṅkya karĕṅö mwaŋ śabda niŋ nīrada*

ꝁyātîŋ rāt sira wiśwamitra ƀagawān muṅgwîrikāŋ kahyaṅan,
tĕkwan rājarĕṣi prasidđa sira mājaṙ đaṙmma saŋ paṇḍita,
byaktêkâtiśayêŋ kasidđan ađikārôttuṅga śudđāgama,
sākṣāt śiṣya ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu manurun saṅkeŋ wadaryāśrama*

tiṅkaḥ rājya patiṅkaḥ iŋ patapan endaḥ de mahaṙṣy-âgĕlar,
maṅkā riŋ pasaƀān saƀān tĕkap ikaŋ śiṣyâtatâkweḥ marĕk,
sinyaŋ taŋ para śiṣya yan waśariṣâgasyak tanorâtuluŋ,
saŋ kily-âraras aṙjja saŋ tapi sĕḍĕŋ lindinya maṅde kĕcap*

cuṇḍuk saŋ naranāŧaputra ri siraŋ rājaṙṣi ƀakty-ârarĕm,
sambaḥ yôliḥ-uliḥ nirâdara sinuṅsuŋ riŋ śiwāmƀâpĕnĕd,
trĕpty-ambĕk nira yan hulūna nira rakwê saŋ mahāpaṇḍita,
maṅgā tan mulihêŋ purī sira yadin sambeganĕn saŋ rĕṣi*

saŋ śrī rājarĕṣi prahaṙṣa sira siḥ de saŋ narendrātmaja,
mojaṙ liŋ nira ƀāgya yan kita ḍataŋ maṅke rikeŋ āśrama,
moliḥ prāṙŧana ni ṅhulun yatiku paṅrakṣanta saṅkeŋ musuḥ,
byaktâwās kita hetu niŋ mari mariṅguŋ de nikaŋ rākṣasa*

ndā t-aṅheṙ sakarĕŋ t-arāṙyyan anaku wruḥ ṅwaŋ ri ṅeltâlaga,
towin taŋ turagâlapâkuru kuraŋ turw-âpa tan lālana,
tan wwantĕn mari kaŋ katĕmwa tan ikaŋ mās ƀoga riŋ kahyaṅan,
mwaŋ siŋ ƀūṣaṇa tan hanâṅlawananê śabdanta yan wruḥ kawi*

<Aṅgitahu>:14.

Alawas nrĕpaputra riŋ himādri,
pinakāśraya de niraŋ mahāṙṣi,
bala dꜽtya tatan muṅup kawös jriḥ,
suꝁa tan sipi saŋ yati n pamūjā*

hana śiṣya mahāṙṣi wiśwamitra,
maṅaran guṇadewa tan hanôli,
wihikan kawi gīta len palambaŋ,
ya ta sānaka de narendraputra*

lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pagagan paran kahāsan,
lalu lampaḥ ira n kaluṅha-luṅhā,
kawawê kahanan lĕwĕs laṅönya*

Irikā ta sira ñ jĕnĕk magoṣṫi,
rikanaŋ tarukan miriŋ śilâlwā,
sĕmi wāhu lĕwas ya tôṅgwan-uṅgwan,

<mattarāga>:15.
– – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 20

saŋ krĕṣṇaputra sira tâtañêŋ sakamatan ri saŋ rĕṣiputra,
mwaŋ maṇḍalêŋ giriwanāntara krama nikā kabeḥ tinañakĕn,
mājaṙ sirêki guṇadewa toḥ bapa tama ṅhulun tuhu-tuhu,
tan saṅśaya pwa ta manaḥta tiṅhalana rāmya niŋ sakamatan*

nyā ŋ maṇḍalârĕṇĕb agöŋ lawasnya marika n lanā kasiratan,
gaṅgā sakeŋ laṅit ikā n tumampuḥ i samīpakanya maparĕk,
nārāyaṇa pratita saŋ makāśrama sadeśa riŋ saƀuwana,
nāhan ta kāraṇa niki n pawitra paranâdidewaśaraṇa*

honya ŋ tapowana ri puñcak iŋ wukiṙ anak samaṙ kalimutan,
mandāra kaywan iŋ alasnya maṅjraḥ asĕkaṙ mapādapa waneḥ,
mandâhĕniŋ lwaḥ ika niṙmmalâtis apitowi tus niŋ acala,
himpĕṙ karas juraŋ ikâlaṅö paran i saŋ kawīśwara maṅö*

śrī yajñawatya sira saŋ pratiṣṫa pinakāđikāra nipuṇa,
sākṣāt ƀaṭāra rawi saŋ paṅajyan iŋ aweda ṅūni karĕṅö,
wākbajrapaṇḍita sira n prawādika wiśeṣa niŋ wruḥ aṅaji,
tāpāya riŋ wiku mawās tĕkap nira tatas riŋ āgamarasa*

rakryan lihat-lihatanêkiŋ āśrama lĕṅöŋ tiniṅgal alawas,
kapwâlaṅö trĕṇalatānya len kayumanis nikâwĕnĕs alĕk,
mwaŋ nāgapuṣpa nika rukṣa sinwam iŋ aśoka mambĕt aṅĕliḥ,
kumbaŋ nikâṅrĕŋ anaṅis midĕṙ sawaŋ asambat iŋ saŋ alalis*

tanseŋ halĕp niki rikāna rakwa kadi kendran iŋ kalĕṅĕṅan,
maṅke wiśīṙṇna kasihan kasiḥnya katunan karaśmin iŋ arūm,
lāwan tikaŋ wĕlas-asiḥ lanâṅalaya tansaḥ iŋ kayu sĕnö,
mwaŋ taŋ dwireꝑa milu kāsihan mabasahan kadut lĕwas awūk*

Atyanta rāmya nika tan hilaŋ paḍa madūm rarasnya n alaṅö,
bĕntaṙ sayat watu karaŋnya riŋ pacira kaswab iŋ tahĕn agöŋ,
rĕṅkā ni gopura śiwaknya lot kakasut iŋ wwad iŋ priḥ awilĕt,
syuḥ śīṙṇna maṇḍala nikârĕmuk gula-gulanya mantĕn amanis*

bapranya wuṅkal inukiṙ winimba wanitā winehan añaṅa,
rukṣâpasaḥ kapĕgatan sĕnĕŋnya kaduk iŋ rĕbaḥ tuwi tibā,
tan wriŋ kwananya karikā nimitta ni kucĕmnya lĕŋlĕŋ akusut,
sāmpun mayat lumabuhêŋ paraŋ ri lari niŋ priyanya kasihan*

Aṙccâparan karika ṅūni riŋ watu karaŋ tiniṅkaḥ arĕcĕp,
Aṅrĕs kasoṅan iŋ aśoka mĕmbaŋ asawit latâŋ jriŋ asĕmi,
piṇḍâlarâṅaluṣakĕn ry-awaknya lulurĕn siliḥ-jaga mĕlĕs,
kady-âpupuṙ muꝁa nikânĕlat kalumutan turuŋ karahupan*

wuṅkal hitĕm patiga niŋ taṭāka riŋ usāna runtuḥ anibā,
len taŋ kari ŋ wwad iŋ aśoka lĕŋlĕŋ asaput pakis dadu mirir,
daṙppâṅlumuḥ mara śilodakanya tumibêŋ prĕduŋ-prĕduŋ aroŋ,
waṙṇnâkĕcap salaḥ-asê rarasnya n inatīta maṅkin alaṅö*

śrīdanta len mĕnuṙ awoṙ lawan trĕṇalatâṅayuḥ wuṅa tali,
sakweḥ nikā wĕlas-arĕpnya tībra kasihan tinambaŋ alawas,
Aṅhiŋ katiṅhalan ikaŋ walik-haḍĕp ikâhyasan linihatan,
mahyun lawad-lawadĕn iŋ kawipriya kunĕŋ mataŋnya n asĕkar*

tañjuŋ wuṅū suraƀi campakâsana marok lawan surataru,
ramyâśilā kumalasā ri soṙnya katiraḥ rumiṅriŋ alaṅö,
paṇḍan lĕṅis rĕbaḥ apan hibĕk gaḍuŋ apiṇḍa tan kahuniṅa,
Eman puḍaknya n abuṅaḥ katon kadi wĕtis niŋ adyaḥ aturū*

ndā paṅrĕṅö ra tapa rakryan aṅgĕḥ ika ṅūni rakwa tarukan,
saŋ đaṙmmadewa sira wiṣṇuputra matapêriya n panaruka,
saṅke kasidđyan ira tulya kendran ikahĕn tapowana nira,
himpĕṙ hyaŋ indra sira deniŋ apsara kabeḥ sumewa ri sira*

saŋ yajñawaty-atiśayêŋ raras kalulut iŋ janāṙddanasuta,
norâṅhirib hayu nirâmanis pituwi katwaŋ iŋ surawađū,
sakweḥ nikaŋ kusuma kāṅinan musiṙ i rūm nirêka mapupul,
sinwam lanā kaṅĕlihan tumirw-i lĕmĕs iŋ tĕṅaḥ tinapihan*

<mrĕdukomala>:16

dewī yajñawatī tiniṅgal ira đaṙmmadewa wĕkasan,
kāri ṅkê patapan tamolaḥ agawe tapabrata ginöŋ,
tan len rakwa sināđya de nira katĕmwa de saŋ alalis,
saṅke tībra nikaŋ larônĕŋ irikā n sirâlabuḥ apuy*

tapwan māri wuwus niraŋ rĕṣisutâwaraḥ duga-duga,
cĕb ṅöṙ twas nira saŋ narendratanayâṅrĕṅö kapĕnĕtan,
Aṅrĕs citta nirâwĕlas tutuṙ i saŋ katiṅgal aturū,
māṙmma mrāt twas ira n tĕñuḥ ri gati saŋ priyā n kasiḥ-arĕp*

tībrâkūŋ sira sāmba mohita rinañca niŋ lulut unĕŋ,
ndi pwêkāna wĕkasta māsku liŋ irânĕhĕṙ maguliṅan,
tan dwâlĕk lumĕyĕp kapaty-apĕga yat mĕgĕŋ lara nira,
liṇḍu taŋ kusumâkĕtĕṙ praƀawa gĕntĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ alon*

Āśāƀūta manastapa prihati teki saŋ rĕṣisuta,
yaṙ ton saŋ naranāŧaputra kapĕjaḥ ndatan pakaraṇa,
maṙmmanyâṅgugaḥ epu liŋnya laki t-aṅliliṙ kita bapa,
sowenya n panaṅis kamantyan atutuṙ ta saŋ nrĕpasuta*

Enak de nrĕpaputra meṅĕt awĕwĕḥ ta luḥ nira tibā,
masrĕt de niŋ aśabda kewala sĕkĕl nikaŋ hati tĕñuḥ,
sambat-sambat ira ndatan sꝑuṭa pĕgat-pĕgat saha kĕtĕr,
lwiṙ kumbaŋ maṅisĕp sĕkaṙ swara nirânaṅis katanĕhan*

nāhan liŋ nira he kakâṙṣitanaya ṅhulun mawaraha,
ṅūni mūla ni janma ni ṅhulun anak ƀaṭāra puruṣa,
nityâṅgöŋ tapa đaṙmmadewa ṅaran i ṅhulun prakaśita,
tan len yajñawatī prasidđa sisihanku haṙṣa rasika*

ndaḥ yekī patapanku ṅūni paḍa keṅĕtan tahĕn ikā,
mwaŋ tekī wulakanya padyusan i kāsiḥ i ṅhulun ike,
tāmankw-îki batuṙnya mātra katutuṙ kw-asiŋ sĕkaṙ arūm,
paṅlīlāṅkw-iki paṅhyaṅanku ri tĕlaskw-amuṣpa majapa*

sakweḥ niŋ paricārikâpsarawađū paḍâhayu rare,
pantĕs ƀāwa nikā hanêrikaŋ aśoka rambay asĕkar,
yan sore paḍa mamrĕm iŋ grĕhalatâkĕmit gati nikā,
dewī muṅgw-irikaŋ jinĕm sira lawan ṅhulun siliḥ-asiḥ*

maṅjanma pwa ƀaṭāra keśawa tumūt ṅhulun nda maṅĕnĕs,
tan pamwīt ṅhulun i sira n kari haneŋ tilam saŋ aturū,
tan toliḥ lara niŋ katiṅgal apan aprĕgi ṅwaŋ alayū,
de niŋ nāgata tan kapaṅgiha wĕkas ƀaṭāra mahulun*

nāhan teki nimitta ni ṅhulun aṅaryakĕn ri saŋ arūm,
tan saṅkeŋ lalis i ṅhulun ṅhulun iki pwa ƀakti mayayaḥ,
ndan saŋ yajñawatī kunĕŋ salaḥ-iḍĕp manĕṅgaḥ alalis,
maṙmmanya n pamalĕs larê hati tĕwĕk nikâlabuḥ apuy*

hana ta kunaŋ tĕkapaṅkwa lumipura lulutkw-iri saŋ tĕkasiḥ,
suꝁa pĕjahâkw-atapêŋ wukiṙ anusupa tan maluyêŋ nagara,
satĕmahanaṅkwa lawan rasika tuhun apaṅgiha tan kasaha,
saꝑala tikâku siwin tan uwaha ri gatiṅku n aniṅgalakĕn*

hanaṅisi māsku kitâraras alaris aweḥ lara kūŋ ri hati,
ndi ta kahananta tuhanku maṅusapana luḥku nihan t-aṅadĕg,
hanawaŋ unĕṅta manambat i kita saŋ anūkṣma pinet ri hati*

ṅkapana manista katĕmwa rari dĕlĕ-dĕlönku rikaŋ kusuma,
wukiṙ aparan ta kunaŋ pamulikana hayunta lĕṅit dahatĕn,
tak arusuhâku yadin lumayarana rarasta yan iŋ pasisi,
mabayaṅanêŋ gagana ṅka turida ni kakanta mamet ri kita*

rumiṅa-riṅâku ri kambaŋ iŋ asana miṅiŋ ri pipinta rari,
katĕmu ri lūm niŋ aśoka lĕmĕs i panĕpinta maminta hulĕs,
hirĕŋ i laṭinta haneŋ tĕbu hirĕŋ amanis sinĕsĕp-sĕsĕpan,
gĕmuḥ i susunta jugâmĕkasi hati nimitta niŋ agriŋ akūŋ*

munisuta maṙmma tĕmĕn sira ri lara narendrasutâṅawaśa,
Irika mataṅguḥ ujaṙ t-adiwasa bapa denta wimūṙcꞓa dahat,
puriḥ ikanaŋ dadi duhꝁa gati nika mataŋnya n ade hiḍĕpĕn,

hana laki tatwa nikaŋ dadi ginaway anitya dadinya kabeḥ,
Anili-niliḥ wiṣaya ŋ manĕmu suꝁa ƀinukti maweḥ prihati,
prawala nikā saŋ aṅenak-inaki ŋ aniliḥ suꝁa moǥa jĕnĕk,
saŋ anĕmu ƀoga ta yan wruha ta sira pinaṇḍita yogya tirun*

lawan ikahĕn tĕmaḥ iŋ wwaŋ akurĕn apasaḥ ta wasāna nikā,
siḥ ika sināhakĕn iŋ pati kalawan inaknya winaṣṭa kabeḥ,
kunaŋ ikanaŋ kari moǥa karakĕtan i rāmya niki n kaƀaran,
Ikaŋ alarê tĕka niŋ pati niyata turuŋ wruḥ ikā n maṅaji*

Iki paṅucap ra ƀujaṅga nira n upaśamê naranāŧasuta,
pitutuṙ i saŋ wihikan tiki juga winuwus ra tapanta rĕṅön,
Ujaṙ ira saŋ guṇadewa mawaraha ri budđi narendrasuta,
ya ta maṅĕne hati hetu ni hĕnĕŋ ira sāmba marĕn manaṅis*

sĕḍĕŋ ira sāmba wimohita tĕka ta tilottamā dewawađū,
Acaru sĕkaṙ ya ri cetya ni hawu nira yajñawatî patapan,
Atapi-tapiḥ gula gaṇṭi tinulis iŋ ĕmas lusuhan saŋ arūm,
Aṅĕmulakĕn suji hantuk i taṅan ira yajñawatī manuji*

kawula nira ŋ nrĕpaputra tumuluy atutuṙ syuḥ ika twas ira,
maṅucapa tan wĕnaṅê pawaraḥ hana yan eliṅa saŋ sapanĕn,
maṅĕn-aṅĕn ambĕk irê saŋ ahayu kari de nira riŋ śayana,
karaṇa ni waspa nirânaputi mata matâmuharâmanisi*

wĕkasan anāntwa sirê saŋ amaraduhitā liŋ irêki nihan,
kaka pu tilottamā tan sinipi puji-pujinta kitâtiśaya,
nahan ika liŋ nira saŋ sinapa midĕm-idĕm wruḥ i saŋ manapa,
Aṅiriṅi līṅan ira mpu tapa ya ta nimitta nirâpihĕnĕŋ*

muwaḥ awuwus ta narendrasuta kaka tilottamā t-âjarakĕn,
wĕkas iy arinta saŋ apsarapatiduhitā ndi manis rasika,
luwaṙ i taṅanku raras nira n aṅuwahi raśmi nirân pinĕkul,
kita karikâṅĕñĕp iŋ maṇik apuji laṅö ṅwaŋ ike mulata*

<jagadđita>:18.

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ narendratanayânĕhĕṙ amĕpĕṙ i saŋ tilottamā,
kepwan saŋ tinañan manaṅśaya paniṅgala nira muwahêŋ suputrikā,
ndātan mājara māṙ manaḥnya mawĕlas ri pamalaku ŋ asiḥ nrĕpātmaja,
rañcâmbĕk ri hatinya meḥ bĕlaha papraṅan iŋ aṅĕn-aṅĕn siliḥ-dĕhā*

Akweḥ siḥnya ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja nimitta ni sahuṙ ika maṙmma haṙṣaja,
siṅgiḥ māti saŋ apsarendraduhitâturun apuy i hilaṅta riŋ tilam,
ndā maṅjanma huwus ri saŋ praƀu riŋ uttaranagara wiśeṣaputrikā,

riŋ kanyāpuri r-uṅgu de saŋ asurendra rikaŋ alaya ratna len saꝁī,

t-aṅkat t-elu mare sira ṅhulun anuntunakĕn i kita haywa saṅśaya*

mwaŋ saŋ sāmba kunĕŋ sira mpu guṇadewa muwaḥ umuliḥ iŋ tapowana,
byātītan hana riŋ hĕnū tucapa saŋ maṇik iŋ ahayu rājakanyakā,
riŋ raṅkaŋ maṇijātirĕṅga sira n aṅliḥ aṅaraŋ inaweśa niŋ smara*

mewĕḥ saŋ wihikan ri budđi nira mesi turida wahu kabwatan raras,
sūkṣmāsāri wināwan iŋ sasisihan siḥ ira hana tikĕl nikaŋ halis,

luñcip niŋ mata dug siṅîṅid-iṅidan winiṣan iŋ amanis mamātyani*

siṅgiḥ yan sira puṣpamūṙtti katĕṅĕṙ paṅawak ira n añampakâkuniŋ,
māmbö rūm ni gĕluŋ nirâhirĕŋ awaṙṇna maṅunĕŋ akilâriris mĕnur,
luṅsuṙ niŋ pupuṙ aṙjja mātra karakĕt ri wijaŋ araras aṅhrĕbuk lĕwas,
śumrīdanta mĕkaṙ katon waja nirâhidu mađu karikā lanā manis*

rūm niŋ puṣpa laṅö ni sinwam iŋ aśoka piniturun i rāmya niŋ kapat,
kapwâṅjanma raras narendraduhitā mamanisi mađu niŋ sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,
sākṣāt śrī ni kalaṅwan iŋ pasisi saṙwwa sĕkaṙ iŋ acalâdi niŋ laṅö,
lakṣmī niŋ puḍak aṅdadî wĕtis ira n lagi pinapag i dèwa niŋ ṭikā*

maṅkā rakwa laris nikaŋ wataŋ aṅāśraya ri jariji saŋ suputrikā,
sinwam niŋ taru nāgapuṣpa n amiraḥ kakaratala rarasnya de nira,
hyaŋ-hyaŋ niŋ salagâkucup mulati sāri ni manis ira tan kĕneŋ lĕwas,

nyā ŋ kĕmbaŋ niŋ wakāta n rakĕt i talapakan soṙ ikê jöŋ suputrī,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ rājasâṅdohi gisi-gisi tĕwas tan kĕnā rūm pan ajriḥ,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ nāgapuṣpâhiwaŋ aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt riŋ kapö ndi n kahopa,
kĕmbaŋ gaṅsal kĕtêriŋ rahat i laṭi nira n rakta somyâṅĕne twas*

Osik taŋ puṣpasāry-âṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn i raras rūm niraŋ rājakanyā,
luṅhâṅilya ṅhrĕbuk de ni wida nira sumāṙ mūṙ ikaŋ campakâmrik,

sore sāmpun ḍawuḥ sapta tĕka kaka rĕken kāsi-kāsiḥ suputrī,

ƀaṅginya n poliḥ-oliḥ hatuṙ inamĕṙ ikiŋ sinwam iŋ nāgapuṣpa,
wwantĕn tênduŋ tĕmĕn saŋ paran iŋ aṅĕn-aṅĕn liŋnya n antuk manĕmbaḥ*

Ambĕk saŋ rājakanyā winaśa-waśa rĕsĕp siḥ nirê saŋ sahaṙṣā,
Āpan mambö kahambö turida nira pinĕm ndan yayâpet raras rūm,
nāhan pājaṙ nira ndi n kusuma kaka mapet patya māṅuṅsya kumbaŋ,
Aṅhiŋ yan wwantĕn iŋ campaka mĕkara sakeŋ nīradâku n sarāga*

nā liŋ saŋ rājakanyā smita nira tan awās waṙṇna maṅrwâsĕnötan,
maṅkin haṙṣā sahaṙṣâṅriṅa-riṅa turidâṅgītakĕn kūŋ niŋ onĕŋ,
tan makweḥ aṅladi twas kiduŋ iki n atĕrĕḥ sūkṣmarāgâṅrĕsi twas,
kĕmbĕŋ niŋ luḥ tikĕl niŋ halis ira panuwal saŋ sĕḍĕŋ maprapañca*

sāmpun prāptêña pahyas nira n apĕnĕd arūm strī walū rājapatnī,
tapwan pānak sama mwaŋ rara pamulu nikânwam susunyâkas ahrit,
tan saḥ riŋ rūm kahambö ri pipi pinaraban ya ŋ parab saŋ madihyaŋ,
meṅĕt tañcānatañcā panĕṅĕṙ ira ri saŋ swāmi cihnêŋ kasatyan*

maṙmmâjaṙ dyaḥ tuhan toḥ t-atĕlasana sapiḥ pwa ŋ sĕkaṙ putra-putran,
milwî saŋ ṅāṙyya nak rakryan apa sira yayaḥta n yayi ṅwaŋ turuŋ wruḥ,
nā liŋnyâwaṙṇna kepwan saŋ ahayu tinañānya n midĕm yan paśabda,
wwantĕn riŋ twasku saŋ sūkṣmaturida husirĕn tan sꝑuṭâliśya-liśyan*

wruḥ riŋ ceṣṭâmacĕḥ rāga nira ri gati saŋ rājaputrī n kĕnêŋ kūŋ,
Āpan sāmpun maṅambaḥ wuni niŋ amuni haṙṣâwiraŋ yan wruhêkā,
hetunyâdandan ahyas hana saji humaḍaŋ mwaŋ sĕkaṙ mrik dinānan,
gundik ramyâtatā maṅharĕpakĕn anawuŋ puṣpa niŋ kanyakâṅjraḥ*

māyā nrĕpaduhitâwaṙṇna ratiḥ apet hayw-aniru-niru hyas nira madanastrī*

saŋ śrī nrĕpaduhitā sāmpun alulud amraŋ buṅaḥ ira himpĕṙ kanaka sinaṅliŋ,
wāhw-âsalin atapiḥ raṇḍi tinulis iŋ mās miriṙ amarantĕn mamutuhi santĕn,
luṅgī hayu nira norâmaḍani dudug riŋ laṅit anawaŋ nīrada masĕnö bāŋ,

Om kaka siṅgiḥ ujaṙtta dalu kasihan i ṅwaŋ alĕḥ piniṅit,
mepu haneŋ nagarâsurawarapuri tiṣṭa lanā n kinĕmit,
ṅūni haneŋ pura len ṅhulun iki tinawan mapasaḥ riŋ yayaḥ,
ṅke pwa taya ŋ kulawaṙgga dalihan iŋ amintani han wijila*

Āḥ kapanêki tuwuḥku karakĕtana rāga sinaṅśayakĕn,
dūra karambatanê lulut iŋ apaṅus aṅrĕs aweha raras,
mawwad aluŋ marikiŋ turida wirasa ta pwa lawan sirarā,
mātaŋ akiŋ ṅwaŋ akiṅkiŋ amariṅin akiŋ biṣama n prihawak*

ndā yatiki n karaṇaṅku n apĕga siwuhĕn mulati ŋ kusuma,
tan hana sambatĕn iŋ manaṅis i tĕka niŋ gĕrĕḥ aṅlawadi,

wwaŋ syapa tâŋ umaṅöt i hudan iŋ adamaṙ kilat iŋ śayana*

rakwa ṅamöṙ amĕkul masalit araras aṅlihaṅi wwaŋ arūm*

nahan wuwus niŋ paricārikâṅucap,
ḍatĕŋ tikaŋ rātri tĕlas ḍawuḥ wwalu,

Atuntunan mwaŋ nrĕpaputra riŋ hawan,
kepwan ri denya n tumamā mareŋ dalĕm,
Apan kulĕm kori tĕlas manaṅkĕbi*

tilottamârĕs kumĕtĕg tikaŋ hati,
Akweḥ tikā saṅśaya niŋ swacittaka,
Antĕn t-alampaḥ kita saprahāra ri,
humantya reḥ niŋ tumamā mare dalĕm*

kaŧañcanêkîña niraŋ suputrikā,

Akweḥ tikaŋ guṇḍik arūm paḍâṅigĕl,
ya hetu niŋ kori humĕṅha sakṣaṇa*

riŋ śūnya kāliḥ dumunuŋ ri paṅhapit*

nā liŋnya luṅhā malipiṙ matūt ahöb*

dewī sira ndaḥ kahatuṙ sĕḍĕŋ suꝁa,

wilāśa niŋ citta kinubđa de nira,
śokâṅaraŋ tan katĕṅĕṙ tikaŋ lara,
Anūkṣma rāgânilib ambĕk iŋ rimaŋ,
muṅgwi twas aṅhiŋ dadi đaṙmmadewa ya*

jātismarā janma nirêka ṅūny-awās,
saraśmi niŋ swāmi kacitta de nira,
lulwī sirê twas cala riŋ kisapwana,
yateka kāṅĕn katutuṙ nirê kakuŋ*

maṅke pwa yan tan hana konĕŋ iŋ liriŋ,

na hetu niŋ hewa tumiṅhalêŋ śaśi*

haywêka deniŋ manaṅis hĕnĕŋ tuhan,
Āpan kapaṅgiḥ dadi đaṙmmadewa ya*

maṅjanma ri śrī naranāŧa keśawa,

saŋ sāmba sajñā nira kaprakāśita,
raras nirâṅde raras iŋ twas iŋ mulat*

kunĕŋ pratiṅkaḥ naranāŧa keśawa,

rumakṣa sakweḥ nira saŋ mahārĕṣi,
Anwam wruhâkīṙtti widagđa śaktimān*

Āḥ kaka haywa kĕdö mirĕsĕpakĕn apet siḥ aminta kasiḥ,
tan wuruŋ aṅlawanê hati marika wuwusta rĕsĕp ri hati,

mojaṙ saŋ nrĕpaputra tiṅhal i kakanta rari baraŋ aṅölakĕn lara,
saŋsāra ṅwaŋ akūŋ kĕna priḥ i wajanta sinawawa ni raśmi niŋ guyu,
māṙ mrāt twasku kanin tĕñuḥ katikĕlan halis ibu tuluṅĕn pwa taṅhulun,
ṅhiŋ jampyaṅkw-i susunta lūŋ ni luṅayanta bĕbĕda ni kakanta riŋ tilam*

dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa winimba kūŋ piniturun saŋ awak iŋ alaṅö linaṅwakĕn,
rūpantêŋ mađu piṇḍa lindi ni matanta kadi juruḥ atuṙ gula drawa,
sotan tā dadi niŋ raras hati rarasta mapamulu ṭikā haneŋ puḍak,
sākṣāt sāri ni sāri niŋ kusuma māsku n ariris iŋ awaṙṇna ṣaṭpada*

Antĕnkw-âṅĕn-aṅĕn katĕmwan i kakanta rasana ri sĕḍĕṅku dewatā,
rakryañ citraraŧātmajâtuha ri putra lĕṅĕŋ anarukêŋ himālaya,
Aṅkat hyaŋ mađusūdanâṅdadi tumūt aku ri sira tatan waraḥ kita,
hīṅan hyaŋ wiđi kapwa hetu ni kakanta rari layat atiṅgal iŋ tilam*

maṅke prāpta kakanta deniŋ utusan sahaja mara humundaṅê ṅhulun,
wwantĕnkw-îki manĕmwa haṙṣa sahasa n sinalaḥ-asa manaḥku tan liniŋ,

rakryan piṇḍahi tâku hetu niŋ aminta kalukunĕn i luḥta riŋ pipi*

doṣaṅkw-î kita ṅūni maṙmma riraŋ iŋ gati ri kita rikāna riŋ jinĕm,
sāmpun siŋ sapanigrahanta ri manĕḥta yadin apusananta riŋ lulut,
mwaŋ yan kūŋ tuwi milwa kūṅku saꝑala n palu-palu turidanta ri ṅhulun,
denyâṅisyani rāgahaṙṣa ya wilaŋ damĕl ibu lawas i ṅwaŋ iŋ paran*

rakryan sanmatanĕn kakanta rari tapwa hiniwagan unĕŋnya yaṇ ḍatĕŋ,
wehĕnta n rĕsĕpâmbĕkanta tuhun aṅlawanana kita tiṅhal i ṅhulun,
sāmpun wruḥ ṅwaŋ i saṅśayanta riŋ apâku tan asiha manuṅgalê kita,
maṙmmâniṅgala riŋ laṅö ṅwaŋ iriya n malalis amĕkasêŋ karaŋ liman*

saŋ hyaŋ niŋ kalaṅön lihat rari riŋ aṅhyaŋ amalaku kakuŋ hanê kita,
pūjaṅkw-î sari sāri muṅgwi gĕluṅanta saha sĕkaṙ urā haneŋ tilam,
mwaŋ sambatkw-i paṅastawaṅku hiḍĕpĕnku wacana niŋ akūŋ mapet asiḥ,
rakryan toḥ t-aṅanugrahêka ri kakanta suṅakĕna pininta ni ṅhulun*

ñĕṙ citta nrĕpaputrikā winuwusan rĕṅu-rĕṅu nira tan tĕkê hati,
tuhw-âlūŋ siḥ irâmĕlas-harĕp aron turida siniram iŋ karāsikan,
mampĕḥ rakwa kĕtĕṙ nirâṅdadi lulut sumalaḥ i sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
maṙmmā niŋ hyun alūŋ ya leśya nira yan paṅuwahi panulak nirêŋ jaja*

siṅhit-siṅhit irê hatîki winĕḍaṙ nira liŋ ira ri saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
wruḥ ṅwaŋ ry-ambĕkan iŋ priyambada mĕne pwa puput ika kuraŋ-kuraŋ wĕlas,
nāntĕn ndī wĕnaṅa ŋ sĕkaṙ muwaha riŋ ƀramara makalisêŋ hrĕbuk miṅiŋ,
ndā maṅkâku yadin katiṅgala sumantĕn anĕsĕla śarīra ni ṅhulun*

maṅke kapwa tĕṅaḥ niŋ aṅlalisi raśmi sĕḍĕŋ iŋ anaḍaḥ siḥ iŋ sĕnĕŋ,
wruḥ pwânāntwa sinanmatêki dadi niŋ sinaṅi-saṅi sinewakêŋ hiḍĕp,
lwiṙ tan sot rika yan kĕdö rawi ꝑalanya riŋ asuji hinundaŋ iŋ lulut,
ṅhiŋ maṅke suꝁa mātya ƀukti pamĕkas kalara niŋ alaṅö kināryakĕn*

Om antĕnku sadenta mojaṙ-ujaṙ aṅlarani hati kakanta tan wiwal,
sāmpun wruḥ ṅwaŋ i suṅsut iŋ kadi kitâhayu manupura rājasêŋ rimaŋ,
yadyastun śapaŧāna ta ṅwaŋ ari denta saꝑala karĕṅö tikaŋ wuwus,
Āpan tan hana śabda niŋ jalada maṅgĕsĕṅana ri kapö niŋ aṅrĕṅö*

ndi n taŋ cātaka nāgatêŋ riris ikaŋ jalada rari sĕḍĕŋnya n aṅlayaŋ,
lāwan ndi n salagâwĕdîŋ riris i meḥnya sumĕkara kagĕntĕran gĕrĕḥ,
maṅkâku n sinaranta kāsihan apan rinirisan aṅusiṙ kitêŋ jinĕm,
haṙṣâsoṅa karāsikan ṅwaŋ aharĕp riŋ amanis ahudan-hudan mađu*

maṅkin trāsa manaḥku de ni panaḥ iŋ madana mamanasi twas i ṅhulun,
yekā n śīṙṇna manaḥku denya kakĕnan lara turida ni rāga niŋ smara,
maṅke pwêki kahaṙṣa ni ṅwaŋ i kitêbu kita madĕha kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
Aṅhiŋ tamba kanin tapiḥ saput ulĕs palakun i kita haywa t-âtĕṅĕt*

wruḥ riŋ ceṣṭa tilottamā n mijil aleśya n aṅĕyĕha wawaŋ tĕkêŋ natar,
tan señjuḥ rasikā kinon maluy alĕs lumaris apituli n pamet sahur,
saŋ sinwī kawĕkas wiraṅwaŋ aṅĕsaḥ prihati linukaran tapiḥ nira,
miṅsĕṙ-miṅsĕṙ aḍuḥ wuwus nira kinewala kaparĕpĕkan tinītihan*

dewī yajñawatī karāgaƀaya riŋ śayana kahilaṅan raras hati,

Aṅasut aṅĕmbul iŋ śara sahâśwa-gajapati marampak atri gumuruḥ*

panaḥ ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja lawan bala nira mĕtu riŋ payudđan asusun,
mijil asuluŋ-suluŋ panaḥ ikaŋ prawala sahaja kīṙṇna sök winulatan,
kumusuḥ abāyubajra tumulak warayaŋ iŋ asurêŋ naƀastala katūt,

<sragđarā>:30.

kālanya n tan katon lwiṙ nikaŋ asurabalâtyanta śabdanya ǥora,

tĕlas abaṅun ta saŋ prawaraputrikâṅĕsaḥ alök,

<Indrabajra>:37.

saŋ śrī narāṙyyâta pacĕḥ kapūhan,
de saŋ suputrâlara rāga māśa,
nāhan tikā hetu nira n patakwan,
ṅkā liŋ nira n tiṅhali dārukîkā*

norâṅgarit riŋ musuḥ aṅgakāra,
luṅhā lumiṅsiṙ tinĕkān paḍârĕs*

Ꜽrāwaṇā wāhana saŋ hyaŋ indra,
mātaṅga śūrêŋ raṇa lāgi-lāgi,
maṅke n lagī wāhana saŋ mahīja,
tan sāra ta n pānulalay rikêŋ praŋ*

bajrâđikārāstra nirêŋ mahendra,
Atyanta riŋ kās kadi hīrabajra,
moǥêka māpĕs maṅĕne mahīja,
leśyanya n unduṙ ya wajanya tĕmpak*

hyaŋ śakra sakrođa ri saŋ mahīja,

sewu mata wyaṙŧa pĕtĕŋ panonya*

prodƀūta mumbul saha đūmaketu,
kapwâṅasut saŋ kṣitijêŋ raṇāṅga,
heman paḍĕm swaŋ kabalik tinisnya*

maṅkā sira hyaŋ yama kaṙwwa ḍaṇḍa,
madwandwa lāwan kṣitijâṅadu kral,
saŋ hyaŋ yamâḍaṇḍa ri ƀūmiputra,
ṅkā ŋ ḍaṇḍa wiƀrāmya katon kawaṅsul*

saŋ hyaŋ nirity-âtahĕn iŋ kamantyan,

pakṣâkral aṅhalwakĕnêŋ mahīja,
wahw-âṅayat yaṙ kabalik ginantaŋ*

sotan sira hyaŋ baruṇâlaḥ aṅrĕs,

papraŋ nirâṅdoḥ milu komba-kombul,
Asriŋ surud toḥ nira riŋ raṇāṅga*

hyaŋ bāyu mādrĕs paṅusiṙ nirêŋ praŋ,

kedĕṙ tĕkê saŋ kṣitiputra đꜽṙyya,

saŋ hyaŋ kuwerâtakut aṙdđa kepwan,

yogāđipêśāna suđīrabudđi,

riŋ swaṙgga sakweḥ para dewatâwrĕg,

sinraŋ sirâpan sira dewarāja*

siḥ saŋ narendrâtiśaya n hineṙ-her,

Aṅhiŋ praƀāwa praƀu yêka tan len,
tambā ni lajjā nira saŋ hyaŋ indra*

nāhan wacana nira saŋ apsarendra ri narendra saha wulat arūm,
cĕb ṅöṙ twas ira narapati ṇ ḍĕṅö sapawaraḥ surasaciwapati,

tan saṅśaya palarĕn i kāya-kāya ni sakāṙyya nira surapati*

ndā mantuka ta rahadi saṅhulun ṅhulun ike wĕkasa nikaŋ ulaḥ,

himpĕṙ kali haliwat i lambuŋ iŋ wukiṙ ujaṙnya titiṙ aṅarape*

hopĕñ juga wacana patik hajî hatuṙ i jöŋ narapati Uniṅan,

wwantĕn kawĕka-wĕkas ikā ri mađya milu śīṙṇna kadi kayu tinor*

mwaŋ kāśrayan ira winiśeṣa yâṣṭaguṇa saŋ praƀu ṅaran ikahĕn*

hĕnti pwa ya kagĕsĕṅana ŋ sarāt mapa tikā hamĕṅan ika pĕjaḥ*

Ajñā nira ya juga linaṅǥanan pisaniṅūn pwa ṅawaśakĕna rāt,

sāmpun pwa sira bara wirođa meman iŋ upāya kahilaṅan ira*

Āpan ƀaya katĕkana wiǥna kāṙyya nrĕpati pwa wawaŋ awawahan*

Iti maṅkanâta pawaraḥ saŋ udđawa,
ri siraŋ nareśwara wawaŋ sira n sahur,
tuhu tan kasaṅśayakĕnanta maṅkata,
Ika saŋ watĕk yadu sayogya maṅkata*

niśaṫôlmukâdi nikanaŋ lumampaha,
kalawan ta satyaka si sāmba śāraṇa,
Irikaŋ tigaŋ wĕṅi wĕkas ya maṅkata,
saha kośa wāhana padāti saṅgĕpan*

ri tĕlas narendra maṅutus lumampaha,
Umuliḥ sirêŋ pura huwus tĕkê dalĕm,
para taṇḍa rakryan umuliḥ sakeŋ saƀā,
ṅuniweḥ watĕk ratu kabeḥ samāṅjuru*

sira saŋ sĕḍĕŋ winiđi maṅkatâlaga,
paḍa gaṙjjitâharĕp akīṙttya riŋ musuḥ,
tuhu wīra satyaka suđīra riŋ raṇa,
kadi siṅha niṙƀaya muliḥ sakeŋ saƀā*

I ḍatĕŋ nirêŋ kuwu nira n kasowaṅan,
Inatag tikaŋ kawula tan hanâkalib,
juru-jurw-adandan ahutaŋ-hutaŋ waneḥ,
Ikanaŋ turuŋ mĕtu dĕmaknya kemĕṅan*

prajurit paṅaṅkat ikahĕn yaŧākrama,
tumatiŋ sinaṇḍaŋ anumāna niŋ wani,
ri tĕlas nikânarima saṅka riŋ tuhan,
wijaḥ asramêŋ lĕbuḥ aganti tan pĕgat*

Ikanaŋ barat wahu ḍatĕŋ sakeŋ ḍusun,
mahiwaŋ sramanya palayū nikā baṅĕt,
Aṅalap tareki milu piŋ pitûmidĕr,
Aṅĕliḥ mutaḥ tahi kaṅelan aṅdĕlĕg*

hana têki wāhu tinibān rawis hañar,
rinuwit ḍaḍap nika pinañjĕṙ iŋ natar,
Inalap nikā raṅin ikâsramêŋ lĕbuḥ,
Agiraŋ paḍâḍara-ḍaran tiniṅhalan*

hana ton rikêpu yan amiṅrwakĕn dadar,
pinutiḥ ri piṅgiṙ i ḍaḍap nikâlĕsĕḥ,
Alĕmĕḥ mamañjĕra mamĕṇḍĕm iŋ grĕha,
Amupuḥ rabinya sahasâgawe pirak*

wwaya len tĕkâṅhyaŋ amalakwa pīguṇa,
Awanĕḥ tikaŋ caṭaka liŋnya riŋ tĕgal,
hana takwa ko liŋ i tuhanya maṅkana,
karaṇanya yan miṅay adoḥ wulat nikā*

nda tatīta kāla katĕkan tigaŋ wĕṅi,
sira saŋ kinon tĕlas adan lumampaha,
bala kośa wāhana tĕlas gĕnĕp kabeḥ,
huwus amwit iŋ nrĕpati len halāyuđa*

lumaris tikaŋ raŧa marampak iŋ lĕbuḥ,
gaja-wāhanāśwapati pādarakṣaka,
gumuruḥ tikaŋ paḍahi-śaṅꝁa-kālaha,
kumĕtug prakampita tikaŋ mahītala*

tumibā tikaŋ riris awoṙ haṅin mirir,
maṅadĕg kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ ikaŋ laṅit rĕmĕŋ,
wihagâhajöŋ swara nikaŋ manuk lĕṅöŋ,
śuƀamaṅgalê laku niraŋ watĕk yadu*

Ucapĕn tikaŋ paṅuṅaṅan saŋ apraṅa,
ry-ulihanya waspa niŋ arūm kĕnêŋ unĕŋ,
Ajuruḥ manis ni liriŋ iŋ matâmanis,
paran iŋ marâgul-agul aṅdyahî rimaŋ*

laraṅan tĕkāsiḥ asusuk-susuk hañar,
saliwaḥ wajanya mapupuk-pupuk hijo,
Anilib pamaṇḍĕm ika riŋ matâmanis,
wiꝑalâwawaṙ gaḍuŋ aṅanti riŋ gĕluŋ*

wuri niŋ kurĕn tadinan iŋ mahas maṅö,
Asadak putiḥ kadi tanaḥ ny-aniṅkahi,
lĕpit iŋ tapiḥ satakis iŋ karas hañar,
Anawaŋ palambaŋ inusap tiniṅhalan*

hana tâwaṅun dinugan iŋ hulat maliŋ,
kawĕnaŋ lulutnya pinuluṇḍas iŋ mata,
prihatin tikā kahilaṅan manaḥ rimaŋ,
Aṅĕsaḥ tumiṅhal i wĕkas Ikaŋ hati*

waratâṅure sahaja yâṅurā manaḥ,
Inajumnya teki gĕluṅanya sök sĕkar,
Irika n katon takĕlĕkanya maṅrawuk,
lĕwu yan kameraṅĕn umuṅkuṙ aṅdadak*

sira saŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ tĕlas lĕpas,
kadi wāḥ katonan ika yan tĕkêŋ tĕgal,
gumuruḥ tikaŋ bala paḍâtiǥūṙṇnita,
kadi śabda niŋ bañu tumampuḥ iŋ juraŋ*

palapat lĕṅöŋ tĕgal alok tikaŋ hawan,
kali luṅka-luṅka rawa saṇḍiŋ iŋ nadī,
tumurun sumĕṅka lari niŋ raŧâgĕlis,
Aduluṙ lawan pawana tan karâṅiriŋ*

kalalu pwa lampaḥ ira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
maṅawe tan adrĕs ahawan gĕgĕṙ-gĕgĕr,
huni niŋ mrĕdaṅga nira rāmya tan pĕgat,
yan abaṇḍuṅan gĕrĕḥ awoṙ awaṅsulan*

hana ta lwaḥ uttama bañunya niṙmmala,
I tĕpinya rāmya paran iŋ kĕnêŋ unĕŋ,
kalakānya rantunan iŋ adyus iŋ gĕgĕr,
galagaḥnya mĕmbaŋ anamaṙ gĕluŋ huwan*

ri pĕluk-pĕluknya hana raṅraṅan katon,
paran iŋ maniṅtiŋ aṅariŋ warĕg Uraŋ,
ri tĕpinya taŋ taratay âtatā katon,
waliwis hanêriya mahâṅisis hĕlar*

para rājaputra haliwat sakeŋ nadī,
giripāṙśśwa kīṙṇna kahawan tĕkap nira,
riŋ aƀīruŧāni kahalintaṅan huwus,
ri tĕlasnya wiṣṭi ya paṅĕntal-ĕntalan*

Iŋ marustanī tĕgal adoḥ kuraŋ bañu,
ya ta kāmbaḥ awyaŋ ikanaŋ dukut lĕpas,
kumukus lĕbūnya dumudug tĕkêŋ laṅit,
kadi tâṅusiṙ bañu mareŋ payođara*

I kurapradeśa kahawan kaŧañcana,
hana jahnawī lwaḥ ika saṅka riŋ laṅit,
śuci niṙmmalâtiśaya tis nikâdalĕm,
Alaṅö tĕpinya hibĕkan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ*

sira saŋ watĕk yadu sahaṙṣa lālana,
kalaṅön linolyan i saganđa niŋ sĕkar,
suꝁa de ni hīs ni sirat iŋ  ṙyyak ombakan,
sahajâmrĕtârasana tis nikaŋ haṅin*

tumurun matīṙŧa sira saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
lara ṅel ṅĕliḥ nira hilaŋ samāntara,
pariśudđa citta nira niṙmmalâbuṅaḥ,
pinakaswaƀāwa saŋ atīṙŧa riŋ śuci*

ri tĕlas nirâdyus irikâlaris muwaḥ,
Irikaŋ halas ri tĕpi niŋ mahānadī,
makiris tikaŋ tahĕn arok lawan latā,
lwiṙ awāhwa-wāhwan ulaḥ an siliḥ-kayuḥ*

mrak i tuṅgak iŋ kayu manis manuṅgilis,
Alaṅö tĕkap ni kĕlab iŋ đwajâkilat,
maṅigĕl ḍĕṅö paḍahi saŋ watĕk yadu,
wĕkasan manawwaŋ irikā lwiṙ ambahan*

tumayuŋ tikaŋ liraŋ i piṅgiṙ iŋ juraŋ,
mabĕbĕd gaḍuŋ kapaṅĕliḥ tiniṅhalan,
Apuji n pĕtuŋ yaya pinaṇḍi riŋ halas,
kadi tan wruhĕn rahayu kabwatan raras*

maṅunĕŋ wuṅū ta n alayū nya kāsihan,
hanamun kabeḥnya paḍa tan hanâsĕkar,
I karinya ṅūni n inatīta niŋ laṅö,
karaṇanya hewa mari tâsuhun sĕkar*

ry-uttarakośalêki kahawan tĕkap yadukula,
rāmya nikâpitowi saha ƀāwaƀoga sulaƀā,
wwaŋ nika daṙśśanīya paḍa sahya suśrama katon,

mwaŋ ri sawaḥnya rāmya mahijo bañunya tan arĕn,

wwaŋ ri waruŋ-waruŋnya maṅiduŋ makaṅsi kukulan,

nista nikā n wiśīṙṇna yan inambaḥ iŋ kuda liman*

Asru tikaŋ lĕbū mĕtu tinūb nikaŋ haliwawar*

sambat ikânaṅis lawan anaknya māsiḥ-asihan*

Aṅgĕḥ ikaŋ balâkĕmit i rājya saŋ kṣitisuta,

sĕḍĕŋ mawurahan tikaŋ yadubala,

wwantĕn dꜽtya murâpatiḥ atuha,
yekâsĕṅhit i saŋ nrĕpatanaya,
raṇḍêkā n tanayanya mapuliha,
Atyanta prakaṭanya katatakut*

mattâgöŋ pwa gajanya kadi gunuŋ,
mwaŋ rĕṅganya suwaṙṇna maṇimaya,
śabdanyâṅrĕguŋ iŋ gagana pĕnuḥ,
Aṅgyat riŋ yaduyođa sĕḍĕŋ amūk*

maṅsö saŋ mura gutgutĕn abutĕŋ,
mwaŋ putranya kabeḥnya sama rĕbaḥ,
wadwanyâtiśayêŋ kagiri-giri,
sewu kweḥnya wiśeṣa paḍa wani*

kontā tomara śūla nika lĕpas,
len taŋ sañjata tulya hudan apuy,
wadwā saŋ yadu duṙbala kakĕnan,
māty-âbāp pinupuḥ ya pinanasan*

konduṙ kolahala ŋ yadubala sök,
śīṙṇnâsiŋ kari māti  kinurubut,
hetunya n malayū layat aluyuk,
deniŋ dꜽtya sakeŋ gagana magöŋ*

maṅkin taŋ muraputra sahasikā,
muṅsiṙ saŋ niśaṫā mura saparĕŋ,
muṅgwiŋ hematalâsurak aṅuhuḥ,
śūlanyâkas agöŋ paḍa lumĕpas*

yeka n yatna siraŋ niśaṫa puliḥ,
hrū tīkṣṇāgra murub linĕpasakĕn,
lāwan hrū niraŋ ulmuka kumukus,
đwasta ŋ śūla tikĕl kĕna tinuju*

krođêkaŋ muraputra ri niśaṫa,
kapwânambuti pāśa nika masö,
yeka n sep tinugĕl tali nikahĕn,
kānin kapwa gulūnya kĕna panaḥ*

wwaŋ sānaknya waneḥ sĕḍĕŋ apuliḥ,
đīrâsĕṅhit i saŋ niśaṫa kabeḥ,
makrak sāhasa kapwa mawa tĕwĕk,
pakṣanyôliha kaṙṣanatanaya*

Ambĕknyâpraṅa moǥa rinuhunan,
bāhunyê tĕṅĕnan pĕgat apasaḥ,
Anyāt dꜽtya tugĕl ri wĕtĕŋ ikā,
deniŋ hrū niraŋ ulmuka tan arĕn*

hĕntîkaŋ hana riŋ kṣiti pinanaḥ,
de saŋ satyaka sāmba sira n amūk,
wadwā niŋ mura śīṙṇna mati matap,
syuḥ mwaŋ wāhana riŋ raṇa magĕlar*

tandaŋ niŋ mura riŋ nrĕpatanaya,
göŋ krođanya mĕlĕg ri liman ikā,
Ambĕknyôliha saŋ nrĕpatisuta,
pāśāstranya ya tâkilat awilĕt*

paṅheṙ koŋ rĕbi liŋnya wahu mayat,
sep tĕṅgĕknya cinakra kapisanan,
mātaṅganya punaḥ ya kinurubut,
pat pādanya pĕgat kĕna pinanaḥ*

māti pwa ŋ mura māwrĕg asasaran,
ṅkā taŋ dꜽtyabalâwĕdi malayū,
māwrī taŋ hana riŋ gaganatala,
luṅhâmet parananya lĕṅit adoḥ*

kālanyâlaḥ ikāŋ asura murud,
paṅheṙ liŋnya nĕhĕṙ milu malayū,
ṅkā hrūnyêka tibā tan inulatan,
Akweḥ dꜽtya jurunya mati kĕna*

konduṙ mūṙ aṅusiṙ kuṭa ya tinūt,
len ṅĕs-ṅösĕn amet lĕkas apuliḥ,
ndātan sāra kĕnêŋ panaḥ akĕdal,
luṅhârĕs ya kabeḥ layat alayū*

Awrĕg taŋ sakuṭâwurahan awū,
towin ṅ-ānala yênapuy umurub,
muntab kadƀuta tulya gunuŋ apuy,
lumrā ŋ đūma sawaŋ tahĕn aṅadĕg*

sāmpun śīṙṇna tikaŋ kuṭa katunu,
Akweḥ strī kabĕnĕm saha tanaya,
kanyâkweḥ katawan hana dinudut,
kasyāsiḥ kumĕtĕṙ tĕhĕṙ anaṅis*

yan bwat saŋ yadu tan hana manawan,
yāwat strī laraṅan hinaliwatan,
Āpan tulya bibîka hiḍĕp ikā,
göŋ-göṅĕn ri kasāđun ira juga*

Āsiŋ drĕwya haneŋ pura niyata,
mās ratnādi tĕlas larut inalap,
wadwā saŋ yaduwīra paḍa sarat,
de niŋ kweḥnya tikaŋ jara-jarahan*

wwantĕn tânĕmu puṇḍutan agiraŋ,
pindĕk wiṅkiṙ isinya kacaŋ irĕŋ,
maṙmmanya n rinubuŋ ginuyu-guyu,
yā liŋnya n sinurak malĕs anurak*

saŋ nāŧātmaja sāmba sira ḍatĕŋ,
mwaŋ wadwā nira sāyuđa maṅiriŋ,
riŋ kanyāƀawanêki paran ira,
Agyā yan mulatê ŋ nrĕpaduhitā*

prāptêŋ jro nagarī nrĕpatanaya,
tan wwantĕn sira saŋ nrĕpaduhitā,
kepwan teka manaḥ nira kumĕtĕr,
de niŋ siḥ marikā bara tinahā*

ṅkānêŋ raṅkaŋ ĕmās ta paran ira,
Uṅgwan yajñawatîka lagi-lagi,
moǥa pwa n taya saŋ nrĕpaduhitā,
yâṅde saṅśaya saŋ nrĕpatanaya*

nāhan liŋ nira yan panaha-nahā,
yan mātyêki sirêkana kalalaḥ,
nyāma nyêka katĕmwa śawa nira,
ṅke riŋ ratnapalaṅka rurubana*

yadyastun rasikā wruha ri wuwus,
byaktânuṅsuṅa liṅku tan asuwe,
maṅke tan hana têkihĕn awaraḥ,
hetuṅkwâpĕga tan wruḥ iŋ ulaha*

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ nrĕpatanaya,
prāptā puṣpawatī manuduhakĕn,
ry-uṅgwan yajñawatī yan asusupan,
saŋ sāmbêka sirâgiraŋ umara*

ṅkā saŋ yajñawatī katĕmu lume,
muṅgwiŋ paṅkwan iraŋ surawanitā,
śokâśā humiḍĕp nrĕpatanaya,
heṙ-herĕn mrĕmakĕn ri lara nira*

śīǥrâṅliŋ tika saŋ suraduhitā,
haṙṣânantwa ri saŋ nrĕpatisuta,
śabdâwoṙ panaṅisnya ya ta giraŋ,
kagyat yajñawatī wawaŋ amĕkul*

luḥ saŋ yajñawatī tĕhĕṙ umilī,
kadyâswāgata riŋ nrĕpatanaya,
wruḥ saŋ sāmba mamakpak aṅusapi,
maṙmmâhĕmban i saŋ nrĕpaduhitā*

sāmpun yajñawatī sira hinalap,
Akweḥ ceṭi tumūt milu katawan,
Agyā mantuka sāmba tĕka ri heŋ,
ndan ri swaṙgga paran suraduhitā*

mantuk saŋ yadu śīǥra tan akaḍat,
sakweḥ niŋ bala tuṣṭa wija-wijaḥ,
ramyâtūt suku niŋ wukiṙ alaṅö,
piṅgiṙ niŋ pasiṙ aṙjja linihatan*

kāry-âdoḥ tikanaŋ pura wĕkasan,
tapwan māri kukusnya winulatan,
lwiṙ hyaŋ niŋ nagarâṅadĕg aṅure,
śokâśâkilayū ri yadukula*

poṙyyaŋ garyaŋ araŋ kayunya wilutan pilaŋ anakan arok lawan kutu-kutu,
śuṣkâdoḥ bañu tūt hawanya karikil gumaway i lĕsu niŋ watĕk yadubala,

söŋ-söŋ haṙṣa nirê saŋ adyaḥ ira tan winawa-wawa nirâhañaŋ sĕḍĕŋ arūm*

ṅkānê saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ gunuŋ ri magađêki kahawan atiduṙgga-duṙgga maƀaya,
ꝁyātîŋ rāt jarasanđa saŋ praƀu rikā musuḥ ira naranāŧa krĕṣṇa malawas,

hetunyân ajĕjĕṙ ta lampaḥ ikanaŋ bala kaṅĕlihan epu luhya wĕkasan,
maṅlampw-âṅadipīra maṅrĕrĕba ta ṅwaŋ ujaṙ ika paḍâṅucap makulĕma*

byatīta māmrĕm yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,

sakrođa takwêŋ yadu-wrĕṣṇiwīra,

Atyanta riŋ lāǥawa suśramêŋ praŋ*

Anĕmwakĕñ cora lumampaḥ iŋ kulĕm,
Ikaŋ maliŋ sāhasikâṅduk aṅgalaḥ,
sĕnĕŋ ranak hyaŋ kaki wāni maṅlawan*

ṅhulun manumpĕt manusup mareŋ sukĕt,
nimitta niŋ tan kĕna de nikaŋ maliŋ,
kĕna pwa ta swāmi ranak mahāyati,
ya hetu niŋ duṣṭa muliḥ paḍâdulur*

mijil ranak hyaŋ kaki saṅka riŋ sukĕt,
rikā n kapaṅgiḥ priya ni ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,
tibā ni luḥ ni ṅhulun aṅdyusi ŋ sĕnĕŋ,
ya hetu niŋ somya kĕcap matâṅdĕlö*

nahan ta liśya nrĕpaputrikâwaraḥ,
mahaṙṣy-amakpak sira maṅrĕṅö wuwus,
Uḍūḥ katuhwan kawĕlas-harĕp dahat,
kitêbu lāwan priya maṅrĕsî hati*

na śabda saŋ paṇḍita māṙ manaḥ nira,
tĕhĕṙ sirâṅdyus ri siraŋ nrĕpātmaja,
saha prayogâmrĕta jīwarakṣaṇa,
nĕhĕṙ minantran sŧiti de mahāyati*

tĕlas narendrātmaja dinyus aṅlilir,
Aminta toyâpan asat gulū nira,
wineḥ i ron iŋ tĕmu de suputrikā,
Umaṅkin enak wĕkasan manaḥ nira*

<wiśwalalita>:48.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

nrĕpaduhitâgiraŋ sira ri paṅliliṙ nrĕpasuta,
maṅupaśamê mahāṙṣi pukulun tasön kasihana,
yaśana ranak mahāyati n awānđawêrikaŋ alas,

Aharĕp amaṙṣuꝁâṅinakanê manaḥ saŋ ahayu*

ri tĕlas irâbaṅun mulat anāntwa riŋ rĕṣiwara,

taṅheḥ yañ caritan lawas nira piraŋ kulĕm sira huwus,
tambâsiŋ tamatan hanâmarasi roga saŋ katanĕhan,
rūm saŋ yajñawatī jugâṅinaki citta saŋ nrĕpasuta,
tambiṙyyan haṅĕt iŋ payođara haṅöt-aṅöt nira n atis*

Eñjiŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra yaṙ warahakĕn taŋ ipyan ahayu,
ṅkānê yajñawatī huwus nira maśoca liŋ nira nihan,
rakryan rakwa tinonku mabrata mawastra piṅhay amawar,
ṅwaŋ rakwêki hane samīpa niy ariṅku tansaḥ aparĕk*

ndā ṅkānê pasaƀān pwa yajña nira saŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabeḥ,
saŋ hyaŋ bahni murub ywa rakwa sira tan pađūma maṅadĕg,

ndîka saŋ niśaŧâhurip kari saŋ ulmuka ndi kawĕkas,
mwaŋ saŋ satyaka śāraṇa pwa hamĕṅān irêkana kabeḥ,
mwaŋ hetunta hurip tĕkap nikanaŋ aṅrĕwĕk waraḥ aku*

nāhan takwan i saŋ nrĕpātmaja si dāruki wruḥ asahur,
sojaṙ saŋ naranāŧaputra bapa śāśwatā sira kabeḥ,
Āpan tan hana śīṙṇna saŋ niśaṫa satyakâhayu sira,

lwiṙ guntuṙ mapagut matampuḥ i tĕṅaḥ tikaŋ gajapati*

paṅhrūk niŋ wani len paṅohan ikanaŋ sĕḍĕŋ kakuwuṅan,

makweḥ taŋ lwaŋ ikaŋ musuḥ pinĕgatan winūk tinĕṅahan*

wwantĕn tânak iraŋ narendra magađādināŧa kawĕnaŋ,
ꝁyātîŋ rāt maṅaran pratīpa kasikĕp binanđan atĕhĕr,

nāhan liŋnya si dārukî sira narendraputra winaraḥ,

nrĕpati krĕṣṇa sirêka kāraṇa*

pamatĕknya hanak nikaŋ durātmā,
tumuluy pwâniru duṣṭa niŋ bapa,
tuwi niṣkaraṇêkihĕn galaknya,
Awamānêŋ atuhâtĕhĕṙ mada*

ndan ikā ri hatinya rakwa nūta,
Irikaŋ ƀoma mataŋnya sāhasa,
kunaŋ āpan akās jugâmbĕk i ṅwaŋ,
tuwi tāde pĕjahêŋ raṇāṅgana*

ri katiṅhalan i ṅhulun mahâkās,
yatikā hetu nikâminaŋ ratu,
saha nuṅgalakĕn manaḥ samitra,
hanawuŋ tuṅgal ikā ya ri ṅhulun*

lwiṙ ikaŋ ratu pat sa-ƀomapakṣa,
si jarāsanđa si cedi duṙjana,
mwaŋ awaṅgapati prasidđa duṣṭa,
ya si śatruntapa nīca kaśmala*

yatikā paḍa ƀakti riŋ mahīja,
sapakon saŋ narakêka tan wihaŋ,
Inalapnya ta kośa ni ṅhulun ya,
tĕka niŋ rājya kapunpunan kabeḥ*

yatikā praƀu hetu niŋ mara ṅke,
Umusiṙ siḥ praƀu wīrarakṣaka,
karaṇā naranāŧa keśawêkā,
Umaritrāṇana kāṙyya ni ṅhulun*

nrĕpa bahlika śālya somadatta,
nrĕpa rukma n paḍa pakṣa ni ṅhulun,
Ikanaŋ milu riŋ musuḥ ya makweḥ,
tan ikâṅdeya wikalpa saŋ praƀu*

nrĕpa pāṇḍawa korawêka tan tūt,
widurôhut ri siraŋ yuđiṣṫira,
tuwi ƀīṣma sirâwaraḥ rikaŋ de,
ri siraŋ hastinarāja taṙ wihaŋ*

nrĕpaputra đanañjaya pwa tuṅgal,
kalawan śrī harimūṙtti ƀūpati,
niyatêka tumūt ri saŋ narendra,
tuwi yan mantu tĕkap nareśwara*

ndan ikā pamiśeṣa saŋ narāṙyya,
nrĕpati krĕṣṇa lawan halāyuđa,
makanaryama budđiy ugrasena,
Irikāŋ sāđya sināđya ni ṅhulun*

sira saŋ baladewa śīǥra mojar,
praƀu tan saṅśaya saŋ nareśwara,
yaduwīra matoha jīwitanya,
sumaraŧyākĕna kāṙyya saŋ praƀu*

sumahuṙ siraŋ ugrasena śīǥra,
ya kĕnoḥ śabda narendra tânaya,
Apan aṅhiŋ i dona niŋ samaṅke,
Umariwrĕtta ri saŋ maṅāśraya*

Aṅucap naranāŧa keśawāṅsa,
pada yuktîka wuwus nareśwara,
yaduwīra saŋ udđawâta mahyun,
ri sapājaṙ naranāŧa tan salaḥ*

ri tĕlasnya n enak apagĕḥ pwa paṅaku nira saŋ watĕk yadu,
nrĕpati druma pwa sira tuṣṭa manaḥ ira sumöŋ mare hati,
Umuliḥ mareŋ kuwu nirâṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn i lĕkas nirâpraṅa,
Inusap nirâwak ira manyus akisut atĕhĕṙ sirâṅgĕtĕm*

I sĕḍĕŋ nira n paḍa suꝁa nrĕpati sahana saŋ watĕk yadu,
ṅuniweḥ narendra harimūṙtti sira tika kagöṅan iŋ suꝁa,
ri ḍatĕŋ narendra haji kimpuruṣapati ri saŋ watĕk yadu,
yatikā prakāśakĕna de nira saꝑala karĕṅwa riŋ musuḥ*

makaleśya ta ŋ mahas acaṅkrama mamarĕkanâŋ ḍusun-ḍusun,
hana paṙwwatêŋ mađura rewataka ṅaran ikā ya lakwana,
Inatag tikaŋ yadu kabeḥ saha tanaya sadāra saṅgĕpan,
tĕka riŋ maƀaṇḍagina kapwa paḍa milu ǥinoṣitan haji*

suꝁa kañcit ambĕk ira saŋ tĕlas inarahakĕn paḍâtihaŋ,
pakaronya wastra binĕbĕd-bĕbĕd inapitan iŋ galaḥ miraḥ,
hana len rinaṇḍi tinulisnya harĕp iŋ arĕjâsawaŋ tinon,
tiga waṙṇna kahyun ika rājasa sinahaja bāŋ lawan putiḥ*

sakatambay eñjiŋ an umaṅkata narapati tan kalūbana,
Adadak tikaŋ wwaŋ i dalĕm nagara wijaḥ akabwatan manis,
yatikā kapantĕsakĕnêŋ sarahi-sarahi n āpti yênapi,
mwaŋ ikaŋ masiñjaṅa katon atulisa ginawe kinasturi*

kahatuṙ wulan kasapuluḥ sĕḍĕŋ i lĕṅĕŋ ikā madūm laṅö,
paḍa tan hanâṅinak-inak sahana-hana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ puri,
raras iŋ lumampaha waneḥ sacinarita nikâmajaŋ wulan,
sama haṙṣa rāmya sawilāśa gati nika saraśmi sasmita*

yatikâṅucap sama samitra gumuṇita sakahyun iŋ hati,
rari yadyapin swan ika tĕmpuhakĕna nira saŋ nareśwara,
Apiliḥ ṅwaŋ iŋ kaharĕp i ṅhulun awĕdi tumiṅhalêŋ maru,
ṅuniwehkw-amaṅgiha kawalwan aku niyata kāwarêŋ prĕman*

rari yan hanêka sira taṇḍa suṅana paranaṅkwa de haji,
Arĕṇaḥ rahadyan i gatinya ta mahuluna denya ri ṅhulun,
wruḥ ikâwayuḥ wruḥ anĕkāni suꝁa tĕhĕṙ aweḥ anaṇḍaṅa,
nda nihañ calanya sanu deṅkw-apiṅit asĕmu tan basêŋ kadaŋ*

lĕṅĕŋ ambĕk i ṅwaŋ amalaṙ turuŋ agati ri jöŋ nareśwara,
raras iŋ sakĕmbaṅa katon anĕku-nĕku kurĕn maṅasyasiḥ,
sahurip sahaṙṣa paḍa rāmya siliḥ-asiḥ anuṅgal iŋ manaḥ,
witade sadenya n ahila ndan ika warĕg akālihan hulĕs*

maluy moliḥ kiṅkiŋ ginuritakĕn iŋ ketaka miṅiŋ*

tiḍak ḍīkötāhui
<krĕti>:62.

hana tânawuŋ turida taṇḍiŋ ika wulaŋ analyani laṅö,
Atajî luṅid ni wacananya rinacanan ikâmukĕt lulut,
Araras makĕmbaṙ i manis niki n inadu hajöŋnya riŋ puḍak,
makatoḥ lĕpiḥ ni lĕpihanya ya mati mapuliḥ karāsikan*

wwaŋ asiḥ masiḥ ri kalaṅön sinalaga ni karaśmi niŋ gati,

suƀaga swatantra ni karasnya huwus ika linādnya riŋ tanaḥ*

tan baribin ta riŋ lagi tinakwanan i wĕkas i citta niŋ rimaŋ,

tan saƀara n katona curawāda mara kita tan intaṙ iŋ karas*

saŋ kadi wimba niŋ sĕmi kalahrun aṅĕliḥ alalâṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,

hyaŋ rati Ambĕk i ṅwaŋ i sira n kita madana mapaṅgihêŋ wukir*

ndan hĕnĕŋ ambwatī hĕnĕṅĕnanta kinalaran apujya tan para,

Aṅhiŋ ikaŋ wilāpa paṅahat-hat iri kita palaṙ pisiṅgihĕn*

Āḥ lĕwu kūṅku de ni pawaraḥta ri gati saŋ inimba riŋ manis,

syuḥ kahilī hatiṅku kawawê tĕṅaḥ iŋ ahayu kāmpiṙ iŋ susu*

kepwan i budđi ni ṅwaŋ aṅiriŋ panarimana riŋ adyaḥ aṅlare,
tan wruḥ i pāmbĕkanya n arusit nĕhĕṙ aṅapusi citta niŋ rimaŋ,

Āpti nikā n hĕnĕŋ kanĕban ambĕk adalihan aṅantyakĕn pariḥ*

tībra kakiṅkiṅan yatika hetu niŋ umarĕk aminta tambana*

maṅkana liŋ nira n ri jaruman saŋ ahayu manilib nĕhĕṙ muliḥ,

wwantĕn strī kinalalwan iŋ jalu maṅanti kajĕjĕpan i haṙṣa niŋ sĕnĕŋ,
