<śāṙddūlawikrīḍta>:73.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

saŋ ƀomâtisaroṣa de ni waraḥ iŋ dꜽtya n wiśīṙṇnêŋ kuṭa,
muntab rakwa panas nikaŋ hati tĕkap saŋ yajñawaty-âhañaŋ,
nāhan hetu nira n muliḥ saka rikaŋ kendran matiṅgal musuḥ,
Agyā n śīǥra tĕkêŋ purī katĕmu taŋ rājyâtunū lwiṙ gunuŋ*

saŋ ƀomâṅucap iŋ mahodara lihat śīṙṇna ŋ kaḍatwan gĕsĕŋ,
de niŋ yādawa wrĕṣṇi nīca paracidranyânĕkāny-ânilib,
duṣṭā krĕṣṇabala pwa yâṅhiwagakĕn tan śāsanêŋ kṣatriya,
sotan taŋ basudewaputra matuhêŋ gowrĕnda ṅūnī n rare*

yan wānya ry-aku kenakanya ri hanaṅku n taṅtaṅanyâpraṅa,
mon yan motusa minta donĕn aku tan dadyâta tan samƀrama,
maṅke pwā paracidra kaśmala nikā tan đaṙmmayudđêŋ musuḥ,
maṅgā tocapĕn iŋ parâmawas ikā ṅūnîrikaŋ yāwana*

maṅke taŋ druma yan paṅuṅsiṙ irikaŋ krĕṣṇâtakut ri ṅhulun,
ƀaktîŋ duṣṭa matiṅgal iŋ sujana đik nindâku riŋ maṅkana,
luṅhâmet pamarāśrayan syapa tatan krođê tĕkapnya n tiwas,
Āpan de ni kakö ni budđi nika hetunya n tan aṅgânuta*

Aṅhiŋ tâṅĕn-aṅĕnku maṅkata dumonê krĕṣṇa tātan waneḥ,
rājyê dwārawatī punaḥ parawaśan sakweḥ nikaŋ maṅjuru,
bwat solaḥ nika taṅgapĕn papagakĕn riŋ praŋ kasiṅhākrĕtin,
tuṇḍanyā makađaṙmmayudđan ikanaŋ kahyunkwa yan papraṅa*

nān liŋ saŋ narakâsahuṙ saŋ inajaṙ yuktîka deyâpraṅa,
sakweḥ niŋ ratu maṅjuru pwa warahĕn rapwan parĕŋ maṅkata,
maṅkā liŋ nika saŋ mahodara wawaŋ luṅhā tikaŋ cāraka,
śīǥrâpan mahawan tawaŋ paḍa madrĕs yekâmawâjñā haji*

ndaḥ waṙṇnan kĕta saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ sāṙ sök pĕnuḥ sañjata,
maṅkat saŋ narakâwimāna maṇipuṣpâtyanta śīǥrâṅlayaŋ,
sakweḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya rākṣasa kabeḥ kapwâhawan riŋ laṅit,
Ākāśâṙdđa pĕpĕt ƀaṭāra sawitā nisteja sāmpun pĕtĕŋ*

Agyā taŋ manapak lĕmaḥ wukiṙ alas đwasta ŋ tahĕn duṙbala,
guntuṙ taŋ himawān prakampita tikaŋ ƀūmy-âtiǥora ṅhaṅin,
kombak wway nikanaŋ samudra kumĕtug taŋ deśa digmaṇḍala,
Utpāta ŋ girisaṅǥa puṅgĕl apagut de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

sakweḥ niŋ kahalintaṅan ratu tumūt kapwâṅiriŋ gadgada,
maṅkin têmbuḥ ikaŋ watĕk naraka kīṙṇna ŋ rāt pĕnuḥ tan katon,
Āpan mānasa dꜽtya rākṣasa marok tuṅgal sapakṣâtĕguḥ,
yekā n byakta sawaṙgga saŋ naraka mattêkā n paṅuṇḍâyuđa*

saŋ cedi mwaŋ awaṅgarāja magađendra mwaŋ kaliṅgāđipa,
nāhan muꝁya nikaŋ tumūt madadakan maṅkat parĕŋ sāyuđa,
tan waṙṇnan ta lawas nirêŋ hawan atīta prāpta riŋ gobraja,
salwā-lwā nikanaŋ palugwan atitip tekaŋ watĕk rākṣasa*

muṅgw-î puñcak ikā ri gobraja siraŋ ƀomâpanas twas nira,
sākṣāt bahni murub tikaŋ muꝁa mabāŋ tekāŋ awak nīśala,
mawrut-wrut kadi đūma roma nira mawyaŋ mekĕl-ekĕl katon,
sāđyâtakwana dāya saŋ naraka riŋ wrĕṣṇy-ânđakâpan kulĕm*

saŋ cedy-âtaña sājña saŋ praƀu paran tôpāya saŋ ƀūpati,
maṅke śatru tĕkāna riŋ kulĕm usön rapwan ya kagyat kabeḥ,
nyāmâtiṅgal anak rabinya malayū kewran tikaŋ jro pura,
tunw-îkaŋ nagarâjaraḥ sahana niŋ ratnādi yekâlapĕn*

luṅhānya n marikā si krĕṣṇa malayū tūtĕn ta de saŋ praƀu,
yadyan sy-âṙjjuna rowaṅanya saꝑalanya mātya kaṙwwênarun,
sāmpun maṅkana hĕntyakĕn bala nikā sāmanta haywênaris,
Aṅhiŋ si druma pañjaran priḥ usirĕn de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

nā liŋ cedipati prayatna ta jarāsanđâsahuṙ gadgada,
Om siṅgiḥ sawuwusta yukti maṅĕnoḥ ri twas prasidđâhayu,
ndan maṅkêki kalaḥnya yan kajagana ṅwaŋ maṅrĕwĕk riŋ kulĕm,
kāṅgĕk piŋ rwa tiwas tikaŋ kakaninan ndātan hanêkâpuliḥ*

Āpan wyakti nikaŋ musuḥ ya rumĕṅö maṅke ṇ ḍatĕŋ saŋ praƀu,
nyā ŋ pekā matihaŋ mataṅhi ya pajaṙnyêkaŋ pamiṅgiṙ kabeḥ,
towîkaŋ balasaṅǥa ṅel nika turuŋ māry-âlapâṅlud rapuḥ,
t-aṅheṙ kapwa wiwekanĕn tĕkapa niŋ maṅdon musuḥ nītiman*

Ambĕk niŋ wwaŋ aśatru duṙnaya wĕnaŋ sepĕn taŋ alpêriya,
saŋ wānî rahinêŋ kulĕm tĕkapa niŋ wwaŋ yan dumonêrikā,
ya byaktêka tiwasnya yan taha-tahan pwêkā hade sāhasa,
Āpan tan rwa ta ya ŋ kabantĕn anĕke ndātan tĕkêŋ don ikā*

saŋ kṣepanya wiwekanĕn juga dĕlöntâmbĕk nikaŋ yādawa,
kweḥnya ŋ wwaŋ makĕḍiknya kawruhan awās ta ŋ wwaŋ ya tan prokṣaka,
yapwan ƀakti musuḥta ƀāgya marikâtūtêka tan saṅgrahan,
byaktâpan parikas lĕkas nika rĕbut kīṙttîŋ raṇa priḥ tĕmĕn*

mojaṙ kaṙṇna paranti niŋ naya wĕkas petĕn tĕkap saŋ praƀu,
Aṅhiŋ praŋ juga kenakanya waṅunĕn tâsön maƀedâdunĕn,
kās niŋ hasta lawan ta laṇḍĕp i tĕwĕktêkaŋ kawīrabratan,
ƀuktîkaŋ ꝑalaƀukti mukti t-aṅusiṙ kīṙtty-âđikārêŋ prajā*

wyaṙŧêkaŋ naya riŋ mahāpraƀawa śakty-âṅhiŋ lĕkasnyâdunĕn,
Āpan đaṙmma ni saŋ mahāpuruṣa tekaŋ sāhasêkiŋ musuḥ,

ndîkâmaṅpaṅa śakti saŋ praƀu rikeŋ rāt dèwa towy-ârarĕm*

nāhan liŋ saŋ awaṅgarāja sumahuṙ saŋ ƀoma tan kaṙkkaśa,

Āpan duṙyyaśanĕn tĕkap niŋ umulat keraŋ yadin tan bisa*

nyā ŋ wwaŋ rūpaka yan mamet iwak iwĕḥ dāyanya yan poliha,
saṅkĕp riŋ paṅalap ta yâpiliḥ uliḥ denyâlĕkas moliha,

tan tūtên panas iŋ hatîki sawalan tan sidđakāṙyyâsarag*

ṅ wwaŋ yan śakti halĕp ri śāsana ni kāṙyya wruḥ manīti ŋ musuḥ,
tan saṅkeŋ pĕjaḥ iŋ musuḥ karaṇa ni ŋ wwaŋ yañ jayêŋ papraṅan,
yan ƀaktîka musuḥnya samƀraman ikê sĕmbaḥnya sambeganĕn,
yekā n kīṙtti tĕmĕn ṅaranya ri siraŋ ƀūpālakā riŋ jagat*

Āpan budđi nikā si krĕṣṇa ta turuŋ ta mwêkihĕn kawruhan,
sugyan wĕdya tumona tapta sumahab kewran puriḥnyâkĕḍik,
dūta pwā ya ta kenakanya rumuhun konĕn ta ƀaktyê kita,
yan tan ƀaktya samaṅkana n lĕkasi tekaŋ dwārawatyâpuyi*

saŋ śatruntapa saŋ mahodara marāhê krĕṣṇa haywâgigu,
towekṣâmbĕk ikaŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ yan ƀaktya yan laṅǥana,

yan tan ƀaktya t-uliḥ tasön tĕka ri don rājyanya sep sāhasan*

ndā tĕmbesuk ikā n lumampaḥ uwusĕn sārîka sāmpun ḍatĕŋ,

ǥora ŋ rākṣasadꜽtyasaṅǥabala śabdanyâṅuhuḥ kātara,

I sĕḍĕŋ iraŋ mahāsurapati praśasta hana riŋ wukiṙ gobraja,

nāhan liŋ saŋ gadâkras rasanya,

donya ṅhiŋ tuṣṭa niŋ wwaŋ sarājya,
maṅkā taŋ śabda maṅke rĕṅönta,
donyâṅde rājya saŋ nāŧa tuṣṭa*

ndā mantra dyusta nityâprameya,
hīṅanya n śudđa tekaŋ kawaṅśan*

maṅke pwâsewakê saŋ mahīja,

byaktêkaŋ deśaƀukti n gatinta,
ƀaktî krĕṣṇâwarĕg ƀukti ƀoma*

ṅwaŋ mitrâtaḥ winehtâtilajja,
nāhan hetu ṅhulun yan pataṅguḥ,
rāmya ṅke yan kitâṅherana ṅke,
santoṣâmukti pöḥ niŋ kasāđun*

Āpan saŋ ƀoma loƀêŋ triloka,
nā hetunyâṅalap siŋ sakahyun,
ndan wwantĕn pwâśraya byakta nīca,
ṅūnîkā sāđu tan sāđu maṅke*

byaktêkānaŋ wwaŋ iŋ budđi sāđu,

nāhan ta yôjaṙ niraŋ ugrasena,

wĕkasan maśabda sira hāḥ kapūhan aku de nikaŋ yadukula,
ri wĕnaŋnya maṅkana wuwusnya tan mawĕdi mātya deṅku ya kabeḥ,

kāla niraŋ mahīsuta ḍatĕŋ prasama saha bala,
gaṙjjita saŋ watĕk yadu mapak sama mapagakĕna,
hetu nirâtihaŋ haṅun-aṅun wahu-wahu tinĕkan,
sañjata rakwa suṅsuṅakĕnêŋ ripu tĕka sahasa*

kweḥ nira saŋ watĕk ratu sahāya paḍa sira hana,

bāhlika somadatta paḍa śakti gati nira kabeḥ,
saŋ nrĕpa winda sānak anuwinda tahu ta malaga*

byakta kĕḍik nikaŋ bala mataŋnya n aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕta*

nāhan ujaṙ niraŋ drupada bāhlika sira sumahur,

wūk ta sakeŋ wurinya caturaṅga saka ri hiriṅan,
nyāma ratunya kāri mapuliḥ kucupi ta ya rĕbut*

saŋ nrĕpa somadatta sumahuṙ taha tan iku bisa,
Antyakĕnâta sāhasa nikaŋ musuḥ amasukana,
sāmpun ikā ṇ ḍatĕŋ tĕhĕṙ anunwani maṅamaḥ-amaḥ,
gyāt ya pisan t-atuṅkĕbana wūk prasama saha bala*

nyāta nikâlayū kahala tūt wuri nika susuni,

mojaṙ ikā saŋ aṙjjuna hade biṣama dahat ikā,

rigrig i rowaŋ iŋ wwaŋ alagâlaḥ awĕdi maṅaliḥ,
haywa hinerakĕñ juga tĕkap niŋ amusuḥ agalak*

śrī naranāŧa krĕṣṇa mawuwus rari diwasa kita,
sāhasa tan tahâmbĕka ni rowaŋ iŋ aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt*

tiṅkaḥ i saŋ krĕtāṙŧa rikanaŋ sama-sama mapagĕḥ,

nora ya meman-eman i patî pati-pati tumĕḍun*

yeka ta kāri hetu nika saŋ wani tan iman-iman,

wīra rare-rarêka pinakālas ira kahilaṅan,
rodra katon kasiṅhan ira n aṅdĕmaki musuḥ ira*

niṙ kawiwekan iŋ daṅu kĕtêkaŋ ulaḥ iŋ alaga,

byūha wineḥ matêka pasaṅĕn wruha ta ri hiriṅan,
tañ jriḥ i wūk nikaŋ ripukulâpagĕḥ ulaḥ-ulahĕn*

tĕkwan ikā hade karuhunâṅlĕkasi kita rari,
tambay iŋ eñjiŋ iṅwaŋ iki maṅkata parĕŋ apisan,
towi kulĕm ḍatĕŋ tuhun adandana ta sira kabeḥ,
ndā si gaṇākumāra ya matuṅgwa kuwu gati nikā*

mwaŋ mantrī nira rakṣakâraŧa sawaŋ karaŋ winulatan,
wwaŋ śūrāṙyya tikêŋ raṇāṅga makapādarakṣaka nira,
ya pwa n tan pabalik surud praŋ ika yan tĕkêŋ lawan ikā*

saŋ nāŧa drupadâhawan gajawiśeṣa pat gaḍiŋ ikā,
đrĕṣṭadyumna ṅarany-anak nira haneŋ raŧâruhuṙ agöŋ,
Akweḥ taŋ caturaṅga saŋ nrĕpati söḥ piraŋ puluḥ iwu,
mantrī taṇḍa nirâhawan raŧa lawan liman kinawacan*

maṅkat saŋ nrĕpa bāhlikâtiśaya riŋ kamānawiƀawan,
lāwan saŋ nrĕpa somadatta paḍa tâhawan raŧa magöŋ,
tan waṙṇnan caturaṅga saŋ nrĕpati kāliḥ ujwala katon,
de niŋ ƀūṣaṇa ratna kañcanamaya pradīpta kumĕñar*

maṅkat saŋ nrĕpa windu lāwan anuwinda sānak adulur,
līlâliṅgiḥ i rĕṅga niŋ gajapati rwa sāmpun arasuk,
sakweḥ niŋ bala wāḥ paḍanya humilī ndatan papĕgatan,
Aryak syandana wāhanāśwagaja pādarakṣa gumuruḥ*

sāmpun maṅkana saŋ narāđipatiy ugrasena wĕkasan,
saŋ wrĕṣṇy-anđakawīra ŋ aṅgaparirakṣa muṅgwiŋ iriṅan,
maṅkā tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ gajāśwaraŧa pādarakṣa wĕki sök,
sākṣāt paṙwwata rug kĕtug ni gubaṙ iŋ watĕk pinamĕgĕt*

saŋ nāŧātmaja kāṙwwa satyaka sudeha muṅgu ri wuri,
mwaŋ saŋ śāraṇa saŋ wicitraka widūratāmrĕta tumūt,
kapwânuṅgaŋ umuṅguḥ iŋ raŧa winaṙṇna-waṙṇna riŋ ĕmās,
lwiṙ kambaŋ manĕḍĕŋ buṅaḥ nira tĕkap nikā n kabaraṇaŋ*

maṅkat saŋ krĕtađaṙmmanāŧa sayuđāꝁya siṅhapuruṣa,
krūrākāra haneŋ raŧāṅga sira n aṅgakāra madulur,
rāmya ŋ taṇḍa kabeḥ tĕkêŋ balasahāya kapwa matitaḥ,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ caturaṅga tan papĕgatan marampak atatā*

saŋ mātsyāđipa māhawan dwirada mīnarūpa marasuk,
molaḥ taṇḍa nirâgulāṅan atulis miraḥ mata kabeḥ,
Akweḥ ƀrĕtya nirâsisik putiḥ anorakĕn bañu pasaŋ,
norêkâpacalan lĕkas nira n anūtakĕn kakulajan*

yapwan kīcaka ŋ aṅgarakṣaka narendra śakti suyaśa,
ndan tahw-âṅawisa ŋ musuḥ tĕka nira n haneŋ raṇasaƀā,
mewĕḥ teka n atĕmwa ros wuku nikaŋ kasiṅhan i sira,
saŋ lāgînucap iŋ katuṅtaṅan i kīṙtti riŋ raṇasaƀā*

⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ –  ⏑| –  ⏑ ⏑|  ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 29

ri tĕlas irân mijil sahana saŋ watĕk yadu lawan watĕk ratu humuŋ tikaŋ bala kabeḥ,
pĕnuḥ irikaŋ tĕgal gahana gahwarâlas alilaŋ wiśīṙṇna tĕkap iŋ raŧâkuda liman,

paḍahi lawan taroñji murawâpratiđwani kĕtug ni kĕṇḍaŋ iŋ aroha ǥora gumuruḥ*

salĕsĕk i lampaḥ iŋ balasamūha tan papĕgatan sakeŋ purasaƀā pwa tan paligaran,

Iṅut-iṅutĕn lanênubatakĕn cucuk ni pikulanya meḥ anukak an kacuṇḍuk iŋ wuri*

hana ta makuṇḍaŋ aṇḍarat i tuṇḍasāra mapĕṅiŋ ri kuṇḍaŋ ika tan pakālib apulut,

luṅhā ŋ lampaḥ saŋ yadu saṅke dwārawatī śīǥra paḍâgyā,
kāwit-kāwit saŋ rĕṣi durwāśêka cumuṇḍuk nrĕpa krĕṣṇa,

sidđāsidđa ŋ wāk śapaŧêṅgal yan mapĕṅiŋ towi kuraŋ twas*

Agyā-gyā-gyā yan tumurun saṅkeŋ raŧa sāmpun ta manambaḥ,
Enak pwa wruḥ saŋ rĕṣi yan trĕptîka kaƀaktin haji ri twas,
menak tâmbĕk niścaya mājaṙ sāṙjjawa somyârūm aśabda*

pun pāṙŧā pun rukma tikaŋ konĕn pun anāraŧyakĕna praŋ,

hari ni ṅhulun daki saŋ aṙjjuna ṅwaŋ awĕkas-wĕkas pwa ri kita,
kalawan ta saŋ nrĕpati rukma rakṣa nikanaŋ watĕk yadubala,

sira saŋ mahāṙṣi sira têkihĕn labuhanâṅhuwus brata nira*

sira saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ mareŋ paƀaratan paḍâhyun ayaśa,
Ikanaŋ bala prakaṭa kātarâmalaku śatru rākṣasabala,
Alapâpraŋ abrata kasiṅhan agya malawas maṅanti labuhan*

nrĕpati druma mwaŋ ika saŋ narendra basudewa muṅgu ri wuri,

mwaŋ ikaŋ gadâwĕsi satal pinañjĕṙ aṅadĕg tiniṅhalan ira*

pinakāđikāra para taṇḍa saŋ kṣitisutâtiśakti suyaśa*

ri wijil nirâṙyya magađâpaḍâhalĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ gajapati,
tĕka sewu taŋ liman agöŋ hane wuri tĕlas kabeḥ makawaca,
turagâpipit piraŋ iwū wwaŋ iŋ raŧa magöŋ arampak atatā,
bala pādarakṣaka pĕnuḥ wajanya mahulap tĕwĕknya lumarap*

milu teka saŋ ratu samāṅjuru prasama tan hanêka makutis,
paḍa tâhalĕp halĕp i saŋ prawīra maraŧêka len aturaga,
papupul ni sañjata nikaŋ samaṅkana wutaḥnya tan papĕgatan,
kadi wāḥ gunuŋ saha watunya śīǥra gumuluŋ tĕkêŋ paƀaratan*

I sĕḍĕŋ ikaŋ watĕk naraka wāspadê rĕpat ikaŋ watĕk yadubala,
Aṅun-aṅun aṅgaraṅgaŋ anĕkāni tan pamali wiṣṭi śūra sahasa,
sawuṙ i panaḥnya gaṇḍi nika sök pasöṙnya lumĕpas lawan gutu-gutuk,

Ikaŋ akudâṅdĕmak praŋ ika siṅlaṙ oliḥ akalis luput kinurubut,
saŋ araŧa sāhasâmanaḥ anūb panaḥnya maṅĕne mamātyani waneḥ,

kuda kĕna māti yênatus-atus lawan raŧa pĕjaḥ ṅ Anuṅgaŋ iriya*

makin asusun tikaŋ bala ri bāhlika n sinusunan muwaḥ lawan abāp,
patĕmu nikâṅlaga prasama malwaŋ-alwaṅi muwaḥ matambĕḥ i wuri,
tuhu paḍa wāni tan dadi surud mamūk amurugul winūk winalĕsan,
hana ta ya kabraṇan mati dudū tikaŋ pinamĕgĕt huwus kapugutan*

bala nira cedināŧa humarĕp mare drupadanāŧa sāhasa masö,
Aṅun-aṅun iŋ lagâdƀuta pamūk nikâtiśaya riŋ kaśūran apagĕḥ,
guragaḍa tan panaṅgĕl agalak parĕŋ kuda raŧanya kapwa kumucup,
capala tĕkâṅgalaḥ riŋ adĕgan tĕkâmraŋ anĕsĕb saroṣa tan arĕs*

binalikakĕn tinaṅkis amalĕs manaṅkis atahĕn winūk sinusunan,
makakĕrĕpuk tikĕl ḍaḍap ikaŋ tibā mati matimbun iŋ raṇasaƀā,
paḍa-paḍa śūra kapwa makaluŋ masiṅhĕl akaraḥ tĕlas karahatan,
Inatus-atus tikaŋ balapadāti wīra kawĕnaŋ katon aguliṅan*

śara niśitâduluṙ watu lawan ta dukduk ahawan laṅit malayanan,
kagila-gila ŋ galaḥ waja nikâṅlarap-larap arok siliḥ-palu waneḥ,
ḍaḍap akatap-katap kagurilap tĕwĕknya maṅĕnêkaŋ amraŋ anacaḥ,
Ikaŋ apuliḥ-puliḥ mapulihan siliḥ-sĕsĕb alaḥ pĕjaḥ tan umurud*

śawa nikanaŋ turaṅga kagulimpaŋ iŋ paƀaratan lawan raŧa rĕmuk,
pira-pira taŋ prawīra mati len sĕḍĕŋ kakuwuṅan maṅohan umĕkĕḥ,
tuhu-tuhu tan hana ŋ pakadaṅan tĕkap nira saŋ amriḥ iŋ raṇasaƀā,
pijĕṙ aṅusiṙ praŋ amrihawak ambĕk amriḥ ayaśâtapêŋ paƀaratan*

bala nira somadatta sahasômasö bala narendra kaṙṇna pinapag,
lumĕpasakĕn panaḥnya hana tâmataŋ sahaja taŋ tĕkâmraŋ anitir,
pinapagakĕn pamūknya n inarug rinok siliḥ-arug laganya wĕkasan,
Ajĕmuṙ arok tikaŋ laga siliḥ-lwaŋ adƀuta Aneka māti matunaḥ*

rika haji winda lāwan anuwinda kīṙṇna gumuluŋ katon i hiriṅan,
kumucup anandaṅîkaŋ i harĕpnya wadwa yawanêśwarātmaja kabeḥ,
Agul-agul aṅgalaḥ mamurugul mabāŋ waja galaḥnya moliḥ amati,
Ikaŋ aṅalap cĕṅĕl curik ikā miraḥ pira-piraŋ puluḥ wwaŋ aṅalap*

hana kĕna duk waneḥ kĕna panaḥ kagaṇḍi kagalaḥ waneḥ wahu tibā,
hana sinĕsĕb pinökan inarug lawan tika galaḥnya tan kapulihan,
papan apagut dudū taŋ anuduk suduknya kapĕluk pupug maṅĕnani,
makakurucuk cucuk ni galaḥ iŋ prawīra kumucup tumandaŋ anucuk*

wahu tumĕḍun waneḥ kinurubut mapakṣa murudâtakut kinurutug,
lalu kaduhuŋ manaḥnya ya katuṇḍuŋ epu mulat iŋ lawan sĕḍĕŋ amūk,
lupa kumĕtig hatinya katutug ḍaḍanya kataraṅgul eṅas aṅaḍuḥ,
Uḍuḥ ibu liŋ nikā n kaliwatan panaḥ wĕkasan aṅḍuhuŋ kĕna dinuk*

Aciṅaŋ ikaŋ tumiṅhali lawanya sāhasa tumandaŋ amraŋ anacaḥ,
mulat i wurî palaywana nikā n kawuntwan atakut ywa tan wriŋ ulaha,
kaparĕpĕkan pwa yâṅlalu manaḥnya mātya karaṇanya yan mrĕm awĕdi,
ri wulat ikā n wuruŋ lawan ikânuruŋ cakĕt agasyak ojaṙ aṅabuk*

hanan arawis ya tâkalis anon lawan kadi pinis hatinya rumaras,
lagi mariṅas kawĕs kawĕnĕsan manon tĕṅĕran iŋ musuḥnya n umasö,
rumaras arĕs hanan maṅĕsĕsan lanâṅgĕgĕs amoṙ iŋ aṅhawin adoḥ,
karaṇa nikā n atis tan inaris-haris rawis ikâradin dinudutan*

hana tikanâ bapaŋ-bapaŋ abāŋ papanya tinahâpa tan wani dahat,
ḍaḍap ikahĕn kinonakĕn ikā n palaywakĕna de ni paṅhawin ikā,
Apitaña tê raṅinya katĕkān ulaḥ pati pĕṅöŋ mahâṅuman-uman,
dalihan ikā malaywani ḍaḍap malayw-akipit eṅas amriḥ anikus*

mapuliḥ ikaŋ prawīra mapuput-puput praŋ ika kapwa moliḥ amaḍĕm,
sakatĕmu de nikâbabaran āwrĕg orig alulun winūk sinusupan,
kuḍuwak ikā miraḥ paḍa kasaŋsaṅan gajiḥ awaṙṇna rumbaḥ amiraḥ,
wiga pagawenya raṇḍa magawe wulañjaṙ agawe rare huwuḥ-uwuḥ*

sĕḍĕŋ arurĕk praŋ iŋ balapadāti len kuda siliḥ-sĕsĕb paḍa wani,
raŧa malawan raŧâraŧa-raŧan paḍâṅlwaŋ ika sewu sowaŋ atugur,

karaṇa nikaŋ tĕgal paƀaratan pĕtĕŋ jĕmuṙ ikaŋ prawīra malaga*

maṅkin maṅgĕḥ pĕtĕŋ ikaŋ alaga,
tan wriŋ rowaŋ sahana-hana nikā,
tĕṅran ndātan hana juga katĕṅĕr,
gĕṇḍiŋ roñji prasama mawurahan*

sakweḥ saŋ nāŧa sumahab i harĕp,
maṅkā sāmantri nira saha liman,
lāwan muṅgwiŋ raŧa mamawa laras,
Akweḥ tekaŋ gajaraŧa maṅiriŋ*

yekā n tandaŋ mamanaḥ anakiti,
māyākāra n tinuju nira kĕna,
mwaŋ kontā tomara nira lumĕpas,
samyânumbak suligi mamisani*

wet niŋ kweḥnya ŋ kĕna kadi rinujak,

sumyuk rāḥnyâdrĕs sumirat aniram,

sakweḥ saŋ māti ya ta winulatan,

ƀāwanyâlaḥ malĕs aṅalahakĕn,
An saŋ wīrâlwaŋ ika kasakitan,
munduṙ sāmpun kalĕpas inusuṅan*

Akweḥ śūrêŋ gaja raŧa kawĕnaŋ,

rĕmpak taŋ syandana turaga pĕjaḥ,

tatkālanya n wahu mapahidĕṅan,

lwiṙnya n tan paṅgalĕŋ aṅiwuŋ amūk*

dantīnyênanti wuri niŋ alayū*

saŋ nāŧâṅheṙ maṅadĕg aṅililan,

makweḥ ta lwaŋ ni musuḥ ira pĕjaḥ*

saŋ yođâsyandana paḍa lumurug,
len taŋ muṅgwī gaja turaga masö*

kīṙṇna n kātiṅgal ika kasulayaḥ*

milwîkaŋ dꜽtya maliman umasö,

seriŋ saŋ mānawiṣama sahasa,
wadwānyâwāhana-turaga-liman*

len tekaŋ senawiṣama mamawa,

kontâṅontêriya pamati musuḥ*

saŋ nrĕpa somadatta mamanaḥ mamarĕpĕki musuḥ,
tĕṅgĕk i duṙṇnayênaraḥ-araḥ nira pinatitisan,
hrū nira ŋ aṙdđacandra lumĕpas murub aṅarab-arab,
ƀinna tibā ta tĕṇḍas i si duṙṇnaya saha lawayan*

krođa tikā n si mānawiṣamâṅlĕpasi śarawara,

kapwa paḍâmanaḥ maraḥ-araḥ ḍaḍa patakuraṅan,
hrūnya sawaŋ suluŋ-suluŋ anon damaṙ aṅarab-arab*

saŋ yaduwīra satyaka wideha sira ta matuluŋ,

lwiṙ kadi siṅha kātara mamatyani gajaḥ agalak*

kadga gadā panaḥ saha galaḥnya ya ta katihalaŋ,
hetu ni duṙggamê tĕgal ayomaya-maya wĕkasan*

krūra nikâṅuhuḥ riris agantya śarawara tibā*

Āḥ pawuwuḥ wuwusnya n awuwuḥ wani nikaŋ alaga,

ṅhiŋ nrĕpa śālya kapwa dinunuŋ saha bala lumurug,
tan hana tan tumūt sahana saŋ ratu marĕk i sira,
kapwa parĕŋ pisan sira n amāḥ gunuŋ awijaḥ amūk*

ǥūṙṇnita taŋ surak saha lawan murawa paḍa humuŋ,
paṅrĕguŋ iŋ gaja ṅhrik i turaṅga ni raŧa niŋ alaḥ,
ǥoṙ huni niŋ gubaṙ humuŋ agĕnturan akĕrĕtugan,
tulya gĕrĕḥ swaranya gumuruḥ kadi gĕlap ataruŋ*

đīra narendra śālya maṅadĕg mayat i laras agöŋ,
hrū nira kātarôjwala manīṙṇna ripukulabala,
maṅkin aneka tampuḥ i panaḥ nira malĕsi musuḥ,
rākṣasa dꜽtya dānawa piśāca mati tĕkap ira*

bāhlikanāŧa len drupadarāja sira sinahasa,
tan hinĕbaŋ-hĕbaŋ tinĕpĕtan bala nira kabalik,
tan hana tâpuliḥ kapalupuy gupu-gupurĕn arĕs,
tan wuwusĕn tikaŋ pĕjaḥ aneka saha kuda liman*

maṅkin alaḥ ta saŋ ratu watĕk yadu bubaṙ i harĕp,
ƀrĕtya nirânanā linĕpasan śarawara niśita,
siŋ mapuliḥ pĕjaḥ karika yan mati pinarĕbutan,
hetu nikâluyuk lĕlĕḥ aṅel asukĕṙ alaradan*

saŋ kicakâṅadĕg saha gadâwĕsi ginĕgĕ nira,
krođa tumandaŋ aṅhala-halâṅubat-abit amupuḥ,
Alwaŋ aneka taŋ yawananāŧasutabala winūk,
sāk śakaṭanya sīṙṇna gaja wāhana nika pinupuḥ*

saŋ yawanendraputra mapuliḥ rumĕbut i kicaka,
lwiṙ kararaṅga sānak apupul sama-sama maṅasut,
tomara konta sāyaka nikâparimita lumĕpas,
lwiṙ sukĕt iŋ halisyus umidĕṙ kumĕtĕṙ aputĕran*

krođa ta saŋ wirāṭapati muṅgwi liman ira masö,

moliḥ amatyanī yawananāŧasuta saha bala*

śeṣa nikaŋ pĕjaḥ ya ta masĕṅhit apuliḥ amanaḥ,

mwaŋ hana tâgadâwĕsi mupuḥ kicaka paḍa mamūk,
kapwa siliḥ-pupuḥ paḍa ta māyuđa magada-gadān*

saŋ drupadātmajêka hinirup ta sira kinucupan,

towi sirêka saŋ drupadarāja tumuluy atuluŋ,
mwaŋ bala riŋ raŧāśwa kumucup saha liman agalak*

saŋ nrĕpa śālya maṅlĕpasakĕn panaḥ ira masulam,

mwaŋ drupadādirāja maṅayat laras ira n amanaḥ,
hrū saha bāyubajra gumuruḥ ya ta pamanaḥ ira*

tan dwa tikāŋ piśāca kalulun kawĕnaŋ ika pĕjaḥ,

yakṣa pĕjaḥ pirêŋ puluḥ aneka juru nika pĕjaḥ,
mukṣa minantran astra malayū ta turaḥ ika kawĕs*

saŋ nrĕpa cedi taṙ wĕnaŋ arĕs ry-alaḥ ikaŋ i kiwa,

len ikaŋ amraŋ aṅduk anuhuk pamaja haji wijaḥ*

bĕntaṙ ikaŋ watĕk yadubala rwaŋ iwu pĕjaḥ amūk,

siŋ mapuliḥ pĕjaḥ yatika hetu nika giri-girin,
tan mawĕdîka kālapana denya harĕpa huripa*

śīǥra đanañjayâjaṙ i narendrasuta yadukula,

ƀoḥ ta t-tamukti ƀukti ꝑalaƀukti tĕwas iŋ alaga,

ṅhiŋ si kaśūran uttama ṅaranya dadaḥ iŋ ahurip*

heman i denta tiṅgalakĕna ŋ yaśa maṅusira len,

yan bwat ikaŋ hurip dadi hilaŋ ya kinatĕṅĕtakĕn,

đaṙmmawiśeṣa riŋ kadi kita wruḥ atapa matĕguḥ,

nān liŋ saŋ pāṙŧa malwī sahana-hana nikā saŋ watĕk wīrayođa,

sāmpun pĕjaḥ saŋ nrĕpa cedi riŋ raṇa,

śīǥrâṅunus kadga nira praƀāswara,
sep saŋ druma n kapraŋ i rĕṅga niŋ raŧa*

lumpat niraŋ kaṙṇna sake swawāhana,
muṅsî sira śrī basudewa tan waneḥ,
Agyā sirâpakṣa manampilêŋ raŧa,
kagyat cinakrâmalĕs amraŋ iŋ tĕwĕk*

māti pwa saŋ rwâsiga kaṙṇna yan katon,
līlâṅadĕg riŋ śakaṭâṅgĕgön laras,
saŋ sāmba sakrođa tĕhĕṙ sirômasö,
tujw-î panaḥ saŋ rawiputra lāǥawa*

saŋ kaṙṇna śīǥra n paṅayat laras nira,
hrū nāgapāśa n tumihaŋ tĕkap nira,
sāmpun lĕpas kātara ƀīṣaṇômaṅaŋ,
śabdanya tan pāntara riŋ naƀastala*

kālanya muṅgwiŋ gaganāntarâṅlayaŋ,
saŋ sāmba sāmpun lumĕpas panaḥ nira,
hrū wꜽnateyāstra mahogra śaktimān,
yekâmaṅan hrū nrĕpa kaṙṇna riŋ laṅit*

saŋ kaṙṇna maṅkin sira tan tahĕn hati,
kālogradaṅṣṭrā lumĕpas tĕkap nira,
saŋ sāmba yatnâmanahi ŋ mahāśara,
mrĕtyuñjayāstrāđipa nāma kātara*

śabdanya ǥorêŋ gaganâtiǥūṙṇnita,
hrū kaṙṇna puṅgĕl katakis tibêŋ lĕmaḥ,
sakrođa rāđeya sirâmanaḥ muwaḥ,
riŋ candrawimbāṙdđaśara praƀāswara*

sāmpun lĕpas ƀīṣaṇa tulya handaru,
sāmba prawīra wruḥ i tampuḥ iŋ panaḥ,
mĕṇḍĕk sirânaṅgulakĕn laras nira,
puṅgĕl ta laṅkap nira paṙwwa riŋ taṅan*

śīǥrâṅalap cakra wawaŋ sirâmalĕs,
puṅgĕl đanuḥ saŋ rawiputra de nira,
maṅsö sirâñakra muwaḥ ndatan surud,
tĕṅgĕk niraŋ kaṙṇna cinakra niṙƀaya*

krođêka saŋ sāmba ri kaṙṇna tan kanin,
nā hetu niŋ mambil ikaŋ gadā n asö,
yekâmupuḥ syandana kaṙṇna riŋ gadā,
kārun lawan sāraŧi māti de nira*

saŋ kaṙṇna śīǥra n tumĕḍun sakeŋ raŧa,
tañ jriḥ tĕhĕṙ sambutakĕn gadā nira,
yekā n paḍâdwandwa gadāyuđêrikā,
lāwan siraŋ sāmba siliḥ-pupuḥ sira*

kapwâṅiriŋ cidra widagđa riŋ sikĕp,
ndātan hanâsoṙ paḍa śakti suśrama,
sidđaṙṣy-anonton hana riŋ naƀastala,
mahyā humuŋ śabda nira n paṅadwakĕn*

saŋ sāmba moǥa n kasikĕp gadā nira,
de saŋ nrĕpâṙkkātmaja riŋ taṅan kiwā,
hastê tĕṅĕn sūṙyyasutâmupuḥ musuḥ,
ṅkānêŋ hujuŋ bāhu niraŋ nrĕpātmaja*

māṙ bāhu saŋ sāmba tĕṅĕn kĕnêŋ gadā,
hetunya siṅsal ta gadā nirê taṅan,
mūṙcꞓā sirê sakṣaṇa de nikaŋ lara,
ṅkâmriḥ sirâtaṅgal uđāni đāraka*

de niŋ kađīran matahĕn sirâtutur,
yekā n amūk prĕp nrĕpa kaṙṇna riŋ kiwān,
rāđeya rĕmpū ta śiraḥ nirâpasaḥ,
maṅlaḥ tibê saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ swawāhana*

saŋ kaṙṇna sāmpun pĕjaḥ iŋ raṇāṅgana,
wadwā nirâwrĕg saha wāhanâlayū,
saŋ sāmba sāmpun winawêŋ raŧâruhur,
Aṅgâmiraḥ dinyus i rāḥ pataṅgaja*

kālanya māwrĕg tikanaŋ balâlayū,
maṅsö jarāsanđa lawan samāṅjuru,
Atyanta riŋ kweḥ tuwi tumpĕkan kabeḥ,
himpĕṙ gunuŋ rug saha wāḥ mahajwala*

<madanalalitā>:93.
– – –| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – – –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏓ = 16

maṅkat saŋ yādawa saha lawan wrĕṣṇyāndaka kabeḥ,
sāmanta mwaŋ bala kadi tasik rob kādrĕsan aṅin,
sakweḥ niŋ sāmaja raŧa kuda lwiṙ duṙggama karaŋ,
saŋ wīrâṅkĕn hyu pinakarayāta praŋnya mamati*

Enak taŋ praŋ matĕmu ri tĕṅaḥ malwaŋ piraŋ iwu,
maṅkin mātimbun akatap atip taŋ sāmaja pĕjaḥ,
maṅkā taŋ syandana hana ta rimpĕk len hana rĕmuk,
membuḥnya n duṙgga pinakasukĕtnyêkaŋ raṇasaƀā*

Akweḥ sāmanta mati kĕna riŋ kontā n kakuwuṅan,
mwaŋ tekaŋ māti kĕna pinanaḥ trus twasnya katibā,
Āstām taŋ pekabala matumaŋ waṅkaynya tinapak,
rodra ŋ wīrâlaga pakatĕkĕnyâkadga niśita*

yekâṅsö saŋ narapati hiraṇyānāƀa nipuṇa,
muṅgwiŋ hastī n kinawacan awaṙṇnâpuy winulatan,
hrū tan pāntêri laras ira kapwa lwiṙ latu-latu,
đwastā taṅyādawabala gĕsöŋ de niŋ panas ikā*

maṅkat saŋ waƀru mapagi hiraṇyâdrĕs raŧa nira,
hrū tīkṣṇâtyanta pamanaḥ ira lwiṙ wintaŋ aṅaliḥ,
kādƀūtâwoṙ kilat awilĕt aṅde rĕs niŋ umulat,
tĕmpuḥnyânīṙṇna makuṭa hiraṇyâsyuḥ katariwal*

mūṙcꞓālök towin alara hiraṇyâpan kakaninan,
krođa n tandaŋ liman ika musî saŋ waƀru kumucup,
yatna śrī waƀru mamanaḥ hiraṇya mwaŋ gajaḥ ira,
cek ceŋ tampuḥ ni warayaŋ irê hastī n kinawacan*

maṅkin krođa ŋ liman aṅuliŋ adrĕs tandaŋ ikahĕn,
Ambĕknyâhyun maṅulĕṅa ri saŋ waƀru n pamurugul,
saŋ waƀru wruḥ tumuluy umurud mwaŋ syandana nira,
Ahyā taŋ śatrubala ha ha hāḥ liŋnyâṅguyu-guyu*

krođâmbĕk saŋ gada mamulihî saŋ waƀru malayū,
śīǥrâmĕṇṭaŋ laras ira lĕpas mwaŋ hrū nira wawaŋ,
limpad tĕṇḍas ni gajaḥ i hiraṇyâpaṙwwa ya bĕlaḥ,
śabdanya n paṅrĕguŋ awurahan munduṙ ya wulaṅun*

sāmpun māti pwa ya kadi gunuŋ rug ǥūṙṇnita humuŋ,
yekā n lumpat narapati hiraṇyâtaṅgal aṅadĕg,
muṇḍôṇḍê śūla niśita murub paṅduk nira lĕpas,
yatnâtā saŋ gada mamalĕs iŋ kontā mamisani*

sāmpun mātîka nrĕpati hiraṇya trus ḍaḍa nira,
yekâṅsö saŋ magađapati muṅgwî sāmajapati,
Atyanta hrū nira kadi ta waṙṣâdrĕs lĕpas ikā,
lāwan taŋ bāyu duluṙ ika wagyūtpāta makilat*

hrū saṅhārāstra pamalĕs iraŋ krĕṣṇātmaja wawaŋ,
mwaŋ bāyw-ākās kadi hira dahat dṛĕṣṇyâmaluyakĕn,
kedĕṙ hrū saŋ magađapati denyâlaḥ maṅadu kās,
tĕmpuḥnyê saŋ magađapati kedĕṙ sāmaja nira*

tambis mātîka nrĕpati jarāsanđa n katuluyan,
yan tan đīrâtĕguḥ atuturêŋ rudrasmrĕti sira,
yekā ta hrū nira ta ya mahāśakti n lĕpasakĕn,
henak de saŋ narapati mahāđyānâṅlĕpasakĕn*

yatna wruḥ saŋ gada linĕpasan mĕṇḍĕk juga sira,
nyā ṅhrū bajrojwala walĕs irâtyantê katatakut,
rūpanya n pañcamuꝁa wipulâkās lwiṙ gunuŋ anak,
rĕñcĕm syuḥ denya gaja magađendrâgĕm kapisanan*

<prĕŧwītala>:94.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

lumumpat ika saŋ narendra magađāđirāja tumuluy,
sumambut irikaŋ gadâwĕsi mupuḥ ri saŋ gada sira,
siraŋ gada luput kunĕŋ raŧa nirêka śīṙṇna kapupuḥ,
gadâwĕsi muwaḥ sinambut ira yan tĕḍun sira wawaŋ*

rikā ta magađendra daṙppa mamupuḥ ri saŋ gada sira,
luput pwa sira saŋ gadêka pinupuḥ malĕs ta ya mupuḥ,
paḍâṅiriṅi cidra saŋ rwa masuwe siliḥ-palu sira,
maṅadwakĕn awū watĕk ratu tumon ri saŋ rwa malaga*

kacidra kapupuḥ lĕṅĕn magađarāja tañ jriḥ atahĕn,
wicitra mamalĕs ḍumaṇḍa ḍaḍa saŋ gadêka tumuluy,
pataṅgul ikanaŋ gadâtikĕl apaṙwwa kaṙwwa ri taṅan,
ya hetu nira saŋ rwa kapwa maṅalap krĕtāla wĕkasan*

mapālaga mapatrayudđa sira kapwa siṅlaṙ akalis,
siliḥ-praŋ asĕluṙ widagđa matakis ri paṅlaga nira,
Amoǥa magađendra yan kĕḍap i soway an kamadĕlön,
kasep kĕna gulū nirêŋ kṣaṇa pĕgat pĕjaḥ kapisanan*

Aŧa ri pĕjaḥ iraŋ jarāsanđa māwrĕg watĕk ƀoma bĕntaṙ numānanya ƀagna n paḍâlaḥ rĕbaḥ kolaḥ-olaḥ winahwaḥ nanârĕs kawöswös kagöman minohan rinok tan pasāra n matiṅgal galaḥ paṇḍi gaṇḍinya lāwan ḍaḍapnya n parok tuṅgal aṅrimpĕd iŋ pekayođa n tibâṅaṅgal-aṅgal jumoṅkoŋ jumaṅkaḥ sukunya n lanā kedĕkan de ni rowaŋnya meḥ mātya yan patyakĕn tekanâṅganya maṅheṙ amoṙ iŋ śawâmet urip kāsihan yâmĕgöŋ prāṇa maṅlimbaŋ iŋ rāḥ kumambaŋ kahilyan śawâmoǥa mārambakan komba-kāmbaḥ ya de niŋ liman saŋ watĕk wrĕṣṇiwīrâṅusī saŋ watĕk ƀūmija,

taku-takutĕn ikaŋ watĕk rākṣasa mwaŋ watĕk yakṣa lāwan piśācâduluṙ nāgaśeṣâlaḥ oliḥ larâlök lanā lwiṙnya maṅboṅlwat alwâmbĕk-ambĕk kaninya n lanâṅĕmbak-ĕmbak mibab yan babak len ri lambuŋ nikâṅambĕk-ambĕk tĕkêŋ ambĕkanya n tan imbā taṅanyânukup tañ cukup tan kacumpwan kacuk-cak ta rāḥnya n lumuñcat lumiñcak tumindak tĕkap niŋ hawan luṅka-luṅka n hibĕk waṅkay iŋ tuṅgaṅan kāraṇanya n paḍâṅĕṅgaḥ-ĕṅgaḥ masambat bapa mwaŋ bibi mwaŋ ri putranya putrīnya maṅkin ta yâṅĕmbiḥ-ĕmbiḥ tibā luḥnya mādrĕs tan ampĕt nimittanya maṅkin taṅisnyâṇḍahuŋ*

kahala kawalayaḥ luyuk śeṣa niŋ māti muṅsiṙ pakuwwanya rewātakârampak iŋ pāṙśśwa len taŋ tibā riŋ juraŋ ƀrĕtya saŋ śrī jarāsanđa sāmpun pĕjaḥ kāsihan yânusup riŋ sukĕt mwaŋ guhênuṅsi nistanya tan mātya de niŋ watĕk yādawânūt suđīrātarêkânujaḥ riŋ tuhuk mamraŋ iŋ ƀindiwālâma-naḥ tan pĕgat hrūnya kontānya tan pāntarâtĕmpuḥ aṅde takutnya ŋ watĕk ƀoma yekârĕbut māṙgga ri priṅga sĕṅkan sĕsök sök siliḥ-tiṇḍiḥ aṅrĕs manaḥ niŋ tumon yênusi,

Agarawalan ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya muṅgwiŋ kudâtuṅgw-i saŋ ƀoma kagyat ḍĕṅö hūŋ nikaŋ wrĕṣṇiyođâṅuhuḥ kātara lwiṙ gĕrĕḥ niŋ catussāgarê kāla niŋ bāyusaṅhāra yekâmaṅun krođa niŋ dꜽtyasaṅǥâṅadĕg sāyuđa n ton ikaŋ cedisenâlayū mwaŋ jarāsanđasenā lawan kaṙṇnasenâduluṙ tan panāŧâpitowin tikâmājaṙ i śrī mahādꜽtyarājā tĕlas māti saŋ mitra katrīṇi yekā n kabāṅan tikâwak nirâsĕṅhit iŋ wrĕṣṇiwīrânđakâtyanta muntab panas niŋ hati,

karaṇa saŋ asurāđipânuṅgaŋ iŋ puṣpakā yômasö mwaŋ tikaŋ dꜽtya-saṅǥâmanek wāhananyâṅrĕgĕp sañjatanyâṅlayaŋ riŋ laṅit kabwaṅan meǥa de ny-aṅin iŋ wāhanâdrĕs katon lwiṙ ǥanêŋ māǥamāsâtri ǥora n gumĕntĕṙ suraknyê ruhuṙ lwiṙ nikā meǥanādêka tambis pĕtĕŋ ṅganya tan wwantĕna ŋ ƀūṣaṇa mwaŋ warāstrâprameyapraƀā ƀāswarânekarūpâkilat mwaŋ larap niŋ krĕtālâtitīkṣṇa n krĕbĕt niŋ đwajanyâhulap māsnya tan papramāṇê ruhuṙ lwiṙnya tāraṅganê kāla niŋ mađyarātrîŋ sarāt,

kala-kala hulap iŋ wiyat ṅ-āmarāśatrunāŧêŋ wimānâsigā ṅkâṅadĕg niṙƀayê śabda niŋ wrĕṣṇiwīrânđakâsampay iŋ rākṣasâpan mahāśakti gamƀīrawīṙyya n watĕk praŋ krĕtākrĕtya riŋ yudđakāṙyyâđikārêŋ kaśūran kađīran lanâkīṙtti ṅūnîŋ raṇâsiŋ musuḥ de nikârĕs dumeḥ göŋnya hĕṅkāra saŋ ƀoma ƀaṅgâṅgakārâṅgĕgö kāƀimānan mahā niṙƀayê saŋ watĕk wrĕṣṇi hamham sirâśatru saŋ hyaŋ mahendrâpĕs opĕk dinon tan pasārêka kāṅĕn tĕkap saŋ mahādānawâmbĕknya siṅhākrĕti*

paṅamaḥ-amaḥ ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtyayođâṅlayaŋ sañjatanyâ hulap lwiṙ hĕlaŋ yan tĕkâmraŋ mamaṇḍĕm śiraḥ niŋ mahāwīra śatrunya meww-īwu yekā n pamaṇḍĕmnya riŋ wrĕṣṇiwīrâgrayođa pwa taŋ dꜽtya tökânikĕp tuṅgaṅan mwaŋ gajaḥ syandanâsiŋ kasambut panimbat nikê saŋ yaduƀrĕtya len rākṣasâṅambaḥ iŋ waṅkay iŋ wīra len taŋ manĕmpal manampil pupū hasta paṅduk nikā mwaŋ panĕmpuḥ nikâṅgyat sakeŋ byoma rodrâkaluŋ twas paḍâbāŋ ḍaḍanyâsawit wuṅsilan limpa sāmpun rinantay nikê hasta maṅkin karĕsrĕs mĕlĕs rāḥ nikâwaṙṇna kĕmbaŋ riŋ ākāśa maƀrâsawaŋ meǥa riŋ kālasanđyâmiraḥ,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:2

Aṅamuk ika waneḥ paṅan waṅkay iŋ wīra mattâṅinum rāḥ warĕg kādƀutâƀerawâkrak gumantyâwĕrö yan pamuṅgĕl gulū niŋ lawan doyan aṅlaṅga rāḥ niŋ trinādîŋ huwus mātya yâtyanta ǥorâpan akweḥ dudū taŋ haneŋ ƀūmi ƀūtâṅgakārânĕpaḥ maṅsa maṅsö masĕṅhit sumambut musuḥnyêkapi ndān tujaḥ deñcacaḥ cūṙṇna saŋsāra denya n kĕna ndan pirul dan kumis len ikaŋ dꜽtya mohâṅamūk dan dinūk dan gutuk riŋ watu ndan pupuḥ den wunuḥ len tinalyan rinantaynya pan den dudut denya kady-âmatĕk den wawêŋ ambarâgantuṅan denya tan māti kapwânaṅis,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:3
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×51 = 159

yadukulabala tañ jriḥ alwaŋ malĕs maṅlwaṅîŋ rākṣasâneka tekaŋ pĕjaḥ len ikaŋ ndan gutuk riŋ cĕṅĕl mwaŋ pupū ndan tĕṅaḥ riŋ lĕṅĕn kaṙwwa ḍaṇḍa n ḍumaṇḍa ŋ watĕk dānawânidra māmraŋ maṅontā n kinontā siliḥ-duk siliḥ-sob siliḥ-cĕṅkaḥ akral tanorâharĕp munduṙ alwat paḍâlwat hanâm-waḥ tikā tan patĕṇḍas kawanđanya kapwâtaruŋ leñ cĕṅĕlnyâsahut riŋ lĕmaḥ rodra lambe nikâbāŋ mibĕk rāḥ piraŋ lakṣa taŋ wīra maṅkâdƀutâwak mahāƀūta rūpanya sākṣāt prawīrôttamâtyanta rodrâdƀutâṅiṇḍarat,

{daṇḍaka}:95.3:3
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [– ⏑ –]×58 = 180

śawa makatĕlĕbuk tibā paṅharĕp niŋ watĕk dꜽtya maṅsö ri saŋ wrĕṣṇiyođā tatan dwa ŋ raŧa syuḥ rĕmĕk de ni tĕmpuḥ ni waṅkay nikaŋ sāmajâpan sawaŋ waṙṣa śꜽlânanâdrĕs tibā riŋ watĕk yādawâwrĕg sĕḍĕŋ duṙbalâkweḥ pĕjaḥ de ni kontā n linesan ḍawuḥnyâwuwuḥ śūla dukduk lawan samby-aṅembuḥ manaḥnya ŋ watĕk rākṣasêŋ ƀūtalâmūk-winūk mamraŋ aṅrok-rinok rodra tekaŋ mulûsusnya denyâṅdudut yeka baṇḍut nikeŋ rowaŋ adwandwayudđâmurĕk yan kabaṇḍut siliḥ-kris siliḥ-māti kâṙwwêŋ raṇāŋ-gêka moǥa n sinuṅsuŋ niŋ apsary-arūm tuṅgalan ndan rĕbut śīǥra māmprĕp muwaḥ*

<śāṙddūlawikrīdita>:96.
– – –|⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ = 19

kālanya n marurĕk tikaŋ praŋ asuwe malwaŋ lĕwiḥ sāyuta,
yekā n konduṙ ikaŋ watĕk yadubalâkweḥ māti de niŋ panaḥ,
saŋsārā marikā n sinambut ikanaŋ dꜽtyâtĕhĕṙ maṅlayaŋ,
rĕmpū syuḥ tinibākĕn iŋ watu rĕmök mwaŋ tĕṇḍas iŋ tuṅgaṅan*

mwaŋ tekaŋ magajaḥ sinambut apuyĕŋ lāwan gajaḥnyênuyĕŋ,
ṅkānê rowaŋ ikā n winantiṅakĕn iŋ dꜽtya n pagantyâṅalap,
mātī wwaŋ tikanaŋ pamantiŋ an arok taṇḍasnya sāmpun rĕmök,
rĕñcĕm tekaŋ anuṅgaŋ osyan inadunyê rĕṅga niŋ sāmaja*

sakweḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya rodra maṅalap dantînadunyêŋ laṅit,
saṅkĕp ƀāwa nikâkaruŋ-karuṅan anyat taŋ  maṅadwâ walaŋ,
lāwan taŋ kadi minda de nika maṅadw-î tampuḥ iŋ sāmaja,
māti mwaŋ gaja paṅgutuk nika ri saŋ yadw-ârĕmuk siŋ kĕna*

Akweḥ saŋ yadu māti denya katibān lāwan raŧa syuḥ rĕmök,
maṅkin māwrĕg i wuntat awri malayū yan ton sahab niŋ musuḥ,
rĕmpak byūha nirêkanaŋ makarawaktrâpan supitnyâradin,
ratw-âbāp mati tan pasāra kawĕnaŋ de niŋ watĕk dānawa*

saŋ rukmâṙjjuna sāmba satyaka suđīrâṅheṙ đanuḥ ywênayat,
śīǥra hrū nira yaṙ lĕpas paḍa parĕŋ moliḥ musuḥ rākṣasa,
Alwaŋ sewu nĕmaŋ puluḥ pisan ikaŋ dꜽtyâṅlayaŋ riŋ laṅit,
wāhw-âraŋ ri gĕlis niraŋ pat amanaḥ teja hyaŋ aṙkkânĕlat*

maṅkin tâlwaŋ anekadānawa pĕjaḥ mwaŋ wāhananya n tibā,
rowaŋnya n katibān rihĕk hana tikĕl jeṅkel dudū taŋ pĕñĕt,
towin satyaka sāmba maṅlawan ikaŋ dꜽtyâhawan riŋ lĕmaḥ,
hetunyâlwaŋ aneka lakṣa niyuta pwa ŋ dꜽtya len rākṣasa*

maṇḍĕg taŋ yaduyođa māri malayū malwī waneḥ riŋ raṇa,
yekâṅsö nika saŋ mahodara manuṅgaŋ riŋ liman syandana,
saŋ rukmā dinunuŋnya śīǥra kumucup tan paṅgalĕŋ sāhasa,
krūranya n pamutĕṙ gadā nika satal göŋnyâṅĕpöṙ yan katon*

tandaŋnya n pamupuḥ raŧa nrĕpati rukma syuḥ tĕkêŋ sāraŧi,
saŋ rukma n tumuluy lumumpat aṅunus patrĕm si tīkṣṇapraƀā,
Aṅsö niŋ liman iŋ mahodara kasep kapraŋ gaḍiŋnyâpasaḥ,
maṅkin krođa mahodarâmurĕkakĕn hastinya pan den wĕlĕg*

muṅgwī hasti nikâtriśūla maluṅid paṅduknya sāmpun lĕpas,
trus limpad hati saŋ narāđipati rukmā denya tan kāwaran,
mahyā rākṣasa yan paṅadwakĕn awū taŋ dꜽtya saṅkeŋ laṅit,
hetunya n sumahab muwaḥ paḍa masö muṅsī surendrātmaja*

wadwānya ŋ bala rākṣasêka makapaṅhañjuṙ nikâṅĕmbuli,
hamham budđi nikā n tumon kanin iraŋ pāṙŧâtĕṅaḥ tan bisa,
liŋnyâṅhel tuwi yan kanin wuwus ikā sambyâṅasut sāhasa,
kontā tomara sañjatanya lumĕpas bāṇanya tan pāntara*

saŋ pāṙŧa n rinĕbut pĕnuḥ panaḥ irêŋ ākāśa digmaṇḍala,
sakweḥ ny-āyuđa niŋ musuḥ kapalupuy puṅgĕl kawaṅsul waneḥ,
tātan pāntara de nirâṅlĕpasakĕn hrū śakti kapwâṅĕne,
đwasta ŋ rākṣasa siŋ masö kĕna tugĕl tĕṇḍasnya sāmpun tibā*

Anyāt rākṣasa dꜽtya tan pasuku len bāhunya sāmpun hilaŋ,
len taŋ kukṣi nikā pĕgat hana bĕlaḥ twasnyâpasaḥ riŋ ḍaḍa,
sākṣāt waṙṣa taŋ antra limpa ruđiranya ŋ papraṅan kādƀuta,
Awwaḥ mastaka yâgĕlaṙ kunapa niŋ dꜽtyā tibâgĕnturan*

maṅsö saŋ narakê saŋ aṙjjuna manuṅgaŋ riŋ wimānâkilā,
śīǥrâpan prihawak makoliha hurip saŋ pāṙŧa nā liŋ nira,
tandaŋ saŋ nrĕpaputra sāmba mamupuḥ lambuŋ nikaŋ puṣpaka,
pok rĕg ǥoŋ đwani niŋ wimāna pinupuḥ de saŋ narendrātmaja*

rĕg rĕg kāṇḍĕg ikaŋ wimāna makihū lambuŋ nikâpan tikĕl,
tambis kedĕṙ ikāna sinrĕŋ inusiṙ de jambawatyātmaja,
molaḥ saŋ narakê punuknya kaguliŋ kāntĕp tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,
śīǥrâwuṅw-aṅalap gadā nira satal rodrâṅalimpuŋ katon*

tandaŋ saŋ kṣitijê narendratanaya krođâṅuhuḥ kātara,
Ꜽ koŋ nīca lihat wĕkasmu n ahurip yekîŋ gadā yatna ko,
nāhan liŋ nira tan dwa yaṙ pupuhakĕn tekaŋ gadā ƀīṣaṇa,
yekā n māti lawan si dāruki parĕŋ saŋ sāmba riŋ sakṣaṇa*

sāmpun māti narendraputra tumuluy saŋ pāṙŧa maṅsö sira,
krođê saŋ narakâṅayat laras ikaŋ gāṇḍewa pūṙwwâwĕlū,
hrū śakty-âkas agöŋ mayomaya lĕpas de saŋ surendrātmaja,
tampuḥnya n paṅĕne wimāna gumuruḥ sākṣāt garantaŋ humuŋ*

rĕmpak rĕṅga nikaŋ wimāna pinanaḥ kārun tikĕl mwaŋ đwaja,
sāmpun śīṙṇna pĕgat maṇiknya katibā maṅlaḥ rikaŋ ƀūtala,
maṅkin krođa mahīsutâdrĕs umasö muṅsî surendrātmaja,
puṅgĕl taŋ kapiketu kādrĕsan aṅin de niŋ wimāna n tĕḍun*

lāwan bahni mijil saṅke taṅan iraŋ ƀomâtirodra n kutug,
lwiṙ đūma n sumarambaḥ iŋ raṇatalâtyantêŋ karĕsrĕs katon,
sākṣātnya n waḍawānalâṅalad-alad hagyâmaṅan ywêŋ lĕmaḥ,
maṅkin wrĕdđa tĕkâṅgĕsöŋ raŧa niraŋ pāṇḍwātmajê sakṣaṇa*

saŋ pāṙŧêka tatan wikāra maṅayat gāṇḍewa đīrâṅadĕg,
ṅkā n brahmāstraśarāgni de nira lĕpas tīkṣṇâgra riŋ ƀīṣaṇa,
himpĕṙ sūṙyya ri kāla niŋ pralaya tejanyâpanas kātara,
śabdanyêŋ gaganāntarāla kumupak sākṣāt gĕlap sāyuta*

tampuḥnyêŋ ḍaḍa saŋ mahīja kumĕtug limpad tanĕmnyâdalĕm,
mūṙcꞓā saŋ narakâsakit sira tibâlĕṇḍö rikaŋ puṣpaka,
ndātan māti sira n hana ŋ wijayamālāpuṣpa saṅkeŋ ibu,
nāhan hetu nirâṅliliṙ dawut ikaŋ hrū śakty-ataṅgal muwaḥ*

tapwan māri hilī nikaŋ ruđira maṅsö dꜽtya mahyuñ jaya,
yekā n sambut ikaŋ lipuŋ makaṅaran sy-âmoǥa tīkṣṇôjwala,
tejanya n pinutĕṙ pĕnuḥ kilat ikā jyotṣṇâduluṙ waṅkawa,
bāyw-âdrĕs kumusuḥ lawañ jalada kedĕṙ ǥūṙṇnitâgĕnturan*

sampunya n lumĕpas ndatan dwa maṅĕne trus twas niraŋ ꝑalguṇa,
mahyā taŋ bala dꜽtya dānawa humuŋ mwaŋ rākṣasâṅadwakĕn,
saŋ ƀomāsura mantuk iŋ kuwu muwaḥ mwaŋ ƀrĕtyaśeṣâṅiriŋ,
byātītan tinuluŋ kaśakti nira hetunya n hilaŋ taŋ lara*

<wikrĕti>:97.

kunaŋ saŋ amarendraputra lumaḥ iŋ raṇa kasihan irâgilaŋ-gilaŋ,
hibĕk ruđira taŋ ḍaḍa drawa tĕkeŋ muꝁa makuṭa kabeḥ kasĕmburan,
lawan paṭa nirâmiraḥ kadi rinaṇḍi rumakĕt iy awak nirômĕlĕs,
tĕkeŋ kawaca hīrabajra kadi tâtĕmaha pawal apan katon abāŋ*

lĕyĕp ni mata saŋ đanañjaya sawaŋ rawi katawĕṅan iŋ lamad-lamad,
Ikaŋ gĕluŋ asāk mĕlĕs karuđiran kadi jalada rinĕṅga riŋ kilat,
halĕp ni muꝁa nispraƀâsĕmu kucĕm kadi ta laṅit i kāla niŋ damar,
Aśeṣa manis iŋ matâsĕmu guladrawa raḥ ira ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ halis*

<mālāwādi>:98.

I pĕjaḥ saŋ aṙjjuna humuŋ tikaŋ ƀuwana ǥūṙṇnita ŋ jalađi mombakan mawalikan,
kumĕtug tikaŋ widik awaṅkawâsaliwĕran taṭitnya tan arĕn gĕlap masahuran,
gumiwaŋ mahītala śilâdri kampita rubuḥ pucaknya humabĕt rĕbaḥ tahĕn ikā,
hyaŋ anantaƀoga calitāgra hogaḥ asuwe đumāraṇa ri polaḥ i kṣititala*

kapĕgan katonan ikanaŋ jagattri pĕpĕk iŋ lĕbū tĕka lawan hudan hawu mĕlĕk,
tuwi tan pateja ri surup ƀaṭāra rawi diṅmuꝁâmrĕm akucĕm wirūpa mawĕnĕs,
panaṅis nikaŋ gĕrĕḥ asaṅǥanî jalađi tan papāntara humuŋ swaranya gumuruḥ,
kĕtĕṙ iŋ patĕṙ tan arĕn iŋ digantara karĕṅw-awaṙṇna sĕsĕgĕn lanâṅisĕk-isĕk*

<waṅśasŧa>:99.

Atītanĕn saŋ nrĕpaputra ꝑalguṇa,
kunaŋ watĕk yādawaśeṣa duṙbala,
paḍâlarâśā kawĕkas wimūṙcꞓita,
pĕtĕŋ nikaŋ twas kadi riŋ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi*

wirāṭarāja drupadâtiduhꝁita,
ra somadatta prihatin sirâputĕk,
ri taṇ ḍatĕŋ ƀūpati keśawêŋ raṇa,
na hetu niŋ motus amĕṅyakĕn laku*

kunaŋ ta saŋ śrī harimūṙttiƀūpati,
tĕlas mamūjê labuhan mahāyati,
Umaṅkat āgyā ḍatĕṅâhawan kulĕm,
haneŋ hawan mwaŋ sira saŋ halāyuđa*

tatas tikaŋ rātri mawā ta sakṣaṇa,
ḍatĕŋ ta konkonan iraŋ watĕk ratu,
wawaŋ manĕmbaḥ ri siraŋ halāyuđa,
lawan ri saŋ śrī harimūṙttiƀūpati*

paḍâwaraḥ ywê gati saŋ đanañjaya,
ya hetu saŋ śrī nrĕpa keśawâlaris,
tan antyakĕn sampuna niŋ waraḥ sira,
tuhun drĕs iŋ lampaḥ irâhawan raŧa*

samaṅkanêkaŋ bala dꜽtya rākṣasa,
wawaŋ sumuṅsuŋ lumagê nareśwara,
pĕnuḥ ta dꜽtyêŋ gaganāntarâtĕtĕl,
tĕkeŋ lĕmaḥ sök hibĕkan balâsura*

larap nikaŋ kañcana ratna ƀūṣana,
lawan kĕñaṙ niŋ kawacâyuđâkilat,
liman lawan syandana wāji wāhana,
Amānuṣâtyanta halĕpnya ƀāswara*

katon sakeŋ doḥ pwa ya de nareśwara,
rĕpatnya tindaknya maṅuṇḍa sañjata,
sihuŋ nikâkās maluṅid paḍâsalit,
matanya malwâdƀuta kātarôjwala*

masö ta saŋ śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa sāhasa,
lawan sira śrī baladewa sāyuđa,
Ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya haneŋ naƀastala,
cinakra niśśeṣa tĕkap janāṙddana*

śawanya himpĕṙ hudan adrĕs adƀuta,
haṅinya tan pāntara wagyut ujwala,
gĕlap ni śabdanya humuŋ tĕkeŋ lĕmaḥ,
gajāśwa tulya wwaḥ ikâsusun tibā*

Ikaŋ watĕk dꜽtya haneŋ mahītala,
ya tênasö ƀrĕtya narendra keśawa,
raŧanya makweḥ saha pādarakṣaka,
rinoknya wadwā baladewa riŋ gajaḥ*

nanā ta wadwā baladewa kāmbulan,
rikā n tumandaŋ tumuluy halāyuđa,
saha krĕp iŋ sāmaja wrĕdđawāhana,
tĕkâmupuḥ riŋ muśalāstra sāhasa*

Aneka ta lwaŋ nikanaŋ balâsura,
dudū tikaŋ māti cinakra tan pira,
śawanya tulyâṅkura sāk amaṙwwata,
hilī ni rāḥnyâdrĕs awaṙṇna wāḥ gunuŋ*

rikā n masö saŋ mapatiḥ mahodara,
manuṅgaŋ iŋ syandana sāmajâgalak,
sahab ni wadwānya paḍâgajaḥ kabeḥ,
Asĕṅhit aṅduk mamanaḥ maṅĕmbuli*

pĕtĕŋ pĕpĕt ƀrĕtya nikaŋ mahodara,
riwut katonanya sahâđwajâhirĕŋ,
sawaŋ rawi śrī baladewa kāmbulan,
mahāpraƀāwa n pamupuḥ balâsura*

marĕn kuniŋ waṙṇna niraŋ halāyuđa,
tĕkap ni rāḥ niŋ ripu māti de nira,
tĕkeŋ halu mwaŋ wuluku pwa yâmiraḥ,
lawan raŧâwaṙṇna hañaṙ cināraṇa*

parĕŋ pamūk niŋ balawīra sök sĕsök,
paḍâhawan wāhana sāha sāmaja,
Alaḥ tikaŋ rākṣasa pādarakṣaka,
rinok minohan linawan siliḥ-sĕsĕb*

mahodarâsĕṅhit i saŋ halāyuđa,
tumandaŋ amraŋ baḍamanya pāt ḍĕpa,
tinaṅkis iŋ laṅgala de halāyuđa,
sinep dinuk riŋ halu ǥora yan tibā*

tĕlas pĕjaḥ saŋ mapatiḥ mahodara,
masö tikaŋ dꜽtya muwaḥ maṅĕmbuli,
narendra krĕṣṇêka winūknya sāhasa,
pĕnuḥ tikaŋ ƀūmi tĕkeŋ naƀastala*

praƀāswarâtyanta halĕpnya riŋ laṅit,
dukūla wastranya waneḥ praƀâsinaŋ,
maṇik nikâƀrā kawacanya kañcana,
kadi pwa wintaŋ yan i kāla niŋ tilĕm*

lĕpas ni kontānya panaḥnya tan pĕgat,
Aneka denyâṅhudanî warāyuđa,
hanan harĕp mamraŋ amoǥa yan katon,
wulatnya meṅas tumuluy maliṇḍuṅan*

masö ta saŋ śrī nrĕpa keśawêŋ musuḥ,
mañakra tan pāntara riŋ balâsura,
Ikaŋ watĕk rākṣasa dꜽtya dānawa,
kadi pwa yênuṇḍuḥ abāp tibêŋ lĕmaḥ*

hanan tugĕl tūṙnya wĕtĕŋnya len gulū,
ri bāhu sĕmpal sasisiḥ lawañ cĕṅĕl,
hanan śiwak paṙwwa parĕŋ tibâpisan,
waneḥ sawaŋ rumbaḥ abāŋ kasamburat*

huwus hilaŋ taŋ bala dꜽtya riŋ laṅit,
tuluy lumampaḥ naranāŧa keśawa,
lawan tika śrī baladewa hop glisan,
tĕkap nirâgyā mulatê saŋ aṙjjuna*

<Upendrabajra>:100.
⏑ – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏓ = 11

katon taŋ utpāta riwut praduṙgga,
kĕtug nikaŋ loṙ kidul iŋ digānta,
samaṅkana ŋ dāruki yan paśabda,
ri pāduka śrī nrĕpa padmanāƀa*

narāṙyya santabya patik narendra,
mucap mahotpāta ḍatĕŋ rikeŋ rāt,
ndatan sakeŋ ƀīta kĕta ŋ maśabda,
ri pamriha śrī naranāŧa donya*

kunĕŋ patik śrī naranāŧa hopĕn,
mucap kaśaktin prĕŧiwīsutêŋ rāt,
Ikaŋ wimānâtiśayêŋ praƀāwa,
nimitta saŋ ƀoma jayêŋ triloka*

wwayêkahĕn śꜽla maṇik nirâgöŋ,
makambaṅan riŋ gaganāntarāla,
hĕlaṙ nikā n tulya sayojanâlwā,
ya tôṅgwan iŋ strī tawan aprameya*

kunaŋ pratijñā nira saŋ mahīja,
tatan pamuktya ŋ wararājakanyā,
ya tan huwus rakwa jayêŋ narendra,
kađīran iŋ ƀoma duwĕg wiwākṣan*

hanêka kĕmbaŋ wijayêka rakwa,
paweḥ ƀaṭārī prĕŧiwî mahīja,
yadin paratrā kṣitijê raṇāṅga,
ya tan hilaŋ kĕmbaŋ ikâhurip ya*

ya têkahĕn keṅĕta saŋ narendra,
wiwākṣitan dāya niŋ aṅlagāna,
nahan liŋ iŋ dāruki saprayatna,
Umođa saŋ śrī nrĕpa padmanāƀa*

ḍatĕŋ ta saŋ nāŧa rikaŋ pakuwwan,
rikā n kapaṅguḥ yadu-wrĕṣṇi māti,
kunaŋ pwa saŋ satyaka duhꝁa moruk,
marĕk ri saŋ ƀūpati śīǥra mojar*

sirâwaraḥ ry-uṅgwan iraŋ kirīṭi,
wawaŋ matanduk tumuluy narendra,
katon ta saŋ pāṙŧa rujit kĕnêŋ hrū,
lawan tikaŋ twas tarawaŋ kĕnêŋ duk*

samaṅkana śrī nrĕpa padmanāƀa,
mĕkul ri saŋ pāṙŧa nĕhĕṙ masambat,
hariṅku tiṅhal ri si krĕṣṇa pāpa,
tatan wĕnaŋ rakṣaka niŋ swawaṙgga*

nihan kitântĕn pĕjaḥ iŋ raṇāṅga,
ṅhulun Ikā hetu niki n tatan len,
Asiḥta ri ṅwaŋ karaṇanta māmriḥ,
lukan pwa yan māti lĕwĕs laraṅku*

<prĕŧwītala>:101.
⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – –| ⏑ ⏓ = 17

nahan wuwus ira n musap muꝁa ni saŋ narendrātmaja,
đanañjaya sirâtahĕn mulati saŋ narendrânaṅis,
ndatan mara hilaŋ tĕmĕn kĕtĕ-kĕtĕg nirê sakṣaṇa,
parĕŋ mwaŋ i hilaŋ ni citta naranāŧa krĕṣṇâlara*

sĕḍĕŋ nrĕpati krĕṣṇa mūṙcꞓita ḍatĕŋ siraŋ durwaśa,
wawaŋ praṇata saŋ narāṙyya maṅusap ri jöŋ saŋ yati,
samaṅkana mahāṙṣi yan paṅupasāntwa saŋ ƀūpati,
wuwus nira krĕtāṙŧađaṙmma pitutuṙ waraḥ siḥ tĕmĕn*

narendra diwasa ŋ wimūṙcꞓita puriḥ nikaŋ wwaŋ pĕjaḥ,
wruhanta rikanaŋ carācara ninitya tekā kabeḥ,
ƀaṭāra tumitaḥ ta haywa ta kita pramādêrikā,
Ikaŋ pati wiśeṣamāṙgga marikā n gatinya n hana*

kalīṅan ika haywa saŋ praƀu wimoha de niŋ lara,
tamomaya dahat manaḥ tatan ulaḥ niŋ aṅrakṣa rāt,
rajahsahitasatwabudđi rikanā gĕgön de haji,
ꝑalanya ya wĕnaŋ sumidđakĕna kāṙyya saŋ ƀūpati*

kunaŋ pwa haji don mamî kita nihan hanânugraha,
paweha ri narendra maṅhuripanêrikā saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tuhun sasiki rakwa yôliha nikê saliŋ saŋ praƀu,
si sāmba karikā ya têki basudewa yan ꝑālguṇa*

ndya têku kaharĕpta haywa masuwe waraḥta ṅhulun,
nahan wacana saŋ mahāṙṣi sumahuṙ ta saŋ ƀūpati,
kĕnoḥ wacana saŋ mahāmuni pawehanânugraha,
kunaŋ pwa kadi kepwan i ṅhulun apan paḍâṅde wĕlas*

siḥ i ṅwaŋ akadaŋ ya kölakĕna de ranak saŋ yati,
đanañjaya huwus hanânak ipun uttamâṅgantyani,
narendra basudewa sāmpun atuhâwĕkâkweḥ tĕmĕn,
si sāmba pukulun sade nipun apan punaŋ wwaŋ sanak*

kunaŋ pwa ŋ amaṅun larê hati ranak mahaṙṣy-âwĕlas,
nrĕpa druma pĕjaḥ mamet śaraṇa ri ṅhulun kāsihan,
ya hetu niŋ aminta sanmata mahāṙṣi ri pwaṅkulun,
Anugrahana jīwitâhuripa de mahāpaṇḍita*

<mrĕdukomala>:102.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

nāhan śabda narendra krĕṣṇa sumahuṙ ta saŋ rĕṣiwara,
siṅgiḥ sāđu nareśwarâharĕp i đaṙmma saŋ mamawa rāt,
swasty-astu praƀu saŋ paṅāśrayana niŋ triloka tulusa,
niṙwiǥnâjayaśatru saŋ narapatîrikaŋ paƀaratan*

lāwan pājaran i ṅhulun ri haji haywa wismrĕti kita,
An sākṣāt naranāŧa wiṣṇu sakalātmakâparimita,
śaktintêka sake kasidđyan iy awakta tan hana waneḥ,
māyākāra tikaŋ śarīra paramāṙŧadewata kita*

nistanyan kita mānuṣākrĕti yayañ jayêŋ kṣitisuta,
Āpan siḥ mami hetu saŋ praƀu manĕmwa śakty-atiśaya,
yogâđyātmika sāđananta saha budđi sattwa mahĕniŋ,
Astu śrī naranāŧa sidđi sakala n pamaṅgiha yaśa*

sāmpun saŋ paramaṙṣi mājaṙ i narendra māsiḥ awĕlas,
Antaṙllīna sirêŋ kamantyan aṅadĕg ta saŋ narapati,
muṅgaḥ riŋ raŧa śīǥra maṅkat iniriŋ nikaŋ bala kabeḥ,
mwaŋ saŋ śrī baladewa satyaka tumūt hane wuri nira*

maṅkat saŋ naranāŧa krĕṣṇa rumĕṅö ta saŋ kṣitisuta,
sāmpun muṅgw-irikaŋ wimāna maṇipuṣpakâsiga sira,
maṅkat mwaŋ bala dꜽtya-dānawa sĕsök lakunya mariwĕg,
prāptêŋ papraṅan adƀuta ŋ bala humuŋ maraṅkit alaga*

tandaŋ śrī baladewa sāhasa mupuḥ mahāsurabala,
mwaŋ saŋ satyaka śālya len drupada saŋ wirāṭanrĕpati,
kapwâganti sirâmanaḥ karaṇa niŋ balâsura nanā,
Aṇḍĕḥ niŋ bala dꜽtya-dānawa malĕs ta yâmarawaśa*

henak taŋ praŋ arok siliḥ-sĕsĕb aneka wīra kawĕnaŋ,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda wāhana mwaŋ ika śabda niŋ kakuwuṅan,
yekā n lot karĕṅö lawan patakis iŋ gadâsriŋ apalu,
kontā tomara kakrĕcik saha kĕtug nikaŋ pamugari*

gĕṇḍiŋ goŋ gubaṙ apratiđwani sahasra ƀinna karĕṅö,
kālanya ŋ praŋ arok masö ta si nisunda dꜽtya pinatiḥ,
toḥ jīwâmrihakĕn ri saŋ naraka lāgy-akīṙtti riŋ ayun,
ndā hetunya kinon tĕkap saŋ asureśwarâmriḥ ayaśa*

maṅkat mwaŋ bala wāhananya sakasewu muꝁya winani,
muṅsî saŋ nrĕpa śālya sāhasa masiṅhanāda gumuruḥ,
wadwā saŋ nrĕpa śālya yatna mamanaḥ riŋ astra niśita,
meṅas taŋ paṅarĕp manoliḥ i wuri n panon lawan amūk*

goŋ goŋ goŋ muni goŋ nareśwara kumon swaƀrĕtya malaga,
Aṅkat niŋ gajawrĕnda tuṅgaṅan i wuntat iŋ raŧa tumūt,
kapwâtampuḥ arok tikaŋ bala siliḥ-praŋ osyan asuwe,
tan pāntê waratomarâṙdđa tumitiḥ sawaŋ hudan agöŋ*

sakweḥ niŋ bala saŋ nisunda n umasö mamūk tan atakut,
kontā kadga gadā tuhuk pinakasañjatanya sawaneḥ,
len tekâṅalaŋ iŋ śilā sakuruṅan ta ya n katihalaŋ,
dantī syandana tuṅgaṅan mati tĕkapnya tan hana bisa*

Awrĕg ƀrĕtya narendra madrapati tan pasāra wĕkasan,
nāhan hetu narendra yatna malagâṅayat laras agöŋ,
hrū bajrāśani śuṣka sewu lumĕpas pisan tĕka pira,
śīṙṇna syuḥ bala dꜽtya denya saha wāhananya kawĕnaŋ*

yekā n tandaŋ ikaŋ nisunda mamanaḥ ri saŋ narapati,
hrūnyâneka ya tâṅĕne đwaja narendra puṅgĕl apasaḥ,
lāwan sāraŧi māti denya kadrĕsan panaḥ narapati,
maṅkin sāhasa saŋ nisunda mamĕḍĕk mahâmarĕpĕki*

hetunya n paṅalap ri tomara nikā praƀāswara katon,
prāyanyâṅduk asep lĕṅĕnya pinanaḥ tĕkap narapati,
wāhw-ânambut ikaŋ kiwanya pinanaḥ muwaḥ rinuhunan,
sāmpun tĕṅgĕk ikā n pĕgat hulu nikâṅlayaŋ kadi hĕlaŋ*

Ambĕknyâpulihan ta lāwan ika saŋ narendra wĕkasan,
hetunya n tumĕḍun sakeŋ gagana göŋ swaranya karĕṅö,
wruḥ saŋ nāŧa mahā prayatna maṅalap swaḍaṇḍa tumuluy,
tampuḥnyêŋ śiraḥ iŋ nisunda kumĕpok muꝁanya pinupuḥ*

sāmpun māti nisunda maṅkin abutĕŋ ta saŋ kṣitisuta,
wwantĕn dꜽtya ṅaranya pañcajana śakti lāgi paṅalaḥ,
len saṅke rikanaŋ si pañcajana māti riŋ jalaniđi,
krūrâkral tahu tâṅlawan hyaŋ irikā n kinon apuliha*

muṅgwiŋ sāmaja pat gaḍiŋnya kadi paṙwwatâlaku-laku,
tandaŋnyê baladewa śūla rinĕgĕpnya kātara murub,
lāwan bahni murub sakeŋ mata nikā lanâlatu-latu,
śīṙṇnêkaŋ bala rohiṇīsuta gĕsĕŋ waneḥ kapanasan*

tandaŋ saŋ baladewa laṅgala minuṣṭi de nira masö,
muṅgwî syandana śīǥra yaṙ putĕrakĕn ta sañjata nira,
krūrâkrak maṅuhuḥ si pañcajana heṙ lihat jaga-jaga,
liŋnya n paṅduk aṅadwakĕn mati ya liŋnya yan panudiṅi*

yatna śrī baladewa yaṙ takisakĕn ta laṅgala nira,
puṅgĕl śūla nikā si pañcajana ƀagna kontal atĕhĕr,
nāhan hetu nikaŋ si pañcajana mĕtta maṅduk amuwaḥ,
tan poliḥ tinakis muwaḥ tikĕl apaṙwwa tan pajamuga*

Ambĕk niṙƀaya dꜽtya pañcajana mamrihâmulihana,
kagyat yan ginayuṙ gulūnya kapuliṙ pĕjaḥ kapisanan,
hetunyâwrĕg ikaŋ balâsura sahāya maṅkin alayū,
muṅsiṙ saŋ kṣitijâruhun-ruhunan atri māty-alulunan*

<Aparāntikā>:103.

si hayagrīwa wawaŋ ta yâpuliḥ,
tan aṅiṣṭî paṅutus mahīsuta,
ri harĕpnyâṅrahatāna riŋ tuhan,
karaṇanya n prihawak ta yômasö*

kadunuŋ satyaka de nikômasö,
pinanaḥnyêŋ śara bāṇa sāyaka,
mamalĕs pwā mamanaḥ ta satyaka,
śarasampāta lĕwiḥ panaḥ nira*

hana kedĕṙ kawaluy waneḥ puhĕr,
si hayagrīwa makin magöŋ galak,
Umalap hrūnya sutīkṣṇa śaktiman*

tinujunyêka gulū ni satyaka,
patitisnyâmatitis tĕlas katon,
lumĕpas hrūnya sĕḍĕŋ haneŋ laṅit,

⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏓ = 23

ri pĕjaḥ ikā n hanêky-asuradānawâpuliḥ anuṅgaŋ iŋ raŧa magöŋ,
ṅaran ika tāra lāgi paṅalaḥ watĕk hyaŋ ika ṅūni riŋ daṅu-daṅū,
saha bala yeka tan dwa tumitiḥ lumiṇḍiḥ irikaŋ watĕk yadubala,

narapatiy ugrasena mamanaḥ riŋ agniśara caṇḍabāyusahita,
pinapagakĕn riŋ aṙṇnawarasâtiǥora gumuruḥ tĕkeŋ awaŋ-awaŋ,

salĕkas irêkihĕn wiꝑala hetu saŋ nrĕpati đꜽṙyya đāraka masö*

kunĕŋ irikā n si tāra masiga dyaya n mulati saŋ narendra mabutĕŋ,

mātī tāra sarodra saŋ kṣitisutômasö sira wawaŋ,
śīṙṇnêkaŋ bala paṅharĕp nrĕpati keśawāṅśa pinanaḥ,
śīǥra śrī nrĕpa krĕṣṇa maṅlĕpasakĕn śarottama sira,
đwasta ŋ dānawa-dꜽtya de nira sapaṅharĕp kṣitisuta*

yekā n sāhasa saŋ mahīsuta haneŋ wimāna magĕlis,
cĕt muṅgwiŋ wuri cĕt haneŋ harĕp amet i cidra caliriŋ,
yatna śrī naranāŧa keśawa haneŋ raŧâkuliliṅan,
Ādrĕs tan katĕṅĕṙ lĕkas nira ri mađya niŋ raṇasaƀā*

krođâmbĕk narakâkrak iŋ gagana kātarâṅamaḥ-amaḥ,
nāhan hetu nira n tĕkâṅabĕnakĕn si puṣpaka sira,

śrī krĕṣṇâtiśayêŋ gĕlĕŋ mayatakĕn panaḥ nira muwaḥ,
nyā ŋ nārāyaṇabāṇa mrĕtyurađanêka de nira lĕpas,
wagyūtpāta halisyus adƀuta duluṙnya kātara dahat,
tan wyaṙŧa n paṅĕne laras kṣitija śīṙṇna puṅgĕl i taṅan*

kombul kedĕṙ ikaŋ wimāna kahiriŋ tĕkap niŋ anila,

gĕntĕṙ yan tumibā prakampa gumiwaŋ tikaŋ kṣititala*

Āpan tan tumuluy cinakra sira de narendra sakarĕŋ,
towin kambaŋ irêkanaŋ wijayamālapuṣpa tinahā,
saṅke hyaŋ prĕŧiwī paweḥ nira ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu ri sira*

saṅketanya rikāna de nira tĕlas prakāśa karĕṅö,

<ƀadralalita>:106.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 21

ri sĕḍĕŋ mahīsuta hilaŋ wimāna nira niṙƀayâṅawaŋ-awaŋ,
maṅagĕm sy-amoǥa sira dug pracaṇḍa pinutĕṙ nirâṅarab-arab,
tumĕḍun sakeŋ gagana ǥūṙṇnitâṅamaḥ-amaḥ sirâṅaraḥ-araḥ,
lumĕpas lipuŋ nira sakeŋ taṅan murub awaṙṇna sūṙyya maṅaliḥ*

saha bāyubajra kumutug dudū ṅhaliwawaṙ lĕbū lĕwu pĕtĕŋ,
lĕpas saṅka riŋ kṣitisutâṅasut nrĕpati krĕṣṇa len bala kabeḥ,
naranāŧa krĕṣṇa tumuluy sirâṅlĕpasi cakra tan papĕgatan,
sumĕsĕb sy-amoǥa tugĕl iŋ naƀastala wiśīṙṇna tan patĕmahan*

Ikanaŋ pĕtĕŋ juga ya tan marĕn tumutup iŋ raṇāṅganasaƀā,
yatika ƀramanta paḍa tan katon sahana niŋ prawīra malaga,
ṅhiŋ ikaŋ liman turaga maṅhrik atry-awurahan ya nitya karĕṅö,
kalawan krĕcik ni tĕwĕk iŋ mayođa matakis lawan waja galaḥ*

Awĕlas narendra harimūṙtti kāraṇa nirâsamāđi wĕkasan,
Irikâtriwikrama ƀaṭāra krĕṣṇa sira wiṣṇu rodra sakala,
Aruhuṙ dudug sira tĕkêrikaŋ paramasatyaloka tumuluy,
Ikanaŋ ḍaḍâtiśaya riŋ lwa māṅuhabi loka saŋ hyaŋ i ruhur*

tuwi sewu tĕṇḍas ira kapwa tâtrinayanê satĕṇḍas umurub,
Asalit sihuŋ nira kunaŋ tutuk nira guhā paḍanya n umaṅaŋ,
mwaŋ ikaŋ taṅan pituŋ iwu prakīṙṇna maṅagĕm warāyuđa kabeḥ,
kadi meru kĕmbaṙ ikanaŋ sukū rwa mawĕki ŋ mahītala pĕpĕk*

ḍĕṅĕn iŋ triloka tumatiŋ haneŋ wulu nirâhirĕŋ kadi sĕmut,
hana yan paṅaṙwwani waneḥ dudū taŋ aṅatĕlwani ŋ wulu siki,
saha sañjatanya bahĕluŋ ladiŋ paḍa masumpahan saha wĕḍuŋ,
mawĕḍak-wĕḍak ruđira ƀīṣaṇâsawit usus tĕkeŋ paru-paru*

sumĕnö tikaŋ makuṭa sewu ƀāskara sahasra tulya mapupul,
mwaŋ ikaŋ maṇik rwaŋ iwu kuṇḍalâtiśaya ƀāswaranya n umurub,
dilaḥ iŋ sihuŋ pataŋ iwu mwaŋ astra kadi bahni tīkṣṇa lumarap,
karaṇanya māwa wĕkasan tikaŋ paƀaratan katon taŋ alaga*

bala dꜽtyadānawa pĕjaḥ piraŋ puluḥ atus ya kedĕk apĕñĕt,
saha wāhananya gaja koṭi-koṭi milu māti kedĕkan apil,
Ikanaŋ haneŋ gagana konduṙ āwrĕg alulun katuṇḍuŋ iŋ awak,
muririŋ kagĕm kĕna ḍinĕṇḍa riŋ ḍĕṅĕn awū cinakra ginadā*

ri sĕḍĕŋ ƀaṭāra hari matriwikrama ḍataŋ ta sañjata nira,
maṅaran si nandaka si pañcajanya kalawan gadā sama dulur,
ṅuniweḥ ta saŋ garuḍa śīǥra kapwa sawawê ƀaṭāra yan agöŋ,
paḍa sewu taŋ harĕp akīṙttya maṅrahatanêŋ ƀaṭāra humarĕk*

Umulat pwa saŋ naraka yan triwikrama ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu sakala,
yatikā n saroṣa tumuluy triwikrama muwaḥ sirâruhuṙ agöŋ,
kadi paṙwwatâtumaŋ ikaŋ hawak winilĕt iŋ ǥanâkilat arĕs,
mwaŋ ikaŋ sꝑuliṣṭatikarômijil saka rikaŋ sihuŋ pat aǥaṣa*

tumuluy sirâṅalap ikaŋ gadâwĕsi sayojanôjwala katon,
pamupuḥ nirêŋ sira ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu wiꝑala n kasaṅga ri taṅan,
Amupuḥ muwaḥ tinakis iŋ gadâwĕsi makāđikāra riŋ agöŋ,
tĕka riŋ diganta karĕṅö đwaninya kadi rūga ŋ aṇḍaƀuwana*

kṣitiputra đīra maṅagĕm prĕp adƀuta ri göŋnya paṙwwatasama,
sahasâmrĕp aṅhala-halêrikaŋ ḍaḍa ƀaṭāra tuṅgĕŋ atĕguḥ,
đwani niŋ gĕlap śatasahasrakoṭi pakaśabda niŋ prĕp anitir,
paḍa saṅśaya ṅhyaŋ anahā waliŋnya rubuha ŋ laṅit mawurahan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:107.

gutgūtĕn ta ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu mamalĕs mamrĕp ri saŋ ƀūmija,
göŋ niŋ prĕp nira merutulya maṅĕne tĕṇḍas ni ƀūmyātmaja,
yekā n kontal ikaŋ maṇikmakuṭa saŋ ƀomêrikaŋ sāgara,
tampuḥ niŋ śatakoṭi handaru tibā tulyanya ǥorâkĕtug*

lumpat saŋ garuḍâṅalap wijayamālāpuṣpa saŋ ƀūmija,
wāhw-âṅambil ikā n prayatna narakâmraŋ wꜽnateyêŋ tĕwĕk,
yekâpaṙwwa bĕlaḥ śiwak ḍaḍa ni saŋ pakṣīndra rāḥ lwiṙ hudan,
Eṅgal mampĕt apan sirâmrĕtamayâtyantêŋ kasidđan sira*

sāmpun kālap ikaŋ sĕkaṙ wijayamālā de kagendrâṅlayaŋ,
maṅsö hyaŋ hari śīǥra yan sikĕp ikā saŋ ƀoma siṅhākrĕti,
sātus hasta nirâmrĕp aṅhala-halêŋ taṇḍas niraŋ ƀūmija,
rĕmpū syuḥ mapasewu de nira śiraḥ saŋ dꜽtyarājā n pĕjaḥ*

sāmpun māti mahīja waṅkay ira meḥ-meḥ yan tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,
kontal riŋ wĕkasan tinampik i hĕlaṙ saŋ wꜽnateyâbaṅĕt,
ṅkānê mađya nikaŋ samudra tumibā kagyat hyaŋ iŋ sāgara,
Eṅgal yan tĕka riŋ rasātala ri paṅkwan śrī prĕŧiwy-ânaṅis*

<jagadđita>:108.

byātītan mati saŋ mahīsuta kunaŋ tura-turaḥ ikanaŋ balāsura,
Aṅboṅlot asĕnötan iŋ jalađi nāgata ri sira ƀaṭāra keśawa,
len tekaŋ maṅusiṙ gunuŋ gahana gahwara paraṅan arĕs magantuṅan,
saŋsāra ŋ kanin aṅlaḥ amriḥ atĕkĕn kawĕlas-arĕp aṅaṅsaṙ iŋ juraŋ*

maṅkat śrī baladewa maṅraraḥ anūt ṅ-asura kuwu-kuwunya sāk punaḥ,
ṅkā yan paṅgiḥ ikaŋ gunuŋ maṇik akambaṅan atiśaya kādƀutâhĕlar,
Akweḥ wrĕkṣa-latanya ratnamaya jaṅga nika kanaka mĕmbaŋ iŋ liraŋ,
mwaŋ groŋ-groŋ ni juraŋ-juraŋnya humiriŋ watu karaŋ i hiriŋnya komala*

strīratnâṙjja hanêrikaŋ maṇimayâsĕmu maṇik inurā kasamburat,
raśminya n paṅurꜽ gĕluŋnya kadi nīlajalada mata komalâmanis,
sĕṅsöŋ niŋ miraḥ iŋ laṭī kakĕñaran dinakara maṇiƀāswarâhulap,
rūpanyâniru hintĕn esi dinĕlö raras i hajĕŋ ikā n pacendrika*

wwantĕn tâlihaṅan karaŋ pracala piṇḍa tulis inapi dèwa niŋ pĕṭa,
waṙṇnanyâkuniŋ anwam iŋ pamulu wimba ni sĕkaṙ iŋ aśoka cāmpaka,
himpĕṙ pādapa reꝁa-reꝁa ni tĕṅaḥnya winuri-wuri niŋ tapiḥ suji,
lindinya n tinĕtĕs hajöŋnya ri matā winulatakĕn i raśmi niŋ sipat*

paṇḍan lĕŋlĕŋ i duṅhus iŋ watu karaŋ sꝑaṭika kinasut iŋ himânipis,
jaṅganyâsĕkaṙ aṅjraḥ aṅjamanikânisiḥ akataraḥ aṙjja kāṅinan,
ṅkā wwantĕn wanitâmaṅun lĕṅĕŋ amaṅku wĕtis aṅĕliḥ aṅligā tĕṅaḥ,
waṙṇna hyaŋ-hyaṅan iŋ ṭikā kajĕnĕkan lĕyĕp alĕbu-lĕbū hrĕbuk miṅiŋ*

kālap taŋ giriratna de halađarâkĕmitan awĕdi riŋ jaruḥ-jaruḥ,
mwaŋ taŋ komala hagraśeṣa nira saŋ kṣititanaya madum-dum iŋ bala,
Eṅgal prāpta huwus haneŋ kuwu muwaḥ nda tucapa ta ƀaṭāra keśawa,
māhêŋ göŋ kadi wuntwa taŋ ƀuwana de nira rawi sumurup sake taṅan*

hyaŋ brahmā sira śīǥra yaṇ ḍatĕŋ anĕmbaḥ ararĕm i ƀaṭāra keśawa,
ƀakty-âṅastuti liŋ nira n praƀu wiśeṣa kita waśawasitwa ƀūpati,
Utpatti-sŧiti-līṇa niŋ ƀuwana kāraṇa nika kita n ādidewatā,
ƀoktêŋ ƀogya kitâtmaśudđa puruṣottama kita paramāṙŧa kewala*

yan riŋ sanđi katatwan iŋ praṇawadewa kita makaśarīra ŋ akṣara,
lit niŋ sūtra subadđabanđana binanđa kita paramatatwa duṙlaƀa,
yan riŋ jyotiṣatantra tan hana waneḥ kita sipat i katĕmwan iŋ pinet,
saŋ kṣepanya wiśeṣa riŋ tiga ƀaṭāra paramaśiwa n iṣṭidewatā*

nyā ŋ lokâhyun i tatwa ni hyaŋ iŋ apa n wruha ri gati ƀaṭāra yan wiƀuḥ,
prajñā yan pamasaŋ samāhita taŧāpi wiṣaya nika tan tĕke kita,
saŋ yogīśwara towi tan wĕnaŋ ataṙkka ri kita humĕnĕŋ kuraŋ hiḍĕp,
pūjā đyāna samāđi đaṙmma pitutuṙ panalimuṙ ira riŋ kapaṇḍitan*

sāmpun maṅkana liŋ prajāpati maṅastuti tĕka sira dewatā kabeḥ,
ƀakty-âhyun mulatê ƀaṭāra mađusūdana paḍa mararĕm krĕtāñjali,
saŋ hyaŋ śakra haneŋ gajendra saha ƀūṣaṇa nira kumĕñaṙ mawaṅkawa,
himpĕṙnya ŋ kanakâkilat kasuluhan dinakara makin ujwalapraƀa*

<sragđarā>:109.

prāpta hyaŋ dwādaśāditya saha raŧa sira ndātan atyanta tīkṣṇa,
sākṣāt wālāṙkka ramyâmuhara suꝁa sirê saŋ watĕk hyaŋ sumaṇḍiŋ,
lāwan saŋ hyaŋ đanendrâhalĕp acĕpuk agöŋ somya muṅgwiŋ palaṅka,
Aƀrâwaṙṇnâṇḍĕp-ĕṇḍĕp kilat ahulap ikaŋ ƀūṣaṇâkweḥ maṇiknya*

ƀaṭāra parameśwarâđipati saŋ watĕk dewatā,
ḍatĕŋ sira lawan gaṇañjaya kumāra tan saḥ tumūt,
maśānti ri ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu sira tuṣṭa haṙṣâgiraŋ,
wuwus nira manoharâjaya-jayâṅgĕlaṙ śāntika*

huwus paḍa ḍatĕŋ pwa saŋ hyaŋ atatâsraṅâṅastuti,
watĕk rĕṣi humūŋ maweda kadi śabda niŋ nīrada,
samaṅkana ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu suꝁa de watĕk dewatā,
nimitta nira yan panāntwa ri ƀaṭāra đātā sira*

nahan liŋ ira he wiriñci kita māsihêŋ rāt kabeḥ,
watĕk hyaŋ ika rakṣanĕnta ṅuniweḥ tikā saŋ rĕṣi,
Apan kita bapêbu niŋ sakalaloka kaṙttā kita,
mataŋnya hayu niŋ jagat juga yatanya tan liṅgara*

tĕlas mara hilaŋ si ƀoma ya kalĕṅka niŋ rāt kabeḥ,
tĕwĕk nika kahaywan iŋ ƀuwana deṅku tan popama,
kitêkana nimitta niŋ tĕhĕra taŋ jagat śāśwata,
marapwan iki tuṣṭa saŋ rĕṣi lawan watĕk dewatā*

sadrĕwya nikanaŋ watĕk hyaŋ inalap nikaŋ ƀūmija,
yateka mulihêka deṅku manĕhĕṙ tikâtūt krama,
kitā tikanaŋ eṅĕtê krama nikā kitâniṅkaha,
Apan mapipika swaƀāwa nikaŋ ahyun iŋ drĕwya len*

nahan ta wuwus i ṅhulun ri sira saŋ watĕk hyaŋ kabeḥ,
kitâtika nimitta niŋ sakalawaṙṇna tan saṅkara,
tĕhĕṙ kita matūta nitya gawayĕn tikāŋ aṙccaṇa,
marapwan ika tuṣṭa taŋ ƀuwanaloka ƀaktî kita*

wuwusku hiḍĕpĕn ta haywa ta kita pramādêŋ hayu,
yatanya kita pagwanâpagĕha riŋ kadewabratan,
tumĕmwa ꝑala niŋ kasidđyan atĕhĕṙ musuḥ tan hana,
ṅhulun muwaḥ ajanma mānuṣa rikaŋ jagat rakṣakā*

tiḍak ḍikĕtahui
<śloka>:111.

na liŋ ƀaṭāra hyaŋ wiṣṇu,
ri sakweḥ para dewatā,
saŋ watĕk hyaŋ kabeḥ tuṣṭa,
maśānti mwaŋ maṅastuti*

ri tĕlas watĕk dewatā,
mantuk riŋ swaṙgga lālana,
rĕp hyaŋ wiṣṇu muwaḥ krĕṣṇa,
somyâpañ citta niṙmmala*

saŋ hyaŋ śakra wawaŋ malwī,
mare śrī krĕṣṇa haṙṣaja,
muṅgwiŋ wāhana mātaṅga,
Iniriŋ niŋ warāpsara*

wawaŋ mojaṙ sirânāntwa,
he saŋ nāŧa lihat praƀu,
ƀārā don mami yan prāpta,
mawehânugrahê kita*

nān liŋ saŋ hyaŋ śakra mojar,
narendrâtyantêŋ gaṙjjita,
dewanāŧa mahādibya,
sanmatâsiha ri ṅhulun*

nihan tânugraha saŋ hyaŋ,
ri ṅhulun tulusâsiha,
saŋ watĕk ratu saŋ hantu,
kapwa wehĕnta jīwita*

narendra druma kasyasiḥ,
pĕjaḥ mwaŋ putra riŋ raṇa,
Amet śaraṇa tan poliḥ,
yâṅde māṙ i twas i ṅhulun*

yadu-wrĕsṇy-anđakâdinya,
lāwan saŋ pininaŋ māti,
sāmānta pratisāmānta,
huripĕn de sureśwara*

ƀrĕtya putra kadaŋ waṙgga,
saŋ watĕk ratu kāsihan,
pĕjaḥ tan tĕkan iŋ mrĕtyu,
yatikā huripĕn muwaḥ*

cedi kaṙṇna jarāsanđa,
byaktêki n musuḥ i ṅhulun,
taŧāpi huripĕn saŋ hyaŋ,
towin kadaŋ ikā tĕhĕr*

paritrāṇâkrĕtađaṙmma,
winiśeṣa ri saŋ praƀu,
śatru towin paritrāṇan,
marapwan mari duṙjana*

ya tā liŋ śrī mahārāja,
sumahuṙ hyaŋ surapati,
praƀu toḥ haywa sandeha,
Astu kahyunta dadyā ya*

sāmpun mojaṙ ƀaṭārendra,
rĕp đyāyī sira niścala,
tĕkâŋ amrĕta riŋ kuṇḍi,
paniram nira riŋ pĕjaḥ*

tan asowe dahat saŋ hyaŋ,
mahurip saŋ watĕk ratu,
tĕka riŋ śatru siŋ yogya,
labđajīwa tĕkeŋ bala*

<jagadđita>:112.

waṙṇnan tôlaḥ i saŋ watĕk ratu samâhurip agarawalan sirâwuṅū,

kāścaṙyyan mulati ŋ pĕjaḥ ruđirasāgara giri śawa niŋ gajaḥ kuda,

ri tĕlas watĕk ratu paḍâhurip suꝁa narendra krĕṣṇa magiraŋ,

surarāja mamwit anĕhĕṙ muliḥ sira n umūṙ tĕkeŋ surapada,
Awiwākṣitan sira kunaŋ pwa saŋ ratu kabeḥ sirêki caritan,

ndaḥ waṙṇnan gati niŋ balâlara ri mitra nika pĕjaḥ anūtakĕn tuhan,

strī belā kapapag maṅiṣṭy-akalihan sinuṇḍaŋ awĕnĕs,

Aparimitêŋ suꝁâsama-samêŋ watĕk yadu kabeḥ,
maṅinum agoṣṫy-amukti ꝑala niŋ jayêŋ raṇasaƀā,

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:118.

saŋ nāŧātmaja sāmba sāmpun arĕṇaḥ tekaŋ dĕmak de haji,
An prāgjyotiṣa rakwa punpunan ira ndātan hanânĕmpila,
mās rwaŋ lakṣa kaṭi n kapaṅguhan irâṅkĕn māsa lek nohanĕn,
hīṅanya n kalĕwiḥ ꝑala śrama nirâsārêŋ raṇâtoḥ ƀaya*

saŋ nāŧa druma mantuk iŋ swanagarêmbuḥ wanwa riŋ yāwana,
bĕṅkat-bĕṅkat irâhawan raŧa mure rambut nirêkâputiḥ,
yapwan putra nirêka saŋ suraŧa kāly-âpan wineḥ putrikā,
de śrī krĕṣṇa tĕlas paḍâsiliḥ-asiḥ rāgapriyâṅgöŋ smara*

ry-antuk saŋ garuḍâduluṙ sira lawan saŋ pañcajanyâṅlayaŋ,
mwaŋ saŋ komudikī sudaṙśśaṇa parĕŋ mwaŋ nandakânraŋ kilat,
prāptêŋ wiṣṇupada ndatīta ta kabeḥ saŋ nāŧa krĕṣṇâjarĕn,
sākṣāt wīṙyya nira n prakāśa karĕṅö riŋ dik-widik niścala*

nāhan hetu niŋ aśwameđa ginawe riŋ dwārawaty-âđika,
de saŋ śrī basudewa kaprakaśitêŋ rāt mwaŋ watĕk dewatā,
söḥ taŋ ratna suwaṙṇna ratnawanitā n paṅgorawêŋ brāhmaṇa,
maṅdadyākĕna haywan iŋ ƀuwana sākṣāt rîndralokânurun*

strī kanyâhayu ratnarājaduhitânwam pat hajöṅyânulus,
Antuk niŋ mamarājaya nrĕpati krĕṣṇâmukti tātan waneḥ,
ramyâwaṙṇna tinuṅgal iŋ jinĕm arūm haṙṣa n saraśmîŋ tilĕm,
Āpan de ni kawiṣṇumūṙttin ira saŋ nāŧa n wĕnaŋ wyāpaka*

ndan saŋ śrī warawīṙyya rukma krĕtađaṙmmādi pralabđêŋ suꝁa,
kapwâmukti sakāpti niŋ manaḥ anūt đaṙmmâpagĕḥ riŋ hayu,
swasŧā niŋ bala rāmya tan hana sasaṙ saṅkêrikaŋ śāsana,
Āstām saŋ caturāśramâtata manūt śāstrâhawan riŋ pada*
